File: /.scratch/trace/assign.mjs

// Assigns segmented components to territories, traces outlines, computes
// pole-of-inaccessibility anchors. Writes shapes.json + review render.
import { readFileSync, writeFileSync } from "node:fs";
import { PNG } from "../../web/node_modules/pngjs/lib/png.js";

const { W, H, kept } = JSON.parse(readFileSync(".scratch/trace/components.json", "utf8"));
const labelsBuf = readFileSync(".scratch/trace/labels.bin");
const comp = new Int32Array(labelsBuf.buffer, labelsBuf.byteOffset, W * H);
const keptById = new Map(kept.map((c) => [c.id, c]));

const src = readFileSync("web/src/game/mapData.ts", "utf8");
const re = /t\(\s*"([a-zA-Z]+)",\s*"[^"]*",\s*([\d.]+),\s*([\d.]+),\s*"([a-zA-Z]+)"/g;
const territories = [];
let m;
while ((m = re.exec(src)) !== null)
  territories.push({ id: m[1], ax: +m[2] * W, ay: +m[3] * H, cont: m[4] });

const CLASS_CONT = {
  northAmerica: "northAmerica", southAmerica: "southAmerica", europe: "europe",
  africa: "africa", asia: "asia", asiaCream: "asia", australia: "australia",
};

// Decoration zones (compass rose, sailing ship) — never territory art.
const DECOR = [
  [40, 580, 240, 820],
  [500, 720, 670, 890],
];
const inDecor = (x, y) => DECOR.some(([x0, y0, x1, y1]) => x >= x0 && y >= y0 && x <= x1 && y <= y1);

// Manual overrides: componentId -> territoryId ("" = drop).
const OVERRIDES = JSON.parse(readFileSync(".scratch/trace/overrides.json", "utf8"));

// --- Stage 0: synthetic splits (artwork merged two territories in one paint) ---
for (const s of OVERRIDES.splits ?? []) {
  const orig = keptById.get(s.comp);
  if (!orig) { console.log(`!! split comp #${s.comp} missing`); continue; }
  const synthId = 1000000 + s.comp;
  const [x0, y0, x1, y1] = orig.bbox;
  let aArea = 0, aSx = 0, aSy = 0, aX0 = W, aY0 = H, aX1 = 0, aY1 = 0;
  let bArea = 0, bSx = 0, bSy = 0, bX0 = W, bY0 = H, bX1 = 0, bY1 = 0;
  for (let y = y0; y <= y1; y++)
    for (let x = x0; x <= x1; x++) {
      const i = y * W + x;
      if (comp[i] !== s.comp) continue;
      const v = s.axis === "y" ? y : x;
      if (v >= s.at) {
        comp[i] = synthId;
        bArea++; bSx += x; bSy += y;
        if (x < bX0) bX0 = x; if (x > bX1) bX1 = x;
        if (y < bY0) bY0 = y; if (y > bY1) bY1 = y;
      } else {
        aArea++; aSx += x; aSy += y;
        if (x < aX0) aX0 = x; if (x > aX1) aX1 = x;
        if (y < aY0) aY0 = y; if (y > aY1) aY1 = y;
      }
    }
  Object.assign(orig, { area: aArea, cx: aSx / aArea, cy: aSy / aArea, bbox: [aX0, aY0, aX1, aY1] });
  const synth = { id: synthId, area: bArea, cx: bSx / bArea, cy: bSy / bArea, avg: orig.avg, bbox: [bX0, bY0, bX1, bY1], cls: orig.cls };
  kept.push(synth);
  keptById.set(synthId, synth);
  OVERRIDES.seeds = OVERRIDES.seeds ?? {};
  OVERRIDES.seeds[s.before] = s.comp;
  OVERRIDES.seeds[s.after] = synthId;
  console.log(`split #${s.comp} -> ${s.before}(${aArea}px) + ${s.after}(${bArea}px)`);
}

// --- Stage 1: seed by anchor containment, with conflict resolution ---
// Territory overrides win first: territoryId -> compId in OVERRIDES.seeds.
const assignment = new Map(); // compId -> territoryId
const seedComp = new Map(); // territoryId -> compId
const seedOverrides = OVERRIDES.seeds ?? {};
const pending = [];
for (const t of territories) {
  if (t.id in seedOverrides) {
    const cid = seedOverrides[t.id];
    assignment.set(cid, t.id);
    seedComp.set(t.id, cid);
    continue;
  }
  const px = Math.round(t.ax), py = Math.round(t.ay);
  const cid = comp[py * W + px];
  if (cid >= 0 && keptById.has(cid)) pending.push({ t, cid });
  else pending.push({ t, cid: null });
}
// containment seeds; if two territories claim one comp, the closer-to-centroid wins
const claims = new Map();
for (const p of pending) {
  if (p.cid == null) continue;
  const c = keptById.get(p.cid);
  const d = Math.hypot(c.cx - p.t.ax, c.cy - p.t.ay);
  const prev = claims.get(p.cid);
  if (!prev || d < prev.d) {
    if (prev) { console.log(`seed conflict #${p.cid}: ${p.t.id} beats ${prev.t.id}`); prev.cid = null; }
    claims.set(p.cid, Object.assign(p, { d }));
  } else {
    console.log(`seed conflict #${p.cid}: ${prev.t.id} beats ${p.t.id}`);
    p.cid = null;
  }
}
for (const [cid, p] of claims) {
  assignment.set(cid, p.t.id);
  seedComp.set(p.t.id, cid);
}
// fallback for unseeded: nearest unassigned compatible comp
for (const p of pending) {
  if (p.cid != null) continue;
  const t = p.t;
  let best = null, bd = Infinity;
  for (const c of kept) {
    if (assignment.has(c.id)) continue;
    if (inDecor(c.cx, c.cy)) continue;
    if (CLASS_CONT[c.cls.name] !== t.cont && c.cls.name !== "northAmerica" && c.cls.name !== "africa") continue;
    const d = (c.cx - t.ax) ** 2 + (c.cy - t.ay) ** 2;
    if (d < bd) { bd = d; best = c.id; }
  }
  if (best == null) { console.log(`!! no seed for ${t.id}`); continue; }
  console.log(`seed(fallback) ${t.id} -> #${best} d=${Math.sqrt(bd).toFixed(0)} area=${keptById.get(best).area}`);
  assignment.set(best, t.id);
  seedComp.set(t.id, best);
}

// --- Stage 2: attach leftovers by pixel distance to seeded comps ---
// Distance = min distance from leftover centroid to any pixel of the seed comp
// (sampled every 3rd pixel inside the seed bbox).
function distToComp(cx, cy, seedC) {
  const [x0, y0, x1, y1] = seedC.bbox;
  let best = Infinity;
  for (let y = y0; y <= y1; y += 3)
    for (let x = x0; x <= x1; x += 3) {
      if (comp[y * W + x] !== seedC.id) continue;
      const d = (x - cx) ** 2 + (y - cy) ** 2;
      if (d < best) best = d;
    }
  return Math.sqrt(best);
}
const attach = OVERRIDES.attach ?? {};
for (const c of kept) {
  if (assignment.has(c.id)) continue;
  if (String(c.id) in attach) {
    const tid = attach[String(c.id)];
    if (tid) assignment.set(c.id, tid);
    continue;
  }
  if (inDecor(c.cx, c.cy)) continue;
  let best = null, bd = Infinity;
  for (const [tid, scid] of seedComp) {
    const t = territories.find((tt) => tt.id === tid);
    const compat = CLASS_CONT[c.cls.name] === t.cont;
    const limit = compat ? 120 : 45;
    const d = distToComp(c.cx, c.cy, keptById.get(scid));
    if (d < limit && d < bd) { bd = d; best = tid; }
  }
  if (best) {
    assignment.set(c.id, best);
    if (c.area > 300) console.log(`attach #${c.id} area=${c.area} (${Math.round(c.cx)},${Math.round(c.cy)}) ${c.cls.name} -> ${best} d=${bd.toFixed(0)}`);
  } else if (c.area > 250) {
    console.log(`?? unassigned #${c.id} area=${c.area} (${Math.round(c.cx)},${Math.round(c.cy)}) ${c.cls.name}`);
  }
}

// --- Stage 3: per-territory mask, hole fill, pole of inaccessibility, contours ---
const compsOf = new Map();
for (const [cid, tid] of assignment) {
  if (!compsOf.has(tid)) compsOf.set(tid, []);
  compsOf.get(tid).push(keptById.get(cid));
}

function traceTerritory(tid) {
  const comps = compsOf.get(tid) ?? [];
  if (!comps.length) return null;
  const compIds = new Set(comps.map((c) => c.id));
  let x0 = W, y0 = H, x1 = 0, y1 = 0;
  for (const c of comps) {
    x0 = Math.min(x0, c.bbox[0]); y0 = Math.min(y0, c.bbox[1]);
    x1 = Math.max(x1, c.bbox[2]); y1 = Math.max(y1, c.bbox[3]);
  }
  x0 = Math.max(0, x0 - 2); y0 = Math.max(0, y0 - 2);
  x1 = Math.min(W - 1, x1 + 2); y1 = Math.min(H - 1, y1 + 2);
  const w = x1 - x0 + 1, h = y1 - y0 + 1;
  const maskT = new Uint8Array(w * h);
  for (let y = 0; y < h; y++)
    for (let x = 0; x < w; x++)
      if (compIds.has(comp[(y + y0) * W + (x + x0)])) maskT[y * w + x] = 1;

  // Hole fill: flood 0-pixels from crop border; unreached zeros become 1.
  // Bridge across thin ink: dilate mask by 2, fill holes, then erode by 2.
  const DIL = 2;
  let cur = maskT;
  for (let d = 0; d < DIL; d++) {
    const next = Uint8Array.from(cur);
    for (let y = 0; y < h; y++)
      for (let x = 0; x < w; x++) {
        const i = y * w + x;
        if (cur[i]) continue;
        if ((x > 0 && cur[i - 1]) || (x < w - 1 && cur[i + 1]) || (y > 0 && cur[i - w]) || (y < h - 1 && cur[i + w])) next[i] = 1;
      }
    cur = next;
  }
  const outside = new Uint8Array(w * h);
  const q = [];
  for (let x = 0; x < w; x++) { q.push(x); q.push((h - 1) * w + x); }
  for (let y = 0; y < h; y++) { q.push(y * w); q.push(y * w + w - 1); }
  for (const i of q) if (!cur[i]) outside[i] = 1;
  let head = 0;
  const queue = q.filter((i) => outside[i]);
  while (head < queue.length) {
    const i = queue[head++];
    const x = i % w, y = (i / w) | 0;
    for (const j of [x > 0 ? i - 1 : -1, x < w - 1 ? i + 1 : -1, y > 0 ? i - w : -1, y < h - 1 ? i + w : -1])
      if (j >= 0 && !cur[j] && !outside[j]) { outside[j] = 1; queue.push(j); }
  }
  const filled = new Uint8Array(w * h);
  for (let i = 0; i < w * h; i++) filled[i] = cur[i] || !outside[i] ? 1 : 0;
  // Erode back
  let er = filled;
  for (let d = 0; d < DIL; d++) {
    const next = Uint8Array.from(er);
    for (let y = 0; y < h; y++)
      for (let x = 0; x < w; x++) {
        const i = y * w + x;
        if (!er[i]) continue;
        if (x === 0 || y === 0 || x === w - 1 || y === h - 1 || !er[i - 1] || !er[i + 1] || !er[i - w] || !er[i + w]) next[i] = 0;
      }
    er = next;
  }
  // Keep union with original mask so thin strips survive erosion.
  const finalMask = new Uint8Array(w * h);
  for (let i = 0; i < w * h; i++) finalMask[i] = er[i] || maskT[i] ? 1 : 0;

  // Pole of inaccessibility on the LARGEST connected part (BFS distance transform).
  const dist = new Int32Array(w * h).fill(-1);
  const dq = [];
  for (let y = 0; y < h; y++)
    for (let x = 0; x < w; x++) {
      const i = y * w + x;
      if (!finalMask[i]) { dist[i] = 0; dq.push(i); }
      else if (x === 0 || y === 0 || x === w - 1 || y === h - 1) { dist[i] = 1; dq.push(i); }
    }
  head = 0;
  let bestI = -1, bestD = -1;
  while (head < dq.length) {
    const i = dq[head++];
    const x = i % w, y = (i / w) | 0;
    for (const j of [x > 0 ? i - 1 : -1, x < w - 1 ? i + 1 : -1, y > 0 ? i - w : -1, y < h - 1 ? i + w : -1])
      if (j >= 0 && dist[j] === -1) { dist[j] = dist[i] + 1; dq.push(j); }
    if (finalMask[i] && dist[i] > bestD) { bestD = dist[i]; bestI = i; }
  }
  const pole = { x: x0 + (bestI % w), y: y0 + ((bestI / w) | 0), clearance: bestD };

  // Boundary-edge chaining: collect oriented unit edges between filled and
  // empty pixels (interior kept on the left), then chain into closed loops.
  const at = (x, y) => (x >= 0 && y >= 0 && x < w && y < h ? finalMask[y * w + x] : 0);
  const edges = new Map(); // "x,y" (start vertex) -> array of end vertices
  const addEdge = (x1, y1, x2, y2) => {
    const k = `${x1},${y1}`;
    if (!edges.has(k)) edges.set(k, []);
    edges.get(k).push([x2, y2]);
  };
  for (let y = 0; y < h; y++)
    for (let x = 0; x < w; x++) {
      if (!at(x, y)) continue;
      if (!at(x, y - 1)) addEdge(x, y, x + 1, y); // top edge, rightward
      if (!at(x + 1, y)) addEdge(x + 1, y, x + 1, y + 1); // right edge, downward
      if (!at(x, y + 1)) addEdge(x + 1, y + 1, x, y + 1); // bottom edge, leftward
      if (!at(x - 1, y)) addEdge(x, y + 1, x, y); // left edge, upward
    }
  const contours = [];
  for (const [startKey, ends] of edges) {
    while (ends.length) {
      const [sx, sy] = startKey.split(",").map(Number);
      let [cx2, cy2] = ends.pop();
      const loop = [[sx, sy], [cx2, cy2]];
      let guard = 0;
      while (guard++ < 200000) {
        const k = `${cx2},${cy2}`;
        const nexts = edges.get(k);
        if (!nexts || !nexts.length) break;
        let pick = 0;
        if (nexts.length > 1) {
          // prefer sharpest left turn to keep loops separate at pinch points
          const [px2, py2] = loop[loop.length - 2];
          const inAngle = Math.atan2(cy2 - py2, cx2 - px2);
          let bestScore = -Infinity;
          for (let i = 0; i < nexts.length; i++) {
            const a = Math.atan2(nexts[i][1] - cy2, nexts[i][0] - cx2);
            let rel = a - inAngle;
            while (rel <= -Math.PI) rel += 2 * Math.PI;
            while (rel > Math.PI) rel -= 2 * Math.PI;
            if (rel > bestScore) { bestScore = rel; pick = i; }
          }
        }
        const [nx, ny] = nexts.splice(pick, 1)[0];
        if (nx === sx && ny === sy) break;
        loop.push([nx, ny]);
        cx2 = nx; cy2 = ny;
      }
      if (loop.length > 12) contours.push(loop.map(([px3, py3]) => [px3 + x0, py3 + y0]));
    }
  }
  return { pole, contours, area: comps.reduce((s, c) => s + c.area, 0) };
}

// Douglas-Peucker simplification
function rdp(pts, eps) {
  if (pts.length < 3) return pts;
  const keep = new Uint8Array(pts.length);
  keep[0] = keep[pts.length - 1] = 1;
  const stack = [[0, pts.length - 1]];
  while (stack.length) {
    const [a, b] = stack.pop();
    const [ax, ay] = pts[a], [bx, by] = pts[b];
    const dx = bx - ax, dy = by - ay;
    const len = Math.hypot(dx, dy) || 1;
    let maxD = 0, maxI = -1;
    for (let i = a + 1; i < b; i++) {
      const d = Math.abs(dy * pts[i][0] - dx * pts[i][1] + bx * ay - by * ax) / len;
      if (d > maxD) { maxD = d; maxI = i; }
    }
    if (maxD > eps) { keep[maxI] = 1; stack.push([a, maxI], [maxI, b]); }
  }
  return pts.filter((_, i) => keep[i]);
}

const shapes = {};
for (const t of territories) {
  const traced = traceTerritory(t.id);
  if (!traced) { console.log(`!! no shape for ${t.id}`); continue; }
  const simplified = traced.contours
    .map((c) => rdp(c, 1.4))
    .filter((c) => c.length >= 4)
    .sort((a, b) => b.length - a.length);
  shapes[t.id] = {
    anchor: { x: traced.pole.x, y: traced.pole.y },
    clearance: traced.pole.clearance,
    area: traced.area,
    contours: simplified,
  };
  console.log(`${t.id.padEnd(20)} anchor=(${traced.pole.x},${traced.pole.y}) clear=${traced.pole.clearance} parts=${simplified.length} pts=${simplified.reduce((s, c) => s + c.length, 0)}`);
}
writeFileSync(".scratch/trace/shapes.json", JSON.stringify({ W, H, shapes }));

// --- Review render ---
const png = PNG.sync.read(readFileSync("web/public/risk/world-map.png"));
const out = new PNG({ width: W, height: H });
png.data.copy(out.data);
function drawLine(xa, ya, xb, yb, r, g, b) {
  const steps = Math.max(Math.abs(xb - xa), Math.abs(yb - ya), 1);
  for (let s = 0; s <= steps; s++) {
    const x = Math.round(xa + ((xb - xa) * s) / steps);
    const y = Math.round(ya + ((yb - ya) * s) / steps);
    if (x < 0 || y < 0 || x >= W || y >= H) continue;
    const i = (y * W + x) * 4;
    out.data[i] = r; out.data[i + 1] = g; out.data[i + 2] = b;
  }
}
function drawDot(x, y, rad, r, g, b) {
  for (let dy = -rad; dy <= rad; dy++)
    for (let dx = -rad; dx <= rad; dx++) {
      if (dx * dx + dy * dy > rad * rad) continue;
      const px = x + dx, py = y + dy;
      if (px < 0 || py < 0 || px >= W || py >= H) continue;
      const i = (py * W + px) * 4;
      out.data[i] = r; out.data[i + 1] = g; out.data[i + 2] = b;
    }
}
const HUES = [[220, 30, 30], [30, 90, 220], [20, 140, 40], [200, 30, 180], [230, 120, 20], [10, 170, 170]];
let hi = 0;
for (const [tid, s] of Object.entries(shapes)) {
  const [r, g, b] = HUES[hi++ % HUES.length];
  for (const c of s.contours)
    for (let i = 0; i < c.length; i++) {
      const [xa, ya] = c[i], [xb, yb] = c[(i + 1) % c.length];
      drawLine(xa, ya, xb, yb, r, g, b);
    }
  drawDot(s.anchor.x, s.anchor.y, 5, r, g, b);
  drawDot(s.anchor.x, s.anchor.y, 2, 255, 255, 255);
}
writeFileSync(".scratch/trace/review.png", PNG.sync.write(out));
console.log("wrote review.png");

   "cls": {
    "name": "southAmerica",
    "dist": 14.52583904633395
   }
  }
 ]

File: /.scratch/trace/gen.mjs

// Generates web/src/game/mapShapes.ts, updates mapData.ts anchors and prints
// the test lock block, from the traced shapes.json.
import { readFileSync, writeFileSync } from "node:fs";

const { W, H, shapes } = JSON.parse(readFileSync(".scratch/trace/shapes.json", "utf8"));

// Territory order + isExtra from mapData for stable output
const src = readFileSync("web/src/game/mapData.ts", "utf8");
const re = /t\(\s*"([a-zA-Z]+)",\s*"[^"]*",\s*([\d.]+),\s*([\d.]+),\s*"([a-zA-Z]+)",\s*\[[^\]]*\](,\s*true)?/g;
const order = [];
let m;
while ((m = re.exec(src)) !== null) order.push({ id: m[1], isExtra: Boolean(m[4] && m[0].includes(", true")) });

const anchors = {};
const paths = {};
for (const { id } of order) {
  const s = shapes[id];
  if (!s) { console.log(`!! missing shape ${id}`); continue; }
  // Piece bases render ~28px below the anchor; lift anchors in tight regions
  // so the base stays on land.
  const shiftY = s.clearance >= 32 ? 0 : Math.min(16, 32 - s.clearance);
  anchors[id] = {
    x: +(s.anchor.x / W).toFixed(4),
    y: +((s.anchor.y - shiftY) / H).toFixed(4),
  };
  const d = s.contours
    .map((c) => {
      const pts = c.map(([x, y]) => `${Math.round(x * 10) / 10} ${Math.round(y * 10) / 10}`);
      return `M${pts.join(" L")} Z`;
    })
    .join(" ");
  paths[id] = d;
}

// mapShapes.ts
let ts = `import type { TerritoryId } from "./types";

/**
 * High-precision territory outlines traced from the painted world board
 * (web/public/risk/world-map.png, ${W}x${H}). Generated by .scratch/trace —
 * do not edit by hand. Coordinates are board pixels.
 */
export const SHAPES_W = ${W};
export const SHAPES_H = ${H};

export const TERRITORY_PATHS: Record<TerritoryId, string> = {
`;
for (const { id } of order) {
  ts += `  ${id}:\n    "${paths[id]}",\n`;
}
ts += `};\n`;
writeFileSync("web/src/game/mapShapes.ts", ts);
console.log(`wrote mapShapes.ts (${(ts.length / 1024).toFixed(0)} KB)`);

// Update mapData.ts anchors in place
let updated = src;
for (const { id } of order) {
  const a = anchors[id];
  const rowRe = new RegExp(`(t\\(\\s*"${id}",\\s*"[^"]*",\\s*)([\\d.]+)(,\\s*)([\\d.]+)`);
  if (!rowRe.test(updated)) { console.log(`!! could not update ${id}`); continue; }
  updated = updated.replace(rowRe, `$1${a.x.toFixed(4)}$3${a.y.toFixed(4)}`);
}
writeFileSync("web/src/game/mapData.ts", updated);
console.log("updated mapData.ts anchors");

// Test lock block (standard territories only)
let block = "";
for (const { id, isExtra } of order) {
  if (isExtra) continue;
  const a = anchors[id];
  block += `  ${id}: [${a.x.toFixed(4)}, ${a.y.toFixed(4)}],\n`;
}
writeFileSync(".scratch/trace/test-coords.txt", block);
console.log(block);

File: /.scratch/trace/label-comps.mjs

// Renders kept component IDs at their centroids for manual identification.
import { readFileSync } from "node:fs";
import { execSync } from "node:child_process";

const { kept } = JSON.parse(readFileSync(".scratch/trace/components.json", "utf8"));
const [outPath, minArea, cx, cy, cw, ch, scale] = process.argv.slice(2);
const min = +(minArea ?? 300);
const crop = cx !== undefined ? { x: +cx, y: +cy, w: +cw, h: +ch, s: +(scale ?? 2) } : null;

let base = "web/public/risk/world-map.png";
if (crop) {
  execSync(`magick "${base}" -crop ${crop.w}x${crop.h}+${crop.x}+${crop.y} +repage -resize ${Math.round(crop.w * crop.s)}x${Math.round(crop.h * crop.s)} .scratch/trace/_crop.png`);
  base = ".scratch/trace/_crop.png";
}
let draw = "";
for (const c of kept) {
  if (c.area < min) continue;
  let px = c.cx, py = c.cy;
  if (crop) {
    if (px < crop.x || px > crop.x + crop.w || py < crop.y || py > crop.y + crop.h) continue;
    px = (px - crop.x) * crop.s;
    py = (py - crop.y) * crop.s;
  }
  draw += ` -fill red -stroke none -draw "circle ${px},${py} ${px + 3},${py}"`;
  draw += ` -fill black -stroke white -strokewidth 1 -pointsize ${crop ? 20 : 15} -draw "text ${px + 5},${py - 4} '${c.id}'"`;
}
execSync(`magick "${base}"${draw} "${outPath}"`);
console.log("wrote", outPath);

File: /.scratch/trace/sample-colors.mjs

// Samples average colors at current territory anchors + ocean reference points.
import { readFileSync } from "node:fs";
import { PNG } from "../../web/node_modules/pngjs/lib/png.js";

const png = PNG.sync.read(readFileSync("web/public/risk/world-map.png"));
const { width: W, height: H, data } = png;
console.log(`image ${W}x${H}`);

const src = readFileSync("web/src/game/mapData.ts", "utf8");
const re = /t\(\s*"([a-zA-Z]+)",\s*"[^"]*",\s*([\d.]+),\s*([\d.]+),\s*"([a-zA-Z]+)"/g;
const anchors = [];
let m;
while ((m = re.exec(src)) !== null) anchors.push({ id: m[1], x: +m[2], y: +m[3], cont: m[4] });

function sample(px, py, rad = 3) {
  let r = 0, g = 0, b = 0, n = 0;
  for (let dy = -rad; dy <= rad; dy++)
    for (let dx = -rad; dx <= rad; dx++) {
      const x = Math.round(px) + dx, y = Math.round(py) + dy;
      if (x < 0 || y < 0 || x >= W || y >= H) continue;
      const i = (y * W + x) * 4;
      r += data[i]; g += data[i + 1]; b += data[i + 2]; n++;
    }
  return [Math.round(r / n), Math.round(g / n), Math.round(b / n)];
}

for (const a of anchors) {
  const c = sample(a.x * W, a.y * H);
  console.log(`${a.id.padEnd(20)} ${a.cont.padEnd(14)} rgb(${c.join(",")})`);
}
console.log("--- ocean refs ---");
for (const [x, y] of [[0.5, 0.95], [0.05, 0.7], [0.65, 0.75], [0.95, 0.45], [0.35, 0.45]]) {
  console.log(`ocean(${x},${y}) rgb(${sample(x * W, y * H).join(",")})`);
}

File: /.scratch/trace/segment.mjs
---

// Segments the painted board into territory regions.
// Walls = dark ink border lines. Ocean = flood fill from image edges.
// Remaining connected components = territory fills, classified by color.
import { readFileSync, writeFileSync } from "node:fs";
import { PNG } from "../../web/node_modules/pngjs/lib/png.js";

const png = PNG.sync.read(readFileSync("web/public/risk/world-map.png"));
const { width: W, height: H, data } = png;
const N = W * H;

const lum = new Float32Array(N);
for (let i = 0; i < N; i++) {
  const r = data[i * 4], g = data[i * 4 + 1], b = data[i * 4 + 2];
  lum[i] = 0.299 * r + 0.587 * g + 0.114 * b;
}

// Per-pixel palette classification (index into PALETTE, done before walls).
const PALETTE = [
  ["northAmerica", [228, 185, 92]],
  ["southAmerica", [220, 130, 88]],
  ["europe", [185, 168, 208]],
  ["africa", [209, 156, 66]],
  ["asia", [185, 201, 124]],
  ["asiaCream", [246, 225, 163]],
  ["australia", [219, 130, 128]],
  ["ocean", [240, 188, 58]],
];
function classifyRGB(r, g, b) {
  let best = 0, bd = Infinity;
  for (let p = 0; p < PALETTE.length; p++) {
    const c = PALETTE[p][1];
    const d = (r - c[0]) ** 2 + (g - c[1]) ** 2 + (b - c[2]) ** 2;
    if (d < bd) { bd = d; best = p; }
  }
  return best;
}
const pixClass = new Uint8Array(N);
for (let i = 0; i < N; i++) pixClass[i] = classifyRGB(data[i * 4], data[i * 4 + 1], data[i * 4 + 2]);

// Local mean luminance via integral image (radius R box) for adaptive walls.
const integral = new Float64Array((W + 1) * (H + 1));
for (let y = 0; y < H; y++) {
  let rowSum = 0;
  for (let x = 0; x < W; x++) {
    rowSum += lum[y * W + x];
    integral[(y + 1) * (W + 1) + (x + 1)] = integral[y * (W + 1) + (x + 1)] + rowSum;
  }
}
const R = 9;
function localMean(x, y) {
  const x0 = Math.max(0, x - R), y0 = Math.max(0, y - R);
  const x1 = Math.min(W - 1, x + R), y1 = Math.min(H - 1, y + R);
  const s =
    integral[(y1 + 1) * (W + 1) + (x1 + 1)] - integral[y0 * (W + 1) + (x1 + 1)] -
    integral[(y1 + 1) * (W + 1) + x0] + integral[y0 * (W + 1) + x0];
  return s / ((x1 - x0 + 1) * (y1 - y0 + 1));
}

// 0 = unassigned, 1 = ink wall, 2 = ocean
// Wall = hard-dark ink OR locally much darker than surroundings (thin borders).
const mask = new Uint8Array(N);
for (let y = 0; y < H; y++)
  for (let x = 0; x < W; x++) {
    const i = y * W + x;
    if (lum[i] < 132 || lum[i] < localMean(x, y) * 0.84) mask[i] = 1;
  }
// Dilate ink by 1px to close anti-aliasing gaps in thin border lines.
const inkCopy = Uint8Array.from(mask);
for (let y = 0; y < H; y++) {
  for (let x = 0; x < W; x++) {
    const i = y * W + x;
    if (inkCopy[i] === 1) continue;
    if (
      (x > 0 && inkCopy[i - 1] === 1) || (x < W - 1 && inkCopy[i + 1] === 1) ||
      (y > 0 && inkCopy[i - W] === 1) || (y < H - 1 && inkCopy[i + W] === 1)
    ) mask[i] = 1;
  }
}

// Flood ocean from all edges (BFS, 4-conn) through non-ink pixels.
const queue = new Int32Array(N);
let qh = 0, qt = 0;
for (let x = 0; x < W; x++) {
  for (const y of [0, H - 1]) {
    const i = y * W + x;
    if (mask[i] === 0) { mask[i] = 2; queue[qt++] = i; }
  }
}
for (let y = 0; y < H; y++) {
  for (const x of [0, W - 1]) {
    const i = y * W + x;
    if (mask[i] === 0) { mask[i] = 2; queue[qt++] = i; }
  }
}
while (qh < qt) {
  const i = queue[qh++];
  const x = i % W, y = (i / W) | 0;
  if (x > 0 && mask[i - 1] === 0) { mask[i - 1] = 2; queue[qt++] = i - 1; }
  if (x < W - 1 && mask[i + 1] === 0) { mask[i + 1] = 2; queue[qt++] = i + 1; }
  if (y > 0 && mask[i - W] === 0) { mask[i - W] = 2; queue[qt++] = i - W; }
  if (y < H - 1 && mask[i + W] === 0) { mask[i + W] = 2; queue[qt++] = i + W; }
}

// Connected components of remaining pixels (4-conn, same palette class only
// so differently-painted neighbors split even if the ink line has gaps).
const comp = new Int32Array(N).fill(-1);
const comps = [];
for (let start = 0; start < N; start++) {
  if (mask[start] !== 0 || comp[start] !== -1) continue;
  const id = comps.length;
  let head = 0, tail = 0;
  queue[tail++] = start;
  comp[start] = id;
  let area = 0, sx = 0, sy = 0, sr = 0, sg = 0, sb = 0;
  let minX = W, maxX = 0, minY = H, maxY = 0;
  while (head < tail) {
    const i = queue[head++];
    const x = i % W, y = (i / W) | 0;
    area++;
    sx += x; sy += y;
    sr += data[i * 4]; sg += data[i * 4 + 1]; sb += data[i * 4 + 2];
    if (x < minX) minX = x; if (x > maxX) maxX = x;
    if (y < minY) minY = y; if (y > maxY) maxY = y;
    const cls = pixClass[start];
    if (x > 0 && mask[i - 1] === 0 && comp[i - 1] === -1 && pixClass[i - 1] === cls) { comp[i - 1] = id; queue[tail++] = i - 1; }
    if (x < W - 1 && mask[i + 1] === 0 && comp[i + 1] === -1 && pixClass[i + 1] === cls) { comp[i + 1] = id; queue[tail++] = i + 1; }
    if (y > 0 && mask[i - W] === 0 && comp[i - W] === -1 && pixClass[i - W] === cls) { comp[i - W] = id; queue[tail++] = i - W; }
    if (y < H - 1 && mask[i + W] === 0 && comp[i + W] === -1 && pixClass[i + W] === cls) { comp[i + W] = id; queue[tail++] = i + W; }
  }
  comps.push({
    id, area,
    cx: sx / area, cy: sy / area,
    avg: [Math.round(sr / area), Math.round(sg / area), Math.round(sb / area)],
    bbox: [minX, minY, maxX, maxY],
  });
}

// Classify each component by nearest palette color.
function classify(avg) {
  let best = null, bd = Infinity;
  for (const [name, c] of PALETTE) {
    const d = (avg[0] - c[0]) ** 2 + (avg[1] - c[1]) ** 2 + (avg[2] - c[2]) ** 2;
    if (d < bd) { bd = d; best = name; }
  }
  return { name: best, dist: Math.sqrt(bd) };
}

const MIN_AREA = 60;
// Island zones where even ocean-tinted small comps must be kept (Falklands etc.)
const KEEP_ZONES = [
  [440, 880, 510, 940],
  [350, 830, 420, 915],
];
const inKeepZone = (c) => KEEP_ZONES.some(([x0, y0, x1, y1]) => c.cx >= x0 && c.cy >= y0 && c.cx <= x1 && c.cy <= y1);
const kept = comps
  .map((c) => ({ ...c, cls: classify(c.avg) }))
  .filter((c) => (c.area >= MIN_AREA && c.cls.name !== "ocean") || (c.area >= 30 && inKeepZone(c)))
  .sort((a, b) => b.area - a.area);

console.log(`components kept: ${kept.length}`);
for (const c of kept) {
  console.log(
    `#${String(c.id).padStart(6)} area=${String(c.area).padStart(7)} ` +
    `c=(${Math.round(c.cx)},${Math.round(c.cy)}) bbox=[${c.bbox.join(",")}] ` +
    `rgb(${c.avg.join(",")}) -> ${c.cls.name} (d=${c.cls.dist.toFixed(0)})`
  );
}

// Save component labels + kept metadata for the next stage.
writeFileSync(".scratch/trace/components.json", JSON.stringify({ W, H, kept }, null, 1));
const buf = Buffer.alloc(N * 4);
for (let i = 0; i < N; i++) buf.writeInt32LE(comp[i], i * 4);
writeFileSync(".scratch/trace/labels.bin", buf);

// Debug render: each kept component gets its continent color, ocean dimmed.
const CONT_COLORS = {
  northAmerica: [217, 177, 103], southAmerica: [224, 143, 116], europe: [130, 100, 200],
  africa: [180, 120, 40], asia: [110, 170, 60], asiaCream: [255, 240, 180], australia: [225, 100, 160],
};
const out = new PNG({ width: W, height: H });
const keptSet = new Map(kept.map((c) => [c.id, c]));
for (let i = 0; i < N; i++) {
  const o = i * 4;
  let r = data[o] * 0.25, g = data[o + 1] * 0.25, b = data[o + 2] * 0.25;
  const c = comp[i] >= 0 ? keptSet.get(comp[i]) : undefined;
  if (c) {
    const cc = CONT_COLORS[c.cls.name];
    r = cc[0]; g = cc[1]; b = cc[2];
  }
  out.data[o] = r; out.data[o + 1] = g; out.data[o + 2] = b; out.data[o + 3] = 255;
}
writeFileSync(".scratch/trace/segmented.png", PNG.sync.write(out));
console.log("wrote segmented.png");

File: /.scratch/overlay-anchors.mjs
---

// Renders territory anchors (from web/src/game/mapData.ts) onto a map image.
// Usage: node .scratch/overlay-anchors.mjs <mapPath> <outPath> [cropX cropY cropW cropH scale]
import { readFileSync, writeFileSync } from "node:fs";
import { execSync } from "node:child_process";

const src = readFileSync("web/src/game/mapData.ts", "utf8");
const re = /t\(\s*"([a-zA-Z]+)",\s*"[^"]*",\s*([\d.]+),\s*([\d.]+)/g;
const anchors = [];
let m;
while ((m = re.exec(src)) !== null) {
  anchors.push({ id: m[1], x: parseFloat(m[2]), y: parseFloat(m[3]) });
}

const [mapPath, outPath, cx, cy, cw, ch, scale] = process.argv.slice(2);
const W = 1536, H = 1024;
const crop = cx !== undefined ? { x: +cx, y: +cy, w: +cw, h: +ch, s: +(scale ?? 1) } : null;

let draw = "";
for (const a of anchors) {
  let px = a.x * W, py = a.y * H;
  if (crop) {
    if (px < crop.x || px > crop.x + crop.w || py < crop.y || py > crop.y + crop.h) continue;
    px = (px - crop.x) * crop.s;
    py = (py - crop.y) * crop.s;
  }
  const r = crop ? 6 : 5;
  draw += ` -fill red -stroke white -strokewidth 2 -draw "circle ${px},${py} ${px + r},${py}"`;
  draw += ` -stroke none -fill black -pointsize ${crop ? 18 : 13} -draw "text ${px + 8},${py + 4} '${a.id}'"`;
}

let base = mapPath;
if (crop) {
  execSync(`magick "${mapPath}" -crop ${crop.w}x${crop.h}+${crop.x}+${crop.y} +repage -resize ${Math.round(crop.w * crop.s)}x${Math.round(crop.h * crop.s)} .scratch/_crop.png`);
  base = ".scratch/_crop.png";
}
execSync(`magick "${base}"${draw} "${outPath}"`);
console.log(`wrote ${outPath} with ${anchors.length} anchors parsed`);

File: /web/scripts/capture-game-map.mjs
---

import { spawn } from "node:child_process";
import { chromium } from "playwright";

const HOST = "127.0.0.1";
const PORT = "8080";
const BASE_URL = `http://${HOST}:${PORT}`;
const OUT = process.env.MAP_SCREENSHOT_PATH ?? "/tmp/game-final.png";

function waitForServer(child) {
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    let settled = false;
    const timeout = setTimeout(() => {
      if (!settled) {
        settled = true;
        reject(new Error(`Timed out waiting for Vite at ${BASE_URL}`));
      }
    }, 30_000);

    const onData = (chunk) => {
      const text = chunk.toString();
      process.stdout.write(text);
      if (!settled && text.includes(BASE_URL)) {
        settled = true;
        clearTimeout(timeout);
        resolve();
      }
    };

    child.stdout.on("data", onData);
    child.stderr.on("data", (chunk) => process.stderr.write(chunk.toString()));
    child.on("exit", (code) => {
      if (!settled) {
        settled = true;
        clearTimeout(timeout);
        reject(new Error(`Vite exited before becoming ready (code ${code ?? "unknown"})`));
      }
    });
  });
}

const appRoot = new URL("..", import.meta.url);
const server = spawn(process.execPath, ["node_modules/vite/bin/vite.js", "--host", HOST], {
  cwd: appRoot,
  stdio: ["ignore", "pipe", "pipe"],
});

let browser;
try {
  await waitForServer(server);
  browser = await chromium.launch({ headless: true });
  const page = await browser.newPage({ viewport: { width: 1196, height: 780 }, deviceScaleFactor: 1 });
  await page.goto(`${BASE_URL}/setup`, { waitUntil: "domcontentloaded" });
  await page.getByText("COMMENCE CAMPAIGN").click();
  await page.waitForSelector('svg[aria-label="Campaign map"]', { timeout: 10_000 });
  await page.waitForTimeout(2_500);
  await page.screenshot({ path: OUT, fullPage: true });
  const viewBox = await page.locator('svg[aria-label="Campaign map"]').evaluate((el) => el.getAttribute("viewBox"));
  console.log(`Captured ${OUT}`);
  console.log(`viewBox: ${viewBox}`);
} finally {
  await browser?.close();
  server.kill("SIGTERM");
}

File: /web/src/components/game/BattleDispatch.tsx

import { FieldPanel, ImperialDivider, SectionHeader } from "@/components/game/FieldPanel";
import { RiskDie } from "@/components/game/RiskDie";
import { ART } from "@/lib/art";
import { TERRITORY_MAP } from "@/game/mapData";
import type { GameState, LogTone } from "@/game/types";
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";

const TONE_CLASS: Record<LogTone, string> = {
  info: "text-muted-foreground",
  gold: "text-gold",
  crimson: "text-crimson-bright",
  battle: "text-foreground",
};

/** "Field Dispatch" panel: latest battle report with hex dice plus the campaign log. */
export function BattleDispatch({ game }: { game: GameState }) {
  const battle = game.lastBattle;
  const attacker = battle ? game.players[battle.attacker] : null;
  const defender = battle ? game.players[battle.defender] : null;

  return (
    <FieldPanel className="flex min-h-0 flex-1 flex-col overflow-hidden">
      <img
        src={ART.warCrest}
        alt=""
        aria-hidden
        className="pointer-events-none absolute -bottom-3 -right-3 h-28 w-28 object-contain opacity-[0.08]"
      />
      <SectionHeader index={2} title="Field Dispatch" />
      {battle && attacker && defender ? (
        <div key={`${battle.from}-${battle.to}-${game.logCounter}`} className="animate-dispatch-in">
          <p className="font-body text-sm">
            <span style={{ color: attacker.color }} className="font-semibold">
              {attacker.name}
            </span>{" "}
            assaults <span className="font-semibold">{TERRITORY_MAP[battle.to].name}</span> from{" "}
            {TERRITORY_MAP[battle.from].name}
            {battle.rounds > 1 && <span className="text-muted-foreground"> — {battle.rounds} rounds</span>}
          </p>
          <div className="mt-2 flex items-center justify-between gap-2">
            <div className="flex gap-1">
              {battle.attackerRolls.map((roll, i) => (
                <RiskDie key={`a-${i}`} value={roll} tier={battle.attackerTier} delay={i * 90} />
              ))}
            </div>
            <span className="font-display text-[10px] uppercase tracking-imperial text-muted-foreground">vs</span>
            <div className="flex gap-1">
              {battle.defenderRolls.map((roll, i) => (
                <RiskDie key={`d-${i}`} value={roll} tier={battle.defenderTier} delay={i * 90 + 60} />
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
          <p className="mt-2 font-body text-xs text-muted-foreground">
            Losses — attacker <span className="font-semibold text-crimson-bright">{battle.attackerLosses}</span>,
            defender <span className="font-semibold text-crimson-bright">{battle.defenderLosses}</span>.{" "}
            {battle.conquered && <span className="font-semibold text-gold">Territory taken.</span>}
          </p>
          <ImperialDivider className="my-3" />
        </div>
      ) : (
        <p className="mb-2 font-body text-xs italic text-muted-foreground">No engagements reported this turn.</p>
      )}
      <div className="min-h-0 flex-1 overflow-y-auto pr-1" aria-live="polite">
        <ul className="space-y-1">
          {game.log.map((entry) => (
            <li key={entry.id} className={cn("font-body text-xs leading-snug", TONE_CLASS[entry.tone])}>
              <span className="mr-1 font-display text-[9px] text-gold-dim">T{entry.turn}</span>
              {entry.text}
            </li>
          ))}
        </ul>
      </div>
    </FieldPanel>
  );
}

File: /web/src/components/game/BattleView.tsx

import { useCallback, useEffect, useRef, useState } from "react";

import { RiskDie } from "@/components/game/RiskDie";
import { battleViewUrl } from "@/game/battleViews";
import { playRandomSfx, playSfx } from "@/lib/sfx";
import { TERRITORY_MAP } from "@/game/mapData";
import type { BattleReport, GameState } from "@/game/types";

const RESULT_HOLD_MS = 3600;

type BattleViewPhase = "ready" | "rolled";

/**
 * Cinematic battle view: the original RISK II aerial painting of the contested
 * territory fills the screen (the manual's "fly-to" sequence) while the dice
 * comparison and casualties play out over it. Shown only for battles involving
 * the human commander — AI-vs-AI engagements resolve fast, as per Fast AI.
 * The commander manually presses the dice to roll, which also satisfies mobile
 * browser audio rules before the battle SFX are fired.
 */
export function BattleView({ game, enabled }: { game: GameState; enabled: boolean }) {
  const [scene, setScene] = useState<BattleReport | null>(null);
  const [sceneKey, setSceneKey] = useState<number>(0);
  const [phase, setPhase] = useState<BattleViewPhase>("ready");
  const lastReportRef = useRef<BattleReport | null>(game.lastBattle);
  const timerRef = useRef<number | null>(null);
  const rolledRef = useRef(false);
  const soundStopsRef = useRef<(() => void)[]>([]);
  const soundTimerRef = useRef<number[]>([]);

  const clearDismissTimer = useCallback(() => {
    if (timerRef.current !== null) {
      window.clearTimeout(timerRef.current);
      timerRef.current = null;
    }
  }, []);

  const stopSceneSounds = useCallback(() => {
    soundTimerRef.current.forEach((timer) => window.clearTimeout(timer));
    soundTimerRef.current = [];
    soundStopsRef.current.forEach((stop) => stop());
    soundStopsRef.current = [];
  }, []);

  const dismiss = useCallback(() => {
    rolledRef.current = false;
    clearDismissTimer();
    stopSceneSounds();
    setScene(null);
  }, [clearDismissTimer, stopSceneSounds]);

  useEffect(() => {
    const report = game.lastBattle;
    if (!report || report === lastReportRef.current) return;
    lastReportRef.current = report;
    if (!enabled) return;
    const attacker = game.players[report.attacker];
    const defender = game.players[report.defender];
    if (!attacker?.isHuman && !defender?.isHuman) return;
    rolledRef.current = false;
    stopSceneSounds();
    clearDismissTimer();
    setPhase("ready");
    setScene(report);
    setSceneKey((k) => k + 1);
  }, [clearDismissTimer, game.lastBattle, game.players, enabled, stopSceneSounds]);

  const rollDice = useCallback(() => {
    if (!scene || rolledRef.current) return;
    rolledRef.current = true;
    setPhase("rolled");
    clearDismissTimer();
    stopSceneSounds();
    const stops = soundStopsRef.current;
    stops.push(playSfx("dice_roll", { volume: 0.62 }));
    stops.push(playSfx("battle_din", { volume: 0.25, maxMs: RESULT_HOLD_MS }));
    soundTimerRef.current.push(
      window.setTimeout(() => {
        const heavy = scene.rounds > 2 || scene.attackerLosses + scene.defenderLosses >= 4;
        stops.push(
          heavy
            ? playRandomSfx(["volley_long", "roar", "cannon_a"], { volume: 0.45 })
            : playRandomSfx(["volley_short", "cannon_b", "cannon_c", "clash_c"], { volume: 0.45 }),
        );
      }, 260),
    );
    if (scene.conquered) {
      soundTimerRef.current.push(
        window.setTimeout(() => {
          stops.push(playSfx("trumpet", { volume: 0.5 }));
        }, 1280),
      );
    }
    timerRef.current = window.setTimeout(() => {
      timerRef.current = null;
      dismiss();
    }, RESULT_HOLD_MS);
  }, [clearDismissTimer, dismiss, scene, stopSceneSounds]);

  useEffect(
    () => () => {
      clearDismissTimer();
      stopSceneSounds();
    },
    [clearDismissTimer, stopSceneSounds],
  );

  if (!scene) return null;

  const attacker = game.players[scene.attacker];
  const defender = game.players[scene.defender];
  if (!attacker || !defender) return null;
  const ground = TERRITORY_MAP[scene.to];
  const rolled = phase === "rolled";

  return (
    <div
      key={sceneKey}
      role="dialog"
      aria-label={`Battle for ${ground.name}`}
      aria-modal="true"
      className="animate-bv-fade fixed inset-0 z-40 block w-full overflow-hidden bg-[#0c1a17] text-left"
    >
      <img
        src={battleViewUrl(scene.to)}
        alt={`Aerial view of the ${ground.name} battlefield`}
        className="animate-bv-flyto absolute inset-0 h-full w-full object-cover"
      />
      <div
        aria-hidden
        className="absolute inset-0"
        style={{
          background:
            "linear-gradient(to bottom, hsl(20 40% 6% / 0.72) 0%, transparent 26%, transparent 55%, hsl(20 40% 6% / 0.85) 100%)",
        }}
      />

      <button
        type="button"
        aria-label="Dismiss battle view"
        onClick={dismiss}
        className="absolute right-4 top-4 z-10 rounded-full border border-[hsl(42_62%_66%/0.45)] bg-black/35 px-3 py-1 font-body text-xs uppercase tracking-widest text-[hsl(43_55%_84%)] backdrop-blur-sm transition hover:bg-black/55"
      >
        Skip
      </button>

      <div className="absolute inset-x-0 top-0 flex flex-col items-center pt-5">
        <p className="font-display text-[10px] uppercase tracking-imperial text-[hsl(40_34%_68%)]">
          The Battle for
        </p>
        <p className="text-gilded font-display text-2xl font-bold uppercase tracking-widest">
          {ground.name}
        </p>
        {scene.rounds > 1 && (
          <p className="mt-0.5 font-body text-xs italic text-[hsl(40_34%_68%)]">
            {scene.rounds} rounds of fighting
          </p>
        )}
      </div>

      {!rolled && (
        <div className="absolute inset-x-0 bottom-0 flex flex-col items-center gap-3 px-4 pb-8">
          <button
            type="button"
            onClick={rollDice}
            disabled={rolled}
            className="animate-bv-dice-prompt rounded-md border border-[hsl(42_62%_66%/0.65)] bg-[hsl(20_40%_8%/0.72)] px-6 py-3 font-display text-sm font-bold uppercase tracking-imperial text-[hsl(43_55%_84%)] shadow-[0_0_30px_hsl(20_40%_6%/0.75)] backdrop-blur-sm transition hover:scale-105 hover:bg-[hsl(20_40%_8%/0.88)]"
          >
            Press dice to roll
          </button>
          <p className="font-body text-[10px] italic text-[hsl(40_34%_68%)]">battle sounds begin on the roll</p>
        </div>
      )}

      {rolled && (
        <div className="animate-bv-results absolute inset-x-0 bottom-0 flex flex-col items-center gap-2 px-4 pb-7">
          <div className="flex items-end justify-center gap-5">
            <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-1.5">
              <p className="font-display text-[10px] uppercase tracking-widest" style={{ color: attacker.color }}>
                {attacker.name}
              </p>
              <div className="flex gap-1">
                {scene.attackerRolls.map((roll, i) => (
                  <RiskDie key={`a-${sceneKey}-${i}`} value={roll} tier={scene.attackerTier} delay={i * 120} />
                ))}
              </div>
            </div>
            <span className="pb-3 font-display text-xs uppercase tracking-imperial text-[hsl(40_34%_68%)]">vs</span>
            <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-1.5">
              <p className="font-display text-[10px] uppercase tracking-widest" style={{ color: defender.color }}>
                {defender.name}
              </p>
              <div className="flex gap-1">
                {scene.defenderRolls.map((roll, i) => (
                  <RiskDie key={`d-${sceneKey}-${i}`} value={roll} tier={scene.defenderTier} delay={i * 120 + 60} />
                ))}
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
          <p className="font-body text-sm text-[hsl(43_55%_84%)]">
            Losses — <span style={{ color: attacker.color }}>{attacker.name}</span>{" "}
            <span className="font-semibold text-[hsl(357_68%_62%)]">{scene.attackerLosses}</span>,{" "}
            <span style={{ color: defender.color }}>{defender.name}</span>{" "}
            <span className="font-semibold text-[hsl(357_68%_62%)]">{scene.defenderLosses}</span>
          </p>
          {scene.conquered && (
            <p className="animate-bv-banner text-gilded border-y border-[hsl(42_62%_66%/0.5)] px-6 py-1 font-display text-sm font-bold uppercase tracking-imperial">
              Territory Taken
            </p>
          )}
          <p className="font-body text-[10px] italic text-[hsl(40_34%_60%)]">skip to dismiss</p>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

import type { ReactNode } from "react";

import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";

/** Parchment game-board panel: double ink border with brass tacks in the corners. */
export function FieldPanel({ children, className }: { children: ReactNode; className?: string }) {
  return (
    <div
      className={cn(
        "parchment-sheet relative rounded-md border-2 border-border/80 bg-card p-4 shadow-[0_6px_20px_hsl(20_40%_6%/0.55),inset_0_1px_0_hsl(48_70%_94%/0.6)]",
        className,
      )}
    >
      <span
        aria-hidden
        className="pointer-events-none absolute inset-1 rounded-sm border border-border/40"
      />
      <Tack className="left-1.5 top-1.5" />
      <Tack className="right-1.5 top-1.5" />
      <Tack className="bottom-1.5 left-1.5" />
      <Tack className="bottom-1.5 right-1.5" />
      {children}
    </div>
  );
}

function Tack({ className }: { className: string }) {
  return (
    <span
      aria-hidden
      className={cn(
        "pointer-events-none absolute h-1.5 w-1.5 rounded-full bg-gradient-to-br from-[hsl(42_60%_60%)] to-[hsl(34_50%_30%)] shadow-[0_1px_1px_hsl(30_40%_15%/0.5)]",
        className,
      )}
    />
  );
}

const ROMAN = ["I", "II", "III", "IV", "V", "VI", "VII", "VIII", "IX", "X"];

/** Roman-numeral section header with letter tracking. */
export function SectionHeader({ index, title, className }: { index?: number; title: string; className?: string }) {
  return (
    <div className={cn("mb-2 flex items-center gap-2", className)}>
      {index !== undefined && (
        <span className="font-display text-[11px] font-bold text-gold">{ROMAN[index - 1] ?? index}.</span>
      )}
      <span className="font-display text-[11px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-imperial text-muted-foreground">
        {title}
      </span>
      <span className="imperial-divider flex-1" />
    </div>
  );
}

export function ImperialDivider({ className }: { className?: string }) {
  return (
    <div className={cn("flex items-center gap-2", className)}>
      <span className="imperial-divider flex-1" />
      <span aria-hidden className="h-1.5 w-1.5 rotate-45 bg-gold" />
      <span className="imperial-divider flex-1" />
    </div>
  );
}

File: /web/src/components/game/Fireworks.tsx

import { useEffect, useRef, useState } from "react";

/**
 * The original RISK II victory fireworks — 21 blue-keyed frames extracted from
 * the game's sprite archive, replayed as staggered bursts across the screen.
 */
const FRAME_COUNT = 21;
const FRAME_MS = 60;

const frameUrl = (i: number): string => `/risk/fireworks/f${String(i).padStart(2, "0")}.png`;

let preloaded = false;
function preloadFrames(): void {
  if (preloaded || typeof window === "undefined") return;
  preloaded = true;
  for (let i = 0; i < FRAME_COUNT; i += 1) {
    const img = new Image();
    img.src = frameUrl(i);
  }
}

interface BurstPose {
  left: number;
  top: number;
  size: number;
}

function Burst({ initialDelay }: { initialDelay: number }) {
  const [frame, setFrame] = useState<number>(-1);
  const [pose, setPose] = useState<BurstPose>(() => ({
    left: 4 + Math.random() * 66,
    top: 4 + Math.random() * 50,
    size: 34 + Math.random() * 26,
  }));
  const timerRef = useRef<number | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    let cancelled = false;

    const runBurst = () => {
      if (cancelled) return;
      setPose({
        left: 4 + Math.random() * 66,
        top: 4 + Math.random() * 50,
        size: 34 + Math.random() * 26,
      });
      let f = 0;
      setFrame(0);
      timerRef.current = window.setInterval(() => {
        f += 1;
        if (f >= FRAME_COUNT) {
          if (timerRef.current !== null) window.clearInterval(timerRef.current);
          setFrame(-1);
          timerRef.current = window.setTimeout(runBurst, 250 + Math.random() * 1100) as unknown as number;
        } else {
          setFrame(f);
        }
      }, FRAME_MS);
    };

    timerRef.current = window.setTimeout(runBurst, initialDelay) as unknown as number;
    return () => {
      cancelled = true;
      if (timerRef.current !== null) {
        window.clearInterval(timerRef.current);
        window.clearTimeout(timerRef.current);
      }
    };
  }, [initialDelay]);

  if (frame < 0) return null;
  return (
    <img
      src={frameUrl(frame)}
      alt=""
      aria-hidden
      draggable={false}
      className="absolute"
      style={{
        left: `${pose.left}%`,
        top: `${pose.top}%`,
        width: `${pose.size}%`,
        maxWidth: 340,
        imageRendering: "pixelated" as const,
        mixBlendMode: "screen" as const,
      }}
    />
  );
}

/** Full-screen celebratory layer; render behind overlay content. */
export function Fireworks({ bursts = 3 }: { bursts?: number }) {
  useEffect(() => {
    preloadFrames();
  }, []);
  return (
    <div aria-hidden className="pointer-events-none absolute inset-0 overflow-hidden">
      {Array.from({ length: bursts }, (_, i) => (
        <Burst key={i} initialDelay={i * 450} />
      ))}
    </div>
  );
}

import { useEffect, useMemo, useState } from "react";
import { useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";
import { Handshake, Shield, Skull, Swords } from "lucide-react";
import { Line, LineChart, ResponsiveContainer, Tooltip, XAxis, YAxis } from "recharts";

import { FieldPanel, ImperialDivider } from "@/components/game/FieldPanel";
import { Fireworks } from "@/components/game/Fireworks";
import { PieceIcon } from "@/components/game/PieceSprite";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { ART } from "@/lib/art";
import { Slider } from "@/components/ui/slider";
import { allianceBetween, grudgeLabel } from "@/game/analysis";
import { isValidSet, tradeValue, CARD_TYPE_LABEL } from "@/game/cards";
import { GENERALS } from "@/game/generals";
import { TERRITORY_MAP } from "@/game/mapData";
import { missionText } from "@/game/missions";
import type { AllianceLevel, GameAction, GameState, RiskCard } from "@/game/types";
import { ALLIANCE_LEVEL_INFO, CARD_RULE_INFO, OBJECTIVE_INFO } from "@/game/types";
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";

interface OverlayProps {
  game: GameState;
  dispatch: (action: GameAction) => void;
}

function OverlayShell({ children, backdrop }: { children: React.ReactNode; backdrop?: React.ReactNode }) {
  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 flex items-center justify-center bg-[#241708]/70 p-4 backdrop-blur-sm">
      {backdrop}
      <div className="relative w-full max-w-md animate-fade-up">{children}</div>
    </div>
  );
}

/** Hot-seat pass-the-device screen between human turns. */
export function HandoffOverlay({ game, dispatch }: OverlayProps) {
  const player = game.players[game.currentPlayer];
  if (!player || !game.awaitingHandoff) return null;
  return (
    <OverlayShell>
      <FieldPanel className="bg-card text-center">
        <p className="font-display text-[10px] uppercase tracking-imperial text-muted-foreground">
          Change of Command — Turn {game.turn}
        </p>
        <ImperialDivider className="my-3" />
        <PieceIcon
          type="cavalry"
          color={player.color}
          size={72}
          className="mx-auto mb-1 drop-shadow-[0_3px_3px_rgba(0,0,0,0.35)]"
        />
        <h2 className="font-display text-2xl font-bold text-foreground">{player.name}</h2>
        <p className="mt-1 font-body text-sm italic text-muted-foreground">
          Pass the device to the {player.colorName} commander. All others, avert your eyes.
        </p>
        {game.setup.objective === "mission" && player.mission && (
          <p className="mt-3 border border-gold-dim/50 bg-gold/10 p-2 font-body text-sm text-gold">
            Secret mission: {missionText(player.mission, game.players)}
          </p>
        )}
        <Button
          className="mt-4 w-full font-display uppercase tracking-imperial"
          onClick={() => dispatch({ type: "ACKNOWLEDGE_HANDOFF" })}
        >
          Take Command
        </Button>
      </FieldPanel>
    </OverlayShell>
  );
}

/** Occupation slider after a successful conquest (human attacker only). */
export function OccupyOverlay({ game, dispatch }: OverlayProps) {
  const pending = game.pendingOccupy;
  const [count, setCount] = useState<number>(pending?.max ?? 1);

  useEffect(() => {
    setCount(pending?.max ?? 1);
  }, [pending?.from, pending?.to, pending?.max]);

  const player = game.players[game.currentPlayer];
  if (!pending || !player?.isHuman) return null;

  return (
    <OverlayShell>
      <FieldPanel className="bg-card">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <Swords className="h-4 w-4 text-gold" />
          <h2 className="font-display text-sm font-bold uppercase tracking-imperial">Territory Taken</h2>
        </div>
        <p className="mt-2 font-body text-sm text-muted-foreground">
          {TERRITORY_MAP[pending.to].name} has fallen. March your armies forward from{" "}
          {TERRITORY_MAP[pending.from].name}.
        </p>
        <div className="mt-4 flex items-center gap-3">
          <Slider
            min={pending.min}
            max={pending.max}
            step={1}
            value={[count]}
            onValueChange={(value) => setCount(value[0] ?? pending.min)}
            disabled={pending.min === pending.max}
          />
          <span className="w-10 text-right font-display text-lg font-bold text-gold">{count}</span>
        </div>
        <Button
          className="mt-4 w-full font-display uppercase tracking-imperial"
          onClick={() => dispatch({ type: "OCCUPY", count })}
        >
          Occupy with {count} {count === 1 ? "army" : "armies"}
        </Button>
      </FieldPanel>
    </OverlayShell>
  );
}

/** Card trade dialog: shown when forced or opened manually during reinforcement. */
export function TradeOverlay({
  game,
  dispatch,
  open,
  onClose,
}: OverlayProps & { open: boolean; onClose: () => void }) {
  const player = game.players[game.currentPlayer];
  const [selected, setSelected] = useState<string[]>([]);

  useEffect(() => {
    setSelected([]);
  }, [game.currentPlayer, open]);

  const selectedCards = useMemo<RiskCard[]>(
    () => (player ? player.cards.filter((c) => selected.includes(c.id)) : []),
    [player, selected],
  );

  if (!player?.isHuman || !open) return null;
  const rule = game.setup.cardRule ?? "ascending";
  const valid = isValidSet(selectedCards);
  const bonus = valid ? tradeValue(selectedCards, rule, game.tradesCompleted) : 0;

  const toggle = (id: string) => {
    setSelected((prev) => (prev.includes(id) ? prev.filter((x) => x !== id) : prev.length < 3 ? [...prev, id] : prev));
  };

  return (
    <OverlayShell>
      <FieldPanel className="bg-card">
        <h2 className="font-display text-sm font-bold uppercase tracking-imperial">Card Exchange</h2>
        <p className="mt-1 font-body text-sm text-muted-foreground">
          {game.mustTrade
            ? "You hold five or more cards — a trade is required before mustering."
            : "Trade three matching or three different cards. A wild counts as any regiment."}
        </p>
        <p className="mt-1 font-body text-xs italic text-gold/80">
          {CARD_RULE_INFO[rule].name}: {CARD_RULE_INFO[rule].description}
        </p>
        <div className="mt-3 grid grid-cols-3 gap-2">
          {player.cards.map((card) => (
            <button
              key={card.id}
              type="button"
              onClick={() => toggle(card.id)}
              className={cn(
                "border p-2 text-left transition-colors",
                selected.includes(card.id) ? "border-gold bg-gold/15" : "border-gold-dim/50 bg-background/40",
              )}
            >
              {card.type === "wild" ? (
                <span aria-hidden className="block h-9 text-center text-2xl leading-9 text-gold">
                  ★
                </span>
              ) : (
                <PieceIcon type={card.type} size={36} color="#7a5a2e" className="mx-auto block" />
              )}
              <p className="text-center font-display text-[10px] font-bold uppercase tracking-wider text-gold">
                {CARD_TYPE_LABEL[card.type]}
              </p>
              <p className="mt-0.5 truncate text-center font-body text-xs text-muted-foreground">
                {card.territory ? TERRITORY_MAP[card.territory].name : "Any regiment"}
              </p>
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>
        <div className="mt-4 flex gap-2">
          <Button
            className="flex-1 font-display uppercase tracking-imperial"
            disabled={!valid || bonus <= 0}
            onClick={() => {
              dispatch({ type: "TRADE_CARDS", cardIds: selected });
              setSelected([]);
              if (!game.mustTrade) onClose();
            }}
          >
            {valid && bonus > 0 ? `Trade for ${bonus} armies` : "Select a set of three"}
          </Button>
          {!game.mustTrade && (
            <Button variant="outline" className="font-display uppercase tracking-imperial" onClick={onClose}>
              Close
            </Button>
          )}
        </div>
      </FieldPanel>
    </OverlayShell>
  );
}

const ALLIANCE_LEVELS: AllianceLevel[] = [1, 2, 3];

/** I-Com panel — threats and alliance proposals to the AI generals (manual, Chapter 9). */
export function DiplomacyOverlay({
  game,
  dispatch,
  open,
  onClose,
}: OverlayProps & { open: boolean; onClose: () => void }) {
  const player = game.players[game.currentPlayer];
  if (!open || !player?.isHuman || game.phase !== "reinforcement") return null;
  const rivals = game.players.filter((p) => !p.isHuman && p.alive);
  return (
    <OverlayShell>
      <FieldPanel className="bg-card">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <Handshake className="h-4 w-4 text-gold" />
          <h2 className="font-display text-sm font-bold uppercase tracking-imperial">I-Com — Diplomacy</h2>
        </div>
        <p className="mt-1 font-body text-xs text-muted-foreground">
          One dispatch per general per turn. Pacts lapse at the end of the next round — break one and they will
          remember.
        </p>
        <ul className="mt-3 max-h-80 space-y-2 overflow-y-auto pr-1">
          {rivals.map((rival) => {
            const general = rival.generalId ? GENERALS[rival.generalId] : null;
            const alliance = allianceBetween(game, player.id, rival.id);
            const messaged = game.proposalsMade.includes(rival.id);
            const attitude = grudgeLabel(rival.grudges[player.id] ?? 0);
            return (
              <li key={rival.id} className="border border-gold-dim/40 bg-background/40 p-2">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                  <span
                    aria-hidden
                    className="h-3 w-3 rounded-full border border-[#3a2812]"
                    style={{ backgroundColor: rival.color }}
                  />
                  <span className="flex-1 truncate font-body text-sm font-semibold">Gen. {rival.name}</span>
                  <span
                    className={cn(
                      "font-display text-[9px] uppercase tracking-widest",
                      attitude.hostile ? "text-crimson-bright" : "text-muted-foreground",
                    )}
                  >
                    {attitude.label}
                  </span>
                </div>
                {general && <p className="mt-0.5 font-body text-[11px] italic text-muted-foreground">{general.description}</p>}
                {alliance ? (
                  <p className="mt-1.5 border border-gold-dim/50 bg-gold/10 px-2 py-1 font-body text-xs text-gold">
                    {ALLIANCE_LEVEL_INFO[alliance.level].name} — lapses after round {alliance.expiresOnRound}
                  </p>
                ) : messaged ? (
                  <p className="mt-1.5 font-body text-xs italic text-muted-foreground">Dispatch already sent this turn.</p>
                ) : (
                  <div className="mt-1.5 flex flex-wrap gap-1">
                    <button
                      type="button"
                      title="Send a threat — no reply expected, and no goodwill earned"
                      onClick={() => dispatch({ type: "SEND_THREAT", target: rival.id })}
                      className="flex items-center gap-1 border border-crimson-bright/60 px-2 py-0.5 font-display text-[10px] uppercase tracking-widest text-crimson-bright transition-colors hover:bg-crimson-bright/10"
                    >
                      <Skull className="h-3 w-3" /> Threat
                    </button>
                    {ALLIANCE_LEVELS.map((level) => (
                      <button
                        key={level}
                        type="button"
                        title={ALLIANCE_LEVEL_INFO[level].description}
                        onClick={() => dispatch({ type: "PROPOSE_ALLIANCE", target: rival.id, level })}
                        className="border border-gold-dim/50 px-2 py-0.5 font-display text-[10px] uppercase tracking-widest text-gold transition-colors hover:bg-gold/10"
                      >
                        Pact {"I".repeat(level)}
                      </button>
                    ))}
                  </div>
                )}
              </li>
            );
          })}
        </ul>
        {game.log[0] && (
          <p className="mt-2 font-body text-xs italic text-muted-foreground" aria-live="polite">
            Latest dispatch: {game.log[0].text}
          </p>
        )}
        <Button variant="outline" className="mt-3 w-full font-display uppercase tracking-imperial" onClick={onClose}>
          Close the Ledger
        </Button>
      </FieldPanel>
    </OverlayShell>
  );
}

/** An AI general's alliance offer awaiting the human commander's answer. */
export function ProposalOverlay({ game, dispatch }: OverlayProps) {
  const proposal = game.pendingProposal;
  if (!proposal) return null;
  const from = game.players[proposal.from];
  const to = game.players[proposal.to];
  if (!from || !to?.isHuman) return null;
  return (
    <OverlayShell>
      <FieldPanel className="bg-card text-center">
        <Handshake className="mx-auto h-8 w-8 text-gold" />
        <p className="mt-2 font-display text-[10px] uppercase tracking-imperial text-muted-foreground">
          A dispatch arrives under a white flag
        </p>
        <ImperialDivider className="my-3" />
        <h2 className="font-display text-xl font-bold">Gen. {from.name} proposes a {ALLIANCE_LEVEL_INFO[proposal.level].name}</h2>
        <p className="mt-2 font-body text-sm italic text-muted-foreground">
          {ALLIANCE_LEVEL_INFO[proposal.level].description} The pact would last through the next round.
        </p>
        <div className="mt-4 flex gap-2">
          <Button
            className="flex-1 font-display uppercase tracking-imperial"
            onClick={() => dispatch({ type: "RESPOND_PROPOSAL", accept: true })}
          >
            Accept the Pact
          </Button>
          <Button
            variant="outline"
            className="flex-1 font-display uppercase tracking-imperial"
            onClick={() => dispatch({ type: "RESPOND_PROPOSAL", accept: false })}
          >
            Refuse
          </Button>
        </div>
      </FieldPanel>
    </OverlayShell>
  );
}

/** Turn-by-turn territory chart shown with the victory proclamation. */
function CampaignChart({ game }: { game: GameState }) {
  const data = useMemo(
    () =>
      game.history.map((snapshot) => {
        const row: Record<string, number> = { turn: snapshot.turn };
        snapshot.counts.forEach((count, i) => {
          row[`p${i}`] = count.territories;
        });
        return row;
      }),
    [game.history],
  );
  if (data.length < 2) return null;
  return (
    <div className="mt-4 text-left">
      <p className="font-display text-[10px] uppercase tracking-imperial text-muted-foreground">
        Territories held, round by round
      </p>
      <div className="mt-1 h-44 w-full">
        <ResponsiveContainer width="100%" height="100%">
          <LineChart data={data} margin={{ top: 6, right: 8, bottom: 0, left: -22 }}>
            <XAxis dataKey="turn" tick={{ fontSize: 10 }} stroke="#8a6a3c" />
            <YAxis tick={{ fontSize: 10 }} stroke="#8a6a3c" allowDecimals={false} />
            <Tooltip
              formatter={(value: number, key: string) => [value, game.players[Number(key.slice(1))]?.name ?? key]}
              labelFormatter={(turn) => `Round ${turn}`}
              contentStyle={{ background: "hsl(46 62% 92%)", border: "1px solid #7a5a2e", fontFamily: "Alegreya, serif", fontSize: 12 }}
            />
            {game.players.map((p) => (
              <Line key={p.id} type="monotone" dataKey={`p${p.id}`} stroke={p.color} strokeWidth={2} dot={false} isAnimationActive={false} />
            ))}
          </LineChart>
        </ResponsiveContainer>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

/** Victory proclamation. */
export function VictoryOverlay({ game, onExit }: { game: GameState; onExit: () => void }) {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  if (game.phase !== "gameOver" || game.winner === null) return null;
  const winner = game.players[game.winner];
  if (!winner) return null;
  return (
    <OverlayShell backdrop={winner.isHuman ? <Fireworks /> : undefined}>
      <FieldPanel className="bg-card text-center">
        <div className="relative mx-auto flex h-24 w-24 items-center justify-center">
          <img
            src={ART.laurelWreath}
            alt=""
            aria-hidden
            className="absolute inset-0 h-full w-full object-contain drop-shadow-[0_2px_4px_rgba(0,0,0,0.35)]"
          />
          <Shield className="h-7 w-7 text-gold" />
        </div>
        <p className="mt-2 font-display text-[10px] uppercase tracking-imperial text-muted-foreground">
          {OBJECTIVE_INFO[game.setup.objective].name} — Turn {game.turn}
        </p>
        <ImperialDivider className="my-3" />
        <h2 className="font-display text-3xl font-black text-gold">{winner.name}</h2>
        <p className="mt-2 font-body text-base italic text-foreground">
          Victory by {game.winReason ?? "conquest"}. The world bows to the {winner.colorName} banner.
        </p>
        <CampaignChart game={game} />
        <div className="mt-5 flex gap-2">
          <Button
            className="flex-1 font-display uppercase tracking-imperial"
            onClick={() => {
              onExit();
              navigate("/setup");
            }}
          >
            New Campaign
          </Button>
          <Button
            variant="outline"
            className="flex-1 font-display uppercase tracking-imperial"
            onClick={() => {
              onExit();
              navigate("/");
            }}
          >
            Main Hall
          </Button>
        </div>
      </FieldPanel>
    </OverlayShell>
  );
}
