File: /web/src/components/game/MapViewport.tsx
---

import { useCallback, useEffect, useLayoutEffect, useMemo, useRef, useState, type ReactNode } from "react";
import { Crosshair, Expand, Minus, Plus } from "lucide-react";

import {
  autoMinVw,
  cameraForAttention,
  clampCamera,
  fitVw,
  fullCamera,
  MANUAL_MIN_VW,
  MAP_H,
  MAP_W,
  viewBoxFor,
  type AttentionPoint,
  type Camera,
} from "@/game/camera";
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";

const DRAG_THRESHOLD_PX = 7;
const DOUBLE_TAP_MS = 320;
const DOUBLE_TAP_RADIUS_PX = 36;
const BUTTON_ZOOM_STEP = 1.45;
const DOUBLE_TAP_ZOOM = 2.4;

interface MapViewportProps {
  /** Weighted points of interest from the attention director. */
  attention: AttentionPoint[];
  /**
   * Scene signature (phase / turn). When it changes the director re-takes
   * the camera, even if the commander had grabbed manual control.
   */
  autoKey: string;
  className?: string;
  children: ReactNode;
}

/**
 * Animated attention camera for the world board. The SVG fills the whole
 * container and the viewBox is computed at the container's LIVE aspect
 * ratio, so the frame adapts to portrait and landscape phones with no
 * letterboxing. In auto mode the camera glides to the attention solver's
 * frame; drag, pinch, wheel or double-tap hands control to the commander;
 * each new scene (turn/phase) hands it back to the director. The viewBox is
 * driven imperatively per animation frame so React never re-renders the
 * board during motion.
 */
export function MapViewport({ attention, autoKey, className, children }: MapViewportProps) {
  const containerRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement | null>(null);
  const svgRef = useRef<SVGSVGElement | null>(null);
  const cameraRef = useRef<Camera>(fullCamera(MAP_W / MAP_H));
  const targetRef = useRef<Camera>(fullCamera(MAP_W / MAP_H));
  const aspectRef = useRef<number>(MAP_W / MAP_H);
  const rafRef = useRef<number>(0);
  const animatingRef = useRef<boolean>(false);
  const pointersRef = useRef<Map<number, { x: number; y: number }>>(new Map());
  const pinchDistRef = useRef<number | null>(null);
  const movedRef = useRef<number>(0);
  const suppressClickRef = useRef<boolean>(false);
  const lastTapRef = useRef<{ time: number; x: number; y: number } | null>(null);
  const prevAutoKeyRef = useRef<string>(autoKey);
  const [auto, setAuto] = useState<boolean>(true);
  const [size, setSize] = useState<{ w: number; h: number }>({ w: 0, h: 0 });

  const aspect = size.h > 0 ? size.w / size.h : MAP_W / MAP_H;

  const applyCamera = useCallback(() => {
    const svg = svgRef.current;
    if (!svg) return;
    svg.setAttribute("viewBox", viewBoxFor(cameraRef.current, aspectRef.current));
    const container = containerRef.current;
    if (container) {
      const canPan = cameraRef.current.vw < fitVw(aspectRef.current) - 1;
      container.style.cursor = canPan ? "grab" : "default";
    }
  }, []);

  const ensureLoop = useCallback(() => {
    if (animatingRef.current) return;
    animatingRef.current = true;
    let last = performance.now();
    const step = (now: number) => {
      const dt = Math.min(0.05, Math.max(0.001, (now - last) / 1000));
      last = now;
      const cam = cameraRef.current;
      const tgt = targetRef.current;
      const k = 1 - Math.exp(-7.5 * dt);
      cam.cx += (tgt.cx - cam.cx) * k;
      cam.cy += (tgt.cy - cam.cy) * k;
      cam.vw += (tgt.vw - cam.vw) * k;
      applyCamera();
      const settled =
        Math.abs(tgt.cx - cam.cx) < 0.4 && Math.abs(tgt.cy - cam.cy) < 0.4 && Math.abs(tgt.vw - cam.vw) < 0.5;
      if (settled) {
        cameraRef.current = { ...tgt };
        applyCamera();
        animatingRef.current = false;
        return;
      }
      rafRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(step);
    };
    rafRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(step);
  }, [applyCamera]);

  // Track the container's live size (orientation changes, keyboard, resizes).
  useLayoutEffect(() => {
    const container = containerRef.current;
    if (!container) return;
    svgRef.current = container.querySelector("svg");
    const measure = () => {
      const rect = container.getBoundingClientRect();
      setSize((prev) =>
        Math.abs(prev.w - rect.width) < 1 && Math.abs(prev.h - rect.height) < 1
          ? prev
          : { w: rect.width, h: rect.height },
      );
    };
    measure();
    const observer = new ResizeObserver(measure);
    observer.observe(container);
    return () => {
      observer.disconnect();
      cancelAnimationFrame(rafRef.current);
      animatingRef.current = false;
    };
  }, []);

  // Re-legalize the camera whenever the viewport aspect changes (rotation).
  useLayoutEffect(() => {
    aspectRef.current = aspect;
    cameraRef.current = clampCamera(cameraRef.current, aspect, 1);
    targetRef.current = clampCamera(targetRef.current, aspect, 1);
    applyCamera();
  }, [aspect, applyCamera]);

  // Each new scene (turn / phase change) hands the camera back to the director.
  useEffect(() => {
    if (prevAutoKeyRef.current !== autoKey) {
      prevAutoKeyRef.current = autoKey;
      setAuto(true);
    }
  }, [autoKey]);

  // The attention solver's frame for the current scene, at the live aspect.
  const autoTarget = useMemo(
    () => cameraForAttention(attention, aspect, autoMinVw(size.w)),
    [attention, aspect, size.w],
  );

  // Follow the director whenever its framing changes.
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!auto || size.w === 0) return;
    targetRef.current = clampCamera(autoTarget, aspectRef.current, 1);
    ensureLoop();
  }, [auto, autoTarget, size.w, ensureLoop]);

  /** Convert a client-space point to map units under the current camera. */
  const toMapPoint = useCallback((clientX: number, clientY: number) => {
    const rect = containerRef.current?.getBoundingClientRect();
    const cam = cameraRef.current;
    if (!rect || rect.width === 0 || rect.height === 0) return { x: cam.cx, y: cam.cy };
    const vh = cam.vw / aspectRef.current;
    return {
      x: cam.cx - cam.vw / 2 + ((clientX - rect.left) / rect.width) * cam.vw,
      y: cam.cy - vh / 2 + ((clientY - rect.top) / rect.height) * vh,
    };
  }, []);

  /** Zoom by a factor (>1 zooms in) keeping the given map point fixed on screen. */
  const zoomAt = useCallback(
    (px: number, py: number, factor: number, animate: boolean) => {
      const cam = cameraRef.current;
      const aspectNow = aspectRef.current;
      const vw = Math.min(fitVw(aspectNow), Math.max(MANUAL_MIN_VW, cam.vw / factor));
      const ratio = vw / cam.vw;
      const next = clampCamera(
        { vw, cx: px - (px - cam.cx) * ratio, cy: py - (py - cam.cy) * ratio },
        aspectNow,
      );
      if (animate) {
        targetRef.current = next;
        ensureLoop();
      } else {
        cameraRef.current = next;
        targetRef.current = { ...next };
        applyCamera();
      }
    },
    [applyCamera, ensureLoop],
  );

  // Wheel zoom (non-passive so we can prevent page scroll) and click
  // suppression after drags/pinches, both attached natively.
  useEffect(() => {
    const container = containerRef.current;
    if (!container) return;
    const onClickCapture = (e: MouseEvent) => {
      if (suppressClickRef.current) {
        suppressClickRef.current = false;
        e.stopPropagation();
        e.preventDefault();
      }
    };
    const onWheel = (e: WheelEvent) => {
      e.preventDefault();
      setAuto(false);
      const p = toMapPoint(e.clientX, e.clientY);
      zoomAt(p.x, p.y, Math.exp(-e.deltaY * 0.0016), false);
    };
    container.addEventListener("click", onClickCapture, true);
    container.addEventListener("wheel", onWheel, { passive: false });
    return () => {
      container.removeEventListener("click", onClickCapture, true);
      container.removeEventListener("wheel", onWheel);
    };
  }, [toMapPoint, zoomAt]);

  const handlePointerDown = (e: React.PointerEvent<HTMLDivElement>) => {
    pointersRef.current.set(e.pointerId, { x: e.clientX, y: e.clientY });
    if (pointersRef.current.size === 1) movedRef.current = 0;
    if (pointersRef.current.size === 2) {
      const pts = [...pointersRef.current.values()];
      const a = pts[0];
      const b = pts[1];
      if (a && b) pinchDistRef.current = Math.hypot(a.x - b.x, a.y - b.y);
      containerRef.current?.setPointerCapture(e.pointerId);
      // Freeze any in-flight auto glide while the commander grabs the map.
      targetRef.current = { ...cameraRef.current };
      setAuto(false);
    }
  };

  const handlePointerMove = (e: React.PointerEvent<HTMLDivElement>) => {
    const prev = pointersRef.current.get(e.pointerId);
    if (!prev) return;
    const curr = { x: e.clientX, y: e.clientY };
    pointersRef.current.set(e.pointerId, curr);
    const rect = containerRef.current?.getBoundingClientRect();
    if (!rect || rect.width === 0 || rect.height === 0) return;

    // Two-finger pinch.
    if (pointersRef.current.size >= 2 && pinchDistRef.current !== null) {
      const pts = [...pointersRef.current.values()];
      const a = pts[0];
      const b = pts[1];
      if (!a || !b) return;
      const dist = Math.hypot(a.x - b.x, a.y - b.y);
      if (dist > 0 && pinchDistRef.current > 0) {
        const mid = toMapPoint((a.x + b.x) / 2, (a.y + b.y) / 2);
        zoomAt(mid.x, mid.y, dist / pinchDistRef.current, false);
      }
      pinchDistRef.current = dist;
      movedRef.current = DRAG_THRESHOLD_PX * 4;
      suppressClickRef.current = true;
      return;
    }

    // Single-pointer pan (only meaningful when zoomed past the fit view).
    const dx = curr.x - prev.x;
    const dy = curr.y - prev.y;
    movedRef.current += Math.abs(dx) + Math.abs(dy);
    if (movedRef.current < DRAG_THRESHOLD_PX) return;
    const cam = cameraRef.current;
    if (cam.vw >= fitVw(aspectRef.current) - 1) return;
    suppressClickRef.current = true;
    setAuto(false);
    const container = containerRef.current;
    if (container && !container.hasPointerCapture(e.pointerId)) {
      container.setPointerCapture(e.pointerId);
    }
    const vh = cam.vw / aspectRef.current;
    const next = clampCamera(
      {
        vw: cam.vw,
        cx: cam.cx - dx * (cam.vw / rect.width),
        cy: cam.cy - dy * (vh / rect.height),
      },
      aspectRef.current,
    );
    cameraRef.current = next;
    targetRef.current = { ...next };
    applyCamera();
  };

  const handlePointerUp = (e: React.PointerEvent<HTMLDivElement>) => {
    pointersRef.current.delete(e.pointerId);
    if (pointersRef.current.size < 2) pinchDistRef.current = null;
    applyCamera();

    // Double-tap (touch): zoom in on the spot, or hand back to the director.
    if (e.pointerType === "touch" && movedRef.current < DRAG_THRESHOLD_PX && pointersRef.current.size === 0) {
      const now = performance.now();
      const lastTap = lastTapRef.current;
      if (
        lastTap &&
        now - lastTap.time < DOUBLE_TAP_MS &&
        Math.hypot(e.clientX - lastTap.x, e.clientY - lastTap.y) < DOUBLE_TAP_RADIUS_PX
      ) {
        lastTapRef.current = null;
        suppressClickRef.current = true;
        if (cameraRef.current.vw < fitVw(aspectRef.current) * 0.6) {
          setAuto(true);
          targetRef.current = clampCamera(autoTarget, aspectRef.current, 1);
          ensureLoop();
        } else {
          setAuto(false);
          const p = toMapPoint(e.clientX, e.clientY);
          zoomAt(p.x, p.y, DOUBLE_TAP_ZOOM, true);
        }
      } else {
        lastTapRef.current = { time: now, x: e.clientX, y: e.clientY };
      }
    }
  };

  const engageAuto = () => {
    setAuto(true);
    targetRef.current = clampCamera(autoTarget, aspectRef.current, 1);
    ensureLoop();
  };

  const showFull = () => {
    setAuto(false);
    targetRef.current = fullCamera(aspectRef.current);
    ensureLoop();
  };

  const nudgeZoom = (factor: number) => {
    setAuto(false);
    const cam = cameraRef.current;
    zoomAt(cam.cx, cam.cy, factor, true);
  };

  return (
    <div
      ref={containerRef}
      className={cn("relative touch-none overflow-hidden", className)}
      onPointerDown={handlePointerDown}
      onPointerMove={handlePointerMove}
      onPointerUp={handlePointerUp}
      onPointerCancel={handlePointerUp}
    >
      {children}
      <div
        className="absolute bottom-2 right-2 z-20 flex flex-col gap-1"
        onPointerDown={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
        role="group"
        aria-label="Map camera controls"
      >
        <ViewportButton active={auto} label="Auto view — frame the action" onClick={engageAuto}>
          <Crosshair className="h-4 w-4" />
        </ViewportButton>
        <ViewportButton label="Zoom in" onClick={() => nudgeZoom(BUTTON_ZOOM_STEP)}>
          <Plus className="h-4 w-4" />
        </ViewportButton>
        <ViewportButton label="Zoom out" onClick={() => nudgeZoom(1 / BUTTON_ZOOM_STEP)}>
          <Minus className="h-4 w-4" />
        </ViewportButton>
        <ViewportButton label="Full board" onClick={showFull}>
          <Expand className="h-4 w-4" />
        </ViewportButton>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

function ViewportButton({
  active,
  label,
  onClick,
  children,
}: {
  active?: boolean;
  label: string;
  onClick: () => void;
  children: ReactNode;
}) {
  return (
    <button
      type="button"
      aria-label={label}
      title={label}
      aria-pressed={active}
      onClick={onClick}
      className={cn(
        "flex h-9 w-9 items-center justify-center rounded-sm border shadow-md backdrop-blur-[2px] transition-colors",
        active
          ? "border-gold bg-gold/25 text-gold"
          : "border-gold-dim/50 bg-[hsl(28_35%_12%/0.72)] text-[hsl(45_60%_80%)] hover:border-gold hover:text-gold",
      )}
    >
      {children}
    </button>
  );
}

import { Check, Crown, RotateCcw, X } from "lucide-react";

import { FieldPanel, ImperialDivider } from "@/components/game/FieldPanel";

const BENEFITS = [

/** Full-screen premium paywall — the Imperial Commission. */
export function PaywallOverlay() {

    usePremium();

        >
          <X className="h-4 w-4" />

          src={ART.laurelWreath}

          The Imperial <span className="text-gilded-crimson">Commission</span>
        </h2>

          A single field promotion unlocks the full theatre of war.
        </p>

        <ImperialDivider className="mx-auto my-4 max-w-[220px]" />

        <ul className="mx-auto max-w-xs space-y-2 text-left">
          {BENEFITS.map((benefit) => (
            <li key={benefit} className="flex items-start gap-2 font-body text-sm leading-snug">
              <Check className="mt-0.5 h-3.5 w-3.5 shrink-0 text-gold" aria-hidden />
              <span>{benefit}</span>
            </li>
          ))}
        </ul>

        <Button
          size="lg"
          className="mt-5 h-12 w-full gap-2 font-display text-sm font-bold uppercase tracking-imperial"
          onClick={purchase}
          disabled={purchasePending}
        >
          <Crown className="h-4 w-4" />
          {purchasePending ? "Opening the treasury..." : `Unlock Premium — ${priceLabel}`}
        </Button>
        <p className="mt-1.5 font-body text-[11px] italic text-muted-foreground">
          One-time purchase. No recurring dues.
        </p>

        <button
          type="button"
          onClick={restore}
          disabled={restorePending}
          className="mx-auto mt-3 flex items-center gap-1.5 font-display text-[11px] uppercase tracking-imperial text-muted-foreground transition-colors hover:text-gold disabled:opacity-50"
        >
          <RotateCcw className="h-3 w-3" />
          {restorePending ? "Consulting the ledger..." : "Restore Purchases"}
        </button>
      </FieldPanel>
    </div>
  );
}

File: /web/src/components/game/PieceSprite.tsx

import { memo } from "react";

import { PIECE_ART } from "@/lib/art";
import type { PieceType } from "@/game/pieces";

/**
 * The piece PNGs are white plastic with gray shading, so a channel-multiply
 * color matrix turns them into any player color while keeping the molded detail.
 */
function tintFilterId(color: string): string {
  return `piece-tint-${color.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g, "")}`;
}

function hexChannels(hex: string): { r: number; g: number; b: number } {
  const clean = hex.replace("#", "");
  const full = clean.length === 3 ? clean.split("").map((c) => c + c).join("") : clean;
  const value = Number.parseInt(full, 16);
  if (Number.isNaN(value)) return { r: 0.5, g: 0.5, b: 0.5 };
  return {
    r: ((value >> 16) & 0xff) / 255,
    g: ((value >> 8) & 0xff) / 255,
    b: (value & 0xff) / 255,
  };
}

/** One SVG tint filter per color — place inside <defs> of the host SVG. */
export function PieceTintFilter({ color }: { color: string }) {
  const { r, g, b } = hexChannels(color);
  return (
    <filter id={tintFilterId(color)} x="-10%" y="-10%" width="120%" height="120%" colorInterpolationFilters="sRGB">
      <feColorMatrix
        type="matrix"
        values={`${r.toFixed(3)} 0 0 0 0  0 ${g.toFixed(3)} 0 0 0  0 0 ${b.toFixed(3)} 0 0  0 0 0 1 0`}
      />
    </filter>
  );
}

/** On-board footprint of each piece, preserving the source art aspect ratio (px in map space). */
export const MAP_PIECE_BOX: Record<PieceType, { width: number; height: number }> = {
  infantry: { width: 18, height: 31 },
  cavalry: { width: 38, height: 40 },
  artillery: { width: 42, height: 22 },
};

/**
 * A playing piece standing on the map. Bottom-anchored at (cx, baseY) so all
 * three piece heights sit on the same base ellipse.
 */
export const MapPiece = memo(function MapPiece({
  type,
  color,
  cx,
  baseY,
  scale = 1,
}: {
  type: PieceType;
  color: string;
  cx: number;
  baseY: number;
  scale?: number;
}) {
  const box = MAP_PIECE_BOX[type];
  const width = box.width * scale;
  const height = box.height * scale;
  return (
    <image
      href={PIECE_ART[type]}
      x={cx - width / 2}
      y={baseY - height}
      width={width}
      height={height}
      filter={`url(#${tintFilterId(color)})`}
      pointerEvents="none"
      aria-hidden
    />
  );
});

/**
 * Standalone tinted piece for HTML contexts (cards, legends, overlays).
 * Each instance carries its own filter def; duplicate ids across instances
 * resolve to identical content, so rendering stays correct.
 */
export const PieceIcon = memo(function PieceIcon({
  type,
  color = "#6b4a26",
  size = 28,
  className,
}: {
  type: PieceType;
  color?: string;
  size?: number;
  className?: string;
}) {
  return (
    <svg width={size} height={size} viewBox="0 0 100 100" className={className} aria-hidden focusable="false">
      <defs>
        <PieceTintFilter color={color} />
      </defs>
      <image href={PIECE_ART[type]} x={0} y={0} width={100} height={100} filter={`url(#${tintFilterId(color)})`} />
    </svg>
  );
});

import { Bot, Crown, Handshake, Skull, User } from "lucide-react";

import { FieldPanel, SectionHeader } from "@/components/game/FieldPanel";
import { GENERALS } from "@/game/generals";
import type { GameState } from "@/game/types";
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";

/** "Field Commanders" roster panel. */
export function PlayerRoster({ game }: { game: GameState }) {
  return (
    <FieldPanel>
      <SectionHeader index={1} title="Field Commanders" />
      <ul className="space-y-1.5">
        {game.players.map((player) => {
          const owned = game.activeIds.filter((id) => game.territories[id].owner === player.id);
          const armies = owned.reduce((sum, id) => sum + game.territories[id].armies, 0);
          const isCurrent = game.currentPlayer === player.id && game.phase !== "gameOver";
          const general = player.generalId ? GENERALS[player.generalId] : null;
          const alliance = game.alliances.find(
            (a) =>
              (a.a === player.id && game.players[a.b]?.isHuman) ||
              (a.b === player.id && game.players[a.a]?.isHuman),
          );
          return (
            <li
              key={player.id}
              className={cn(
                "flex items-center gap-2 border border-transparent px-2 py-1.5 transition-colors",
                isCurrent && "rounded border-gold-dim/70 bg-gold/10",
                !player.alive && "opacity-45",
              )}
            >
              <span
                aria-hidden
                className="h-3.5 w-3.5 shrink-0 rounded-full border border-[#3a2812] shadow-[inset_-1px_-1px_1px_rgba(0,0,0,0.3),inset_1px_1px_1px_rgba(255,255,255,0.4)]"
                style={{ backgroundColor: player.color }}
              />
              <span className="min-w-0 flex-1 truncate font-body text-sm font-semibold">
                {player.name}
                {general && <span className="ml-1 text-xs font-normal text-muted-foreground">({general.name})</span>}
              </span>
              {player.alive && !player.isHuman && alliance && (
                <Handshake
                  className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-gold"
                  aria-label={`Allied (Level ${alliance.level})`}
                />
              )}
              {!player.alive ? (
                <Skull className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-crimson-bright" aria-label="Destroyed" />
              ) : player.isHuman ? (
                <User className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-muted-foreground" aria-label="Human" />
              ) : (
                <Bot className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-muted-foreground" aria-label="AI general" />
              )}
              {isCurrent && <Crown className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-gold" aria-label="Current turn" />}
              <span className="w-16 text-right font-display text-[11px] text-muted-foreground">
                {owned.length} ter · {armies}
              </span>
            </li>
          );
        })}
      </ul>
    </FieldPanel>
  );
}

File: /web/src/components/game/RiskDie.tsx

import type { DiceTier } from "@/game/types";

/**
 * Authentic RISK II die face — the original 22×22 sprites (red attacker die,
 * gold defender die) upscaled with hard pixels. Tier escalation is expressed
 * by recolouring the base sprites with CSS filters so the tiered D12 system
 * keeps its colour language.
 */
const TIER_SPRITE: Record<DiceTier, { sprite: "red" | "gold"; filter?: string }> = {
  white: { sprite: "red", filter: "grayscale(1) brightness(2.1)" },
  yellow: { sprite: "gold" },
  green: { sprite: "red", filter: "hue-rotate(115deg) brightness(0.95)" },
  red: { sprite: "red" },
  black: { sprite: "red", filter: "brightness(0.45) saturate(0.6)" },
};

export function RiskDie({ value, tier, delay = 0 }: { value: number; tier: DiceTier; delay?: number }) {
  const face = Math.min(6, Math.max(1, Math.round(value)));
  const { sprite, filter } = TIER_SPRITE[tier];
  return (
    <img
      src={`/risk/dice/${sprite}_${face}.png`}
      alt={`${tier} die showing ${face}`}
      width={36}
      height={36}
      className="h-9 w-9 animate-die-roll drop-shadow-md"
      style={{ imageRendering: "pixelated" as const, filter, animationDelay: `${delay}ms` }}
      draggable={false}
    />
  );
}

File: /web/src/components/game/TopBar.tsx

import { Coins, DoorOpen, Flag, Handshake, Layers, Swords, Volume2, VolumeX } from "lucide-react";
import { useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";

import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { toggleSfxMuted, useSfxMuted } from "@/lib/sfx";
import { missionText } from "@/game/missions";
import type { GameAction, GamePhase, GameState } from "@/game/types";
import { OBJECTIVE_INFO } from "@/game/types";
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";

const PHASES: { phase: GamePhase; roman: string; label: string; short: string }[] = [
  { phase: "reinforcement", roman: "I", label: "Muster", short: "DEP" },
  { phase: "attack", roman: "II", label: "Engagement", short: "ENG" },
  { phase: "fortify", roman: "III", label: "Manoeuvre", short: "MAN" },
];

interface TopBarProps {
  game: GameState;
  dispatch: (action: GameAction) => void;
  deployAmount: number;
  onDeployAmountChange: (amount: number) => void;
  onOpenCards: () => void;
  onOpenDiplomacy: () => void;
  allOut: boolean;
  onAllOutChange: (value: boolean) => void;
}

const SETUP_PHASE_LABEL: Partial<Record<GamePhase, string>> = {
  territoryGrab: "Territory Grab",
  election: "Election",
  initialDeploy: "Initial Muster",
  chooseCapital: "Choose Capital",
};

/** Commander's desk HUD strip. */
export function TopBar({ game, dispatch, deployAmount, onDeployAmountChange, onOpenCards, onOpenDiplomacy, allOut, onAllOutChange }: TopBarProps) {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const sfxMuted = useSfxMuted();
  const player = game.players[game.currentPlayer];
  if (!player) return null;
  const isHumanTurn = player.isHuman && !game.awaitingHandoff;
  const setupLabel = SETUP_PHASE_LABEL[game.phase];
  const singleHuman = game.players.filter((p) => p.isHuman && p.alive).length === 1;
  const aiRivals = game.players.some((p) => !p.isHuman && p.alive);

  return (
    <header className="absolute inset-x-0 top-0 z-30 border-b border-border/60 bg-card/80 px-2 py-1 shadow-[0_2px_8px_hsl(30_40%_20%/0.25)] backdrop-blur-md">
      <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-x-3 gap-y-1">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <span
            aria-hidden
            className="h-4 w-4 rounded-full border-2 border-[#3a2812] shadow-[inset_-1px_-2px_2px_rgba(0,0,0,0.3),inset_1px_1px_2px_rgba(255,255,255,0.4)]"
            style={{ backgroundColor: player.color }}
          />
          <div className="leading-tight">
            <p className="font-display text-sm font-bold">{player.name}</p>
            <p className="font-display text-[9px] uppercase tracking-imperial text-muted-foreground">
              {game.setup.tournamentGame !== undefined ? `Tournament ${game.setup.tournamentGame}/16 · ` : ""}
              Turn {game.turn} — {OBJECTIVE_INFO[game.setup.objective].name}
            </p>
          </div>
        </div>

        <nav aria-label="Phases" className="flex items-center gap-1">
          {setupLabel !== undefined && (
            <span className="border border-gold bg-gold/15 px-2 py-0.5 font-display text-[10px] uppercase tracking-widest text-gold">
              {setupLabel}
            </span>
          )}
          {PHASES.map((p) => (
            <span
              key={p.phase}
              className={cn(
                "border px-2 py-0.5 font-display text-[10px] uppercase tracking-widest",
                game.phase === p.phase
                  ? "border-gold bg-gold/15 text-gold"
                  : "border-transparent text-muted-foreground/60",
              )}
              title={p.label}
            >
              {p.roman}. {p.short}
            </span>
          ))}
        </nav>

        {game.phase === "election" && game.election && (
          <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
            <Coins className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-gold" />
            <span className="font-display text-xs font-bold text-gold">
              {game.election.points[game.players.findIndex((p) => p.isHuman)] ?? 0}
            </span>
            <span className="font-body text-xs text-muted-foreground">election points</span>
          </div>
        )}

        {game.phase === "initialDeploy" && isHumanTurn && (
          <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
            <Flag className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-gold" />
            <span className="font-display text-xs font-bold text-gold">{game.initialRemaining[player.id] ?? 0}</span>
            <span className="font-body text-xs text-muted-foreground">to muster</span>
          </div>
        )}

        {game.phase === "reinforcement" && isHumanTurn && (
          <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
            <Flag className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-gold" />
            <span className="font-display text-xs font-bold text-gold">{game.reinforcementsRemaining}</span>
            <span className="font-body text-xs text-muted-foreground">to place</span>
            <div className="ml-1 flex gap-1">
              {[1, 3, 0].map((amount) => (
                <button
                  key={amount}
                  type="button"
                  onClick={() => onDeployAmountChange(amount)}
                  className={cn(
                    "border px-1.5 py-0.5 font-display text-[10px]",
                    deployAmount === amount
                      ? "border-gold bg-gold/15 text-gold"
                      : "border-gold-dim/50 text-muted-foreground",
                  )}
                >
                  {amount === 0 ? "ALL" : `+${amount}`}
                </button>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
        )}

        <div className="ml-auto flex items-center gap-2">
          {isHumanTurn && game.phase === "reinforcement" && singleHuman && aiRivals && (
            <Button
              size="sm"
              variant="outline"
              className="h-7 gap-1 font-display text-[10px] uppercase tracking-widest"
              onClick={onOpenDiplomacy}
            >
              <Handshake className="h-3 w-3" /> Diplomacy
            </Button>
          )}
          {isHumanTurn && player.cards.length > 0 && game.phase === "reinforcement" && (
            <Button size="sm" variant="outline" className="h-7 gap-1 font-display text-[10px] uppercase tracking-widest" onClick={onOpenCards}>
              <Layers className="h-3 w-3" /> Cards ({player.cards.length})
            </Button>
          )}
          {isHumanTurn && game.phase === "attack" && !game.pendingOccupy && (
            <>
              <button
                type="button"
                onClick={() => onAllOutChange(!allOut)}
                title="All-out: keep rolling until the territory falls or the assault is spent"
                className={cn(
                  "border px-2 py-1 font-display text-[10px] uppercase tracking-widest transition-colors",
                  allOut
                    ? "border-crimson-bright bg-crimson-bright/15 text-crimson-bright"
                    : "border-gold-dim/50 text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground",
                )}
              >
                All-out {allOut ? "On" : "Off"}
              </button>
              <Button
                size="sm"
                className="h-7 gap-1 font-display text-[10px] uppercase tracking-widest"
                onClick={() => dispatch({ type: "END_ATTACK" })}
              >
                <Swords className="h-3 w-3" /> Cease Attack
              </Button>
            </>
          )}
          {isHumanTurn && game.phase === "fortify" && (
            <Button
              size="sm"
              className="h-7 font-display text-[10px] uppercase tracking-widest"
              onClick={() => dispatch({ type: "END_TURN" })}
            >
              Hold Positions — End Turn
            </Button>
          )}
          <Button
            size="sm"
            variant="ghost"
            className="h-7 w-7 p-0 text-muted-foreground hover:text-gold"
            title={sfxMuted ? "Unmute battle sounds" : "Mute battle sounds"}
            aria-label={sfxMuted ? "Unmute battle sounds" : "Mute battle sounds"}
            aria-pressed={sfxMuted}
            onClick={toggleSfxMuted}
          >
            {sfxMuted ? <VolumeX className="h-3.5 w-3.5" /> : <Volume2 className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />}
          </Button>
          <Button
            size="sm"
            variant="ghost"
            className="h-7 gap-1 font-display text-[10px] uppercase tracking-widest text-muted-foreground hover:text-gold"
            title="Return to the Main Hall — the campaign is saved automatically"
            onClick={() => navigate("/")}
          >
            <DoorOpen className="h-3 w-3" /> Hall
          </Button>
        </div>
      </div>
      {game.setup.objective === "mission" && player.isHuman && !game.awaitingHandoff && player.mission && (
        <p className="mt-0.5 truncate font-body text-[11px] italic leading-tight text-gold/80">
          Secret mission: {missionText(player.mission, game.players)}
        </p>
      )}
    </header>
  );
}

File: /web/src/components/game/TournamentOverlay.tsx
---

import { useState } from "react";
import { useQuery, useQueryClient } from "@tanstack/react-query";
import { Medal, Skull, Swords, Trophy } from "lucide-react";
import { useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";

import { FieldPanel, ImperialDivider } from "@/components/game/FieldPanel";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import {
  clearTournamentProgress,
  getTournamentProgress,
  saveTournamentProgress,
  submitHighScore,
} from "@/db/repository";
import {
  buildTournamentSetup,
  TOURNAMENT_GAMES,
  TOURNAMENT_LENGTH,
  tournamentResult,
} from "@/game/tournament";
import type { GameState } from "@/game/types";
import { useGame } from "@/state/GameContext";

/**
 * Tournament battle verdict (manual, Chapter 9 points system). Shown when a
 * tournament game concludes — or the moment the human commander is destroyed,
 * which ends the tournament outright.
 */
export function TournamentOverlay({ game }: { game: GameState }) {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const queryClient = useQueryClient();
  const { startGame, abandonGame } = useGame();
  const [busy, setBusy] = useState<boolean>(false);
  const progressQuery = useQuery({ queryKey: ["tournament"], queryFn: () => getTournamentProgress() });

  const gameIndex = game.setup.tournamentGame;
  const human = game.players.find((p) => p.isHuman);
  const show = gameIndex !== undefined && (game.phase === "gameOver" || (human !== undefined && !human.alive));
  if (!show || gameIndex === undefined || !human) return null;

  const def = TOURNAMENT_GAMES[gameIndex - 1];
  const result = tournamentResult(game);
  const banked = progressQuery.data?.totalPoints ?? 0;
  const commanderName = progressQuery.data?.name ?? human.name;
  const isFinalGame = gameIndex >= TOURNAMENT_LENGTH;

  const invalidate = () => {
    queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ["tournament"] });
    queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ["high-scores"] });
  };

  const handleRetry = () => {
    if (!def) return;
    startGame(buildTournamentSetup(def, commanderName));
  };

  const handleAdvance = async () => {
    setBusy(true);
    try {
      const total = banked + result.points;
      if (isFinalGame) {
        await submitHighScore(commanderName, total, TOURNAMENT_LENGTH);
        await clearTournamentProgress();
        invalidate();
        abandonGame();
        navigate("/tournament");
        return;
      }
      await saveTournamentProgress({ name: commanderName, currentGame: gameIndex + 1, totalPoints: total });
      invalidate();
      const next = TOURNAMENT_GAMES[gameIndex];
      if (next) startGame(buildTournamentSetup(next, commanderName));
    } finally {
      setBusy(false);
    }
  };

  const handleEliminated = async () => {
    setBusy(true);
    try {
      if (banked > 0) {
        await submitHighScore(commanderName, banked, gameIndex - 1);
      }
      await clearTournamentProgress();
      invalidate();
      abandonGame();
      navigate("/tournament");
    } finally {
      setBusy(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 flex items-center justify-center bg-[#241708]/70 p-4 backdrop-blur-sm">
      <div className="w-full max-w-md animate-fade-up">
        <FieldPanel className="bg-card text-center">
          {result.eliminated ? (
            <Skull className="mx-auto h-9 w-9 text-crimson-bright" aria-hidden />
          ) : (
            <Trophy className="mx-auto h-9 w-9 text-gold" aria-hidden />
          )}
          <p className="mt-2 font-display text-[10px] uppercase tracking-imperial text-muted-foreground">
            Tournament — Game {gameIndex} of {TOURNAMENT_LENGTH}: {def?.title ?? "Battle"}
          </p>
          <ImperialDivider className="my-3" />

          {result.eliminated ? (
            <>
              <h2 className="font-display text-2xl font-black text-crimson-bright">Destroyed in the Field</h2>
              <p className="mt-2 font-body text-sm italic text-muted-foreground">
                A fallen commander earns no points, and the tournament ends here. Your banked total of{" "}
                <span className="font-semibold text-foreground">{banked} points</span> across{" "}
                {gameIndex - 1} completed {gameIndex - 1 === 1 ? "game" : "games"} goes to the ledger.
              </p>
              <Button
                className="mt-5 w-full font-display uppercase tracking-imperial"
                onClick={handleEliminated}
                disabled={busy}
              >
                Record the Score
              </Button>
            </>
          ) : (
            <>
              <h2 className="font-display text-2xl font-black text-gold">
                {result.won ? "Victory!" : result.progressed ? "Battle Survived" : "No Ground Gained"}
              </h2>
              <ul className="mx-auto mt-3 max-w-xs space-y-1 text-left font-body text-sm">
                <li className="flex justify-between">
                  <span className="text-muted-foreground">Won the game</span>
                  <span className="font-semibold">{result.won ? "+150" : "—"}</span>
                </li>
                <li className="flex justify-between">
                  <span className="text-muted-foreground">
                    Opponents destroyed ({result.kills})
                  </span>
                  <span className="font-semibold">{result.kills > 0 ? `+${result.kills * 20}` : "—"}</span>
                </li>
                <li className="flex justify-between">
                  <span className="text-muted-foreground">Most troops at game end</span>
                  <span className="font-semibold">{result.mostTroops ? "+30" : "—"}</span>
                </li>
                <li className="flex justify-between border-t border-gold-dim/50 pt-1">
                  <span className="font-semibold">This battle</span>
                  <span className="font-display font-bold text-gold">{result.points} pts</span>
                </li>
                <li className="flex justify-between">
                  <span className="font-semibold">Tournament total</span>
                  <span className="font-display font-bold text-gold">{banked + result.points} pts</span>
                </li>
              </ul>
              {!result.progressed && (
                <p className="mt-3 font-body text-xs italic text-muted-foreground">
                  To advance you must win, or destroy at least one opponent and survive. Retry the battle.
                </p>
              )}
              <div className="mt-5 flex gap-2">
                {result.progressed && (
                  <Button
                    className="flex-1 gap-1.5 font-display text-xs uppercase tracking-imperial"
                    onClick={handleAdvance}
                    disabled={busy}
                  >
                    {isFinalGame ? (
                      <>
                        <Medal className="h-3.5 w-3.5" /> Complete the Tournament
                      </>
                    ) : (
                      <>
                        <Swords className="h-3.5 w-3.5" /> Advance to Game {gameIndex + 1}
                      </>
                    )}
                  </Button>
                )}
                <Button
                  variant={result.progressed ? "outline" : "default"}
                  className="flex-1 font-display text-xs uppercase tracking-imperial"
                  onClick={handleRetry}
                  disabled={busy}
                >
                  Retry for a Better Score
                </Button>
              </div>
            </>
          )}
        </FieldPanel>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

File: /web/src/components/game/WorldMap.tsx
---

import { memo, useMemo } from "react";

import { ART } from "@/lib/art";
import { MapPiece, PieceTintFilter } from "@/components/game/PieceSprite";
import { borderThreat, largestEmpire } from "@/game/analysis";
import { activeTerritories, CONTINENTS } from "@/game/mapData";
import { TERRITORY_PATHS } from "@/game/mapShapes";
import { breakdownLabel, dominantPiece } from "@/game/pieces";
import type { ContinentId, GameState, TerritoryId } from "@/game/types";

/** RISK II view modifiers (manual, Chapter 9). */
export type MapViewMode = "board" | "ownership" | "threats" | "strength" | "empire";

export const MAP_VIEW_LABEL: Record<MapViewMode, string> = {
  board: "Board",
  ownership: "Ownership",
  threats: "Border Threats",
  strength: "Troop Strength",
  empire: "Empires",
};

/** Blue (safe/weak) → red (dangerous/strong) heat color. */
function heat(t: number): string {
  const clamped = Math.min(1, Math.max(0, t));
  return `hsl(${Math.round(215 - 215 * clamped)} 78% 46%)`;
}

const W = 1536;
const H = 1024;

const BOARD_SCALE = W / 1000;
const scaleBoard = (value: number) => value * BOARD_SCALE;

const INK = "#6b4a26";
const INK_DARK = "#4a3418";

const PIECE_BASE_OFFSET_Y = scaleBoard(18);
const PIECE_SHADOW_OFFSET_Y = PIECE_BASE_OFFSET_Y + scaleBoard(2);
const PIECE_SPRITE_BASE_OFFSET_Y = PIECE_BASE_OFFSET_Y + scaleBoard(1);
const ARMY_ROUNDEL_OFFSET_X = scaleBoard(13);
const ARMY_ROUNDEL_OFFSET_Y = PIECE_BASE_OFFSET_Y - scaleBoard(7);

/**
 * Neighbor pairs that cross open water — only these get the classic red dashed
 * sea-route lines. Land adjacencies are implied by the painted borders.
 */
const SEA_ROUTES = new Set<string>(
  [
    ["alaska", "kamchatka"],
    ["greenland", "northwestTerritory"],
    ["greenland", "ontario"],
    ["greenland", "quebec"],
    ["greenland", "iceland"],
    ["greenland", "svalbard"],
    ["iceland", "svalbard"],
    ["iceland", "scandinavia"],
    ["iceland", "greatBritain"],
    ["scandinavia", "svalbard"],
    ["scandinavia", "greatBritain"],
    ["greatBritain", "northernEurope"],
    ["greatBritain", "westernEurope"],
    ["brazil", "northAfrica"],
    ["westernEurope", "northAfrica"],
    ["southernEurope", "northAfrica"],
    ["southernEurope", "egypt"],
    ["eastAfrica", "middleEast"],
    ["eastAfrica", "madagascar"],
    ["southAfrica", "madagascar"],
    ["madagascar", "falklandIslands"],
    ["argentina", "falklandIslands"],
    ["argentina", "newZealand"],
    ["easternAustralia", "newZealand"],
    ["kamchatka", "japan"],
    ["mongolia", "japan"],
    ["japan", "philippines"],
    ["japan", "hawaii"],
    ["westernUS", "hawaii"],
    ["siam", "indonesia"],
    ["siam", "philippines"],
    ["philippines", "indonesia"],
    ["indonesia", "newGuinea"],
    ["indonesia", "westernAustralia"],
    ["newGuinea", "westernAustralia"],
    ["newGuinea", "easternAustralia"],
  ].map((pair) => [...pair].sort().join("~")),
);

interface WorldMapProps {
  game: GameState;
  selected: TerritoryId | null;
  targets: Set<TerritoryId>;
  interactive: Set<TerritoryId>;
  viewMode: MapViewMode;
  onTerritoryClick: (id: TerritoryId) => void;
}

interface Edge {
  key: string;
  segments: { x1: number; y1: number; x2: number; y2: number }[];
}

function buildEdges(includeExtra: boolean): Edge[] {
  const defs = activeTerritories(includeExtra);
  const pos = new Map<TerritoryId, { x: number; y: number }>();
  for (const def of defs) pos.set(def.id, { x: def.x * W, y: def.y * H });
  const seen = new Set<string>();
  const edges: Edge[] = [];
  for (const def of defs) {
    for (const neighbor of def.neighbors) {
      const key = [def.id, neighbor].sort().join("~");
      if (seen.has(key)) continue;
      seen.add(key);
      if (!SEA_ROUTES.has(key)) continue;
      const a = pos.get(def.id);
      const b = pos.get(neighbor);
      if (!a || !b) continue;
      if (Math.abs(a.x - b.x) > W * 0.5) {
        // Wrap-around route (e.g. Alaska–Kamchatka): exit both map edges.
        const left = a.x < b.x ? a : b;
        const right = a.x < b.x ? b : a;
        edges.push({
          key,
          segments: [
            { x1: left.x, y1: left.y, x2: 0, y2: (left.y + right.y) / 2 },
            { x1: W, y1: (left.y + right.y) / 2, x2: right.x, y2: right.y },
          ],
        });
      } else {
        edges.push({ key, segments: [{ x1: a.x, y1: a.y, x2: b.x, y2: b.y }] });
      }
    }
  }
  return edges;
}

function OceanLabel({ x, y, lines, size = 14 }: { x: number; y: number; lines: string[]; size?: number }) {
  return (
    <g aria-hidden pointerEvents="none">
      {lines.map((line, i) => (
        <text
          key={line}
          x={x}
          y={y + i * (size + scaleBoard(7))}
          textAnchor="middle"
          fontSize={size}
          fontFamily="'IM Fell English SC', serif"
          letterSpacing="0.4em"
          fill="#8a6a3c"
          opacity="0.8"
        >
          {line}
        </text>
      ))}
    </g>
  );
}

export const WorldMap = memo(function WorldMap({ game, selected, targets, interactive, viewMode, onTerritoryClick }: WorldMapProps) {
  const defs = useMemo(() => activeTerritories(game.setup.useExtraTerritories), [game.setup.useExtraTerritories]);
  const edges = useMemo(() => buildEdges(game.setup.useExtraTerritories), [game.setup.useExtraTerritories]);
  const capitals = useMemo(() => {
    const map = new Map<TerritoryId, number>();
    for (const p of game.players) {
      if (p.capital) map.set(p.capital, p.id);
    }
    return map;
  }, [game.players]);
  const pieceColors = useMemo(
    () => Array.from(new Set([...game.players.map((p) => p.color), "#666666"])),
    [game.players],
  );

  // View-modifier tint per territory (manual, Chapter 9: The View Modifier).
  const overlay = useMemo(() => {
    if (viewMode === "board") return null;
    const map = new Map<TerritoryId, string>();
    if (viewMode === "ownership") {
      for (const id of game.activeIds) {
        const owner = game.players[game.territories[id].owner];
        if (owner) map.set(id, owner.color);
      }
    } else if (viewMode === "threats") {
      for (const id of game.activeIds) {
        const territory = game.territories[id];
        if (territory.owner < 0) continue;
        const threat = borderThreat(game, id, territory.owner);
        const ratio = threat / Math.max(1, territory.armies);
        map.set(id, heat(ratio / 3));
      }
    } else if (viewMode === "strength") {
      const max = Math.max(1, ...game.activeIds.map((id) => game.territories[id].armies));
      for (const id of game.activeIds) {
        if (game.territories[id].owner < 0) continue;
        map.set(id, heat(game.territories[id].armies / max));
      }
    } else if (viewMode === "empire") {
      for (const player of game.players) {
        if (!player.alive) continue;
        for (const id of largestEmpire(game, player.id)) {
          map.set(id, player.color);
        }
      }
    }
    return map;
  }, [game, viewMode]);

  return (
    // The viewBox is intentionally NOT set via JSX: the MapViewport camera rig
    // drives it imperatively each animation frame (at the container's live
    // aspect ratio), and a React-managed attribute would snap back to the
    // full board on every re-render. The svg fills the container completely —
    // portrait and landscape framing is the camera's job, not CSS letterboxing.
    <svg className="h-full w-full select-none" role="application" aria-label="Campaign map">
      <defs>
        <radialGradient id="seaVignette" cx="50%" cy="42%" r="85%">
          <stop offset="0%" stopColor="hsl(30 40% 30%)" stopOpacity="0" />
          <stop offset="75%" stopColor="hsl(30 42% 28%)" stopOpacity="0.05" />
          <stop offset="100%" stopColor="hsl(28 44% 22%)" stopOpacity="0.28" />
        </radialGradient>
        {pieceColors.map((color) => (
          <PieceTintFilter key={color} color={color} />
        ))}
      </defs>

      {/* The painted Risk II world board */}
      <image
        href={ART.worldBoard}
        x={0}
        y={0}
        width={W}
        height={H}
        preserveAspectRatio="none"
        pointerEvents="none"
        aria-hidden
      />
      <rect width={W} height={H} fill="url(#seaVignette)" pointerEvents="none" />

      {/* Ocean lettering */}
      <OceanLabel x={scaleBoard(75)} y={scaleBoard(392)} lines={["Pacific", "Ocean"]} size={scaleBoard(14)} />
      <OceanLabel x={scaleBoard(352)} y={scaleBoard(230)} lines={["Atlantic", "Ocean"]} size={scaleBoard(12)} />
      <OceanLabel x={scaleBoard(655)} y={scaleBoard(455)} lines={["Indian", "Ocean"]} size={scaleBoard(14)} />

      {/* Sea routes — classic red dashed lines, drawn under the land so only water crossings show */}
      {edges.map((edge) =>
        edge.segments.map((s, i) => (
          <line
            key={`${edge.key}-${i}`}
            x1={s.x1}
            y1={s.y1}
            x2={s.x2}
            y2={s.y2}
            stroke="#a63d2b"
            strokeOpacity="0.65"
            strokeWidth={scaleBoard(1.6)}
            strokeDasharray="5 5"
          />
        )),
      )}

      {/* Territory shapes — traced outlines used as full-area hit targets */}
      {defs.map((def) => {
        const isTarget = targets.has(def.id);
        const isInteractive = interactive.has(def.id) || isTarget;
        return (
          <path
            key={`shape-${def.id}`}
            d={TERRITORY_PATHS[def.id]}
            className={`territory-shape ${isInteractive ? "active" : ""}`}
            fill="transparent"
            onClick={() => onTerritoryClick(def.id)}
            aria-hidden
          />
        );
      })}

      {/* View-modifier tints under the pieces — fill the actual territory shape */}
      {overlay &&
        defs.map((def) => {
          const tint = overlay.get(def.id);
          if (!tint) return null;
          return (
            <path
              key={`view-${def.id}`}
              d={TERRITORY_PATHS[def.id]}
              fill={tint}
              fillOpacity={0.36}
              stroke={tint}
              strokeOpacity={0.8}
              strokeWidth={scaleBoard(1.4)}
              pointerEvents="none"
            />
          );
        })}

      {/* Selection / target outlines on the traced territory borders */}
      {defs.map((def) => {
        const isSelected = selected === def.id;
        const isTarget = targets.has(def.id);
        if (!isSelected && !isTarget) return null;
        return (
          <path
            key={`ring-${def.id}`}
            d={TERRITORY_PATHS[def.id]}
            fill={isSelected ? "hsl(43 88% 50% / 0.14)" : "hsl(0 70% 45% / 0.12)"}
            stroke={isSelected ? "hsl(43 88% 40%)" : "#b3262a"}
            strokeWidth={scaleBoard(2.5)}
            strokeDasharray={isTarget ? "6 8" : undefined}
            className={isSelected ? "animate-ring-pulse" : "animate-target-dash"}
            pointerEvents="none"
          />
        );
      })}

      {/* Army pieces — infantry (1), cavalry (5), artillery (10) */}
      {defs.map((def) => {
        const territory = game.territories[def.id];
        const unclaimed = territory.owner < 0;
        const owner = game.players[territory.owner];
        const color = owner?.color ?? "#666666";
        const cx = def.x * W;
        const cy = def.y * H;
        const isInteractive = interactive.has(def.id) || targets.has(def.id);
        const capitalOwner = capitals.get(def.id);
        const piece = dominantPiece(territory.armies);
        if (unclaimed) {
          return (
            <g
              key={def.id}
              className={`territory-node ${isInteractive ? "" : "inert"}`}
              onClick={() => onTerritoryClick(def.id)}
              role="button"
              aria-label={`${def.name}, unclaimed`}
            >
              <circle
                cx={cx}
                cy={cy}
                r={scaleBoard(11)}
                fill="hsl(46 55% 88% / 0.55)"
                stroke={isInteractive ? "hsl(43 88% 40%)" : INK}
                strokeWidth={isInteractive ? scaleBoard(2) : scaleBoard(1.2)}
                strokeDasharray="3 3"
                className={isInteractive ? "animate-ring-pulse" : undefined}
              />
              <text
                x={cx}
                y={cy + scaleBoard(25)}
                textAnchor="middle"
                fontSize={scaleBoard(10)}
                fontFamily="'IM Fell English', serif"
                fill={INK_DARK}
                stroke="hsl(46 60% 88% / 0.85)"
                strokeWidth={scaleBoard(2.5)}
                paintOrder="stroke"
              >
                {def.name}
              </text>
            </g>
          );
        }
        return (
          <g
            key={def.id}
            className={`territory-node ${isInteractive ? "" : "inert"}`}
            onClick={() => onTerritoryClick(def.id)}
            role="button"
            aria-label={`${def.name}, ${owner?.name ?? "unknown"}, ${territory.armies} armies (${breakdownLabel(territory.armies)})`}
            opacity={isInteractive ? 1 : 0.94}
          >
            <ellipse cx={cx + scaleBoard(1)} cy={cy + PIECE_SHADOW_OFFSET_Y} rx={scaleBoard(14.5)} ry={scaleBoard(4.5)} fill="#2e2010" opacity="0.25" />
            {/* Plastic base the piece stands on. A measured vertical offset places the base in the territory body while the label remains readable below it. */}
            <ellipse
              cx={cx}
              cy={cy + PIECE_BASE_OFFSET_Y}
              rx={scaleBoard(13)}
              ry={scaleBoard(4.2)}
              fill={color}
              stroke="#3a2812"
              strokeWidth={scaleBoard(1.2)}
            />
            <MapPiece type={piece} color={color} cx={cx} baseY={cy + PIECE_SPRITE_BASE_OFFSET_Y} scale={BOARD_SCALE} />
            {capitalOwner !== undefined && (
              <text
                x={cx - scaleBoard(15)}
                y={cy - scaleBoard(12)}
                textAnchor="middle"
                fontSize={scaleBoard(13)}
                fill="#7a5a10"
                stroke="hsl(46 60% 90% / 0.9)"
                strokeWidth={scaleBoard(2)}
                paintOrder="stroke"
              >
                ★
              </text>
            )}

            {/* Muster-count roundel */}
            <circle
              cx={cx + ARMY_ROUNDEL_OFFSET_X}
              cy={cy + ARMY_ROUNDEL_OFFSET_Y}
              r={scaleBoard(8)}
              fill="hsl(46 62% 90%)"
              stroke="#6b4a26"
              strokeWidth={scaleBoard(1)}
            />
            <text
              x={cx + ARMY_ROUNDEL_OFFSET_X}
              y={cy + ARMY_ROUNDEL_OFFSET_Y + scaleBoard(3.5)}
              textAnchor="middle"
              fontSize={scaleBoard(territory.armies > 99 ? 8 : 10)}
              fontWeight="800"
              fontFamily="Alegreya, serif"
              fill={INK_DARK}
            >
              {territory.armies}
            </text>
            <text
              x={cx}
              y={cy + scaleBoard(31)}
              textAnchor="middle"
              fontSize={scaleBoard(10)}
              fontFamily="'IM Fell English', serif"
              fill={INK_DARK}
              stroke="hsl(46 60% 88% / 0.85)"
              strokeWidth={scaleBoard(2.5)}
              paintOrder="stroke"
            >
              {def.name}
            </text>
          </g>
        );
      })}

      {/* Continent legend */}
      <g transform={`translate(${scaleBoard(14)}, ${H - scaleBoard(24)})`}>
        {(Object.keys(CONTINENTS) as ContinentId[]).map((id, i) => (
          <g key={id} transform={`translate(${i * scaleBoard(128)}, 0)`}>
            <circle cx={scaleBoard(5)} cy={scaleBoard(5)} r={scaleBoard(5)} fill={CONTINENTS[id].color} stroke={INK} strokeWidth={scaleBoard(0.8)} />
            <text x={scaleBoard(15)} y={scaleBoard(9)} fontSize={scaleBoard(10.5)} fontFamily="'IM Fell English', serif" fill="#5b4020">
              {CONTINENTS[id].name} +{CONTINENTS[id].bonus}
            </text>
          </g>
        ))}
      </g>

      {/* Double map frame */}
      <rect x={scaleBoard(1.5)} y={scaleBoard(1.5)} width={W - scaleBoard(3)} height={H - scaleBoard(3)} fill="none" stroke="#7a5a2e" strokeWidth={scaleBoard(3)} />
      <rect x={scaleBoard(7)} y={scaleBoard(7)} width={W - scaleBoard(14)} height={H - scaleBoard(14)} fill="none" stroke="#7a5a2e" strokeOpacity="0.6" strokeWidth={scaleBoard(1)} />
    </svg>
  );
});

import * as AccordionPrimitive from "@radix-ui/react-accordion";
import { ChevronDown } from "lucide-react";
import * as React from "react";

import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";

const Accordion = AccordionPrimitive.Root;

const AccordionItem = ({ ref, className, ...props }: React.ComponentPropsWithRef<typeof AccordionPrimitive.Item>) => (
  <AccordionPrimitive.Item ref={ref} className={cn("border-b", className)} {...props} />
);
AccordionItem.displayName = "AccordionItem";

const AccordionTrigger = ({
  ref,
  className,
  children,
  ...props
}: React.ComponentPropsWithRef<typeof AccordionPrimitive.Trigger>) => (
  <AccordionPrimitive.Header className="flex">
    <AccordionPrimitive.Trigger
      ref={ref}
      className={cn(
        "flex flex-1 items-center justify-between py-4 font-medium transition-all hover:underline [&[data-state=open]>svg]:rotate-180",
        className,
      )}
      {...props}
    >
      {children}
      <ChevronDown className="h-4 w-4 shrink-0 transition-transform duration-200" />
    </AccordionPrimitive.Trigger>
  </AccordionPrimitive.Header>
);
AccordionTrigger.displayName = AccordionPrimitive.Trigger.displayName;

const AccordionContent = ({
  ref,
  className,
  children,
  ...props
}: React.ComponentPropsWithRef<typeof AccordionPrimitive.Content>) => (
  <AccordionPrimitive.Content
    ref={ref}
    className="overflow-hidden text-sm transition-all data-[state=closed]:animate-accordion-up data-[state=open]:animate-accordion-down"
    {...props}
  >
    <div className={cn("pb-4 pt-0", className)}>{children}</div>
  </AccordionPrimitive.Content>
);

AccordionContent.displayName = AccordionPrimitive.Content.displayName;

export { Accordion, AccordionItem, AccordionTrigger, AccordionContent };

);

);
AlertDialogDescription.displayName = AlertDialogPrimitive.Description.displayName;

}: React.ComponentPropsWithRef<typeof AlertDialogPrimitive.Action>) => (

);

  ref,

  ...props
}: React.ComponentPropsWithRef<typeof AlertDialogPrimitive.Cancel>) => (

    ref={ref}
    className={cn(buttonVariants({ variant: "outline" }), "mt-2 sm:mt-0", className)}
    {...props}
  />
);
AlertDialogCancel.displayName = AlertDialogPrimitive.Cancel.displayName;

import { cva, type VariantProps } from "class-variance-authority";
import * as React from "react";

import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";

const alertVariants = cva(
  "relative w-full rounded-lg border p-4 [&>svg~*]:pl-7 [&>svg+div]:translate-y-[-3px] [&>svg]:absolute [&>svg]:left-4 [&>svg]:top-4 [&>svg]:text-foreground",
  {
    variants: {
      variant: {
        default: "bg-background text-foreground",
        destructive: "border-destructive/50 text-destructive dark:border-destructive [&>svg]:text-destructive",
      },
    },
    defaultVariants: {
      variant: "default",
    },
  },
);

const Alert = ({
  ref,
  className,
  variant,
  ...props
}: React.ComponentPropsWithRef<"div"> & VariantProps<typeof alertVariants>) => (
  <div ref={ref} role="alert" className={cn(alertVariants({ variant }), className)} {...props} />
);
Alert.displayName = "Alert";

const AlertTitle = ({ ref, className, ...props }: React.ComponentPropsWithRef<"h5">) => (
  <h5 ref={ref} className={cn("mb-1 font-medium leading-none tracking-tight", className)} {...props} />
);
AlertTitle.displayName = "AlertTitle";

const AlertDescription = ({ ref, className, ...props }: React.ComponentPropsWithRef<"div">) => (
  <div ref={ref} className={cn("text-sm [&_p]:leading-relaxed", className)} {...props} />
);
AlertDescription.displayName = "AlertDescription";

export { Alert, AlertTitle, AlertDescription };

import { cva, type VariantProps } from "class-variance-authority";
import * as React from "react";

import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";

const badgeVariants = cva(
  "inline-flex items-center rounded-full border px-2.5 py-0.5 text-xs font-semibold transition-colors focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-ring focus:ring-offset-2",
  {
    variants: {
      variant: {
        default: "border-transparent bg-primary text-primary-foreground hover:bg-primary/80",
        secondary: "border-transparent bg-secondary text-secondary-foreground hover:bg-secondary/80",
        destructive: "border-transparent bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground hover:bg-destructive/80",
        outline: "text-foreground",
      },
    },
    defaultVariants: {
      variant: "default",
    },
  },
);

export interface BadgeProps extends React.HTMLAttributes<HTMLDivElement>, VariantProps<typeof badgeVariants> {}

function Badge({ className, variant, ...props }: BadgeProps) {
  return <div className={cn(badgeVariants({ variant }), className)} {...props} />;
}

export { Badge, badgeVariants };

    ref={ref}

      "flex flex-wrap items-center gap-1.5 break-words text-sm text-muted-foreground sm:gap-2.5",

  />
);

  ref,

  ...props
}: React.ComponentPropsWithRef<"a"> & {

  </span>
);

import { Slot } from "@radix-ui/react-slot";
import { cva, type VariantProps } from "class-variance-authority";
import * as React from "react";

import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";

const buttonVariants = cva(
  "inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 whitespace-nowrap rounded-md text-sm font-medium ring-offset-background transition-colors focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-ring focus-visible:ring-offset-2 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 [&_svg]:pointer-events-none [&_svg]:size-4 [&_svg]:shrink-0",
  {
    variants: {
      variant: {
        default: "bg-primary text-primary-foreground hover:bg-primary/90",
        destructive: "bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground hover:bg-destructive/90",
        outline: "border border-input bg-background hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground",
        secondary: "bg-secondary text-secondary-foreground hover:bg-secondary/80",
        ghost: "hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground",
        link: "text-primary underline-offset-4 hover:underline",
      },
      size: {
        default: "h-10 px-4 py-2",
        sm: "h-9 rounded-md px-3",
        lg: "h-11 rounded-md px-8",
        icon: "h-10 w-10",
      },
    },
    defaultVariants: {
      variant: "default",
      size: "default",
    },
  },
);

export interface ButtonProps extends React.ComponentPropsWithRef<"button">, VariantProps<typeof buttonVariants> {
  asChild?: boolean;
}

const Button = ({ ref, className, variant, size, asChild = false, ...props }: ButtonProps) => {
  const Comp = asChild ? Slot : "button";
  return <Comp className={cn(buttonVariants({ variant, size, className }))} ref={ref} {...props} />;
};
Button.displayName = "Button";

export { Button, buttonVariants };

File: /web/src/components/ui/carousel.tsx
---

import useEmblaCarousel, { type UseEmblaCarouselType } from "embla-carousel-react";
import { ArrowLeft, ArrowRight } from "lucide-react";
import * as React from "react";

import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";

type CarouselApi = UseEmblaCarouselType[1];
type UseCarouselParameters = Parameters<typeof useEmblaCarousel>;
type CarouselOptions = UseCarouselParameters[0];
type CarouselPlugin = UseCarouselParameters[1];

type CarouselProps = {
  opts?: CarouselOptions;
  plugins?: CarouselPlugin;
  orientation?: "horizontal" | "vertical";
  setApi?: (api: CarouselApi) => void;
};

type CarouselContextProps = {
  carouselRef: ReturnType<typeof useEmblaCarousel>[0];
  api: ReturnType<typeof useEmblaCarousel>[1];
  scrollPrev: () => void;
  scrollNext: () => void;
  canScrollPrev: boolean;
  canScrollNext: boolean;
} & CarouselProps;

const CarouselContext = React.createContext<CarouselContextProps | null>(null);

function useCarousel() {
  const context = React.useContext(CarouselContext);

  if (!context) {
    throw new Error("useCarousel must be used within a <Carousel />");
  }

  return context;
}

const Carousel = ({
  ref,
  orientation = "horizontal",
  opts,
  setApi,
  plugins,
  className,
  children,
  ...props
}: React.ComponentPropsWithRef<"div"> & CarouselProps) => {
  const [carouselRef, api] = useEmblaCarousel(
    {
      ...opts,
      axis: orientation === "horizontal" ? "x" : "y",
    },
    plugins,
  );
  const [canScrollPrev, setCanScrollPrev] = React.useState(false);
  const [canScrollNext, setCanScrollNext] = React.useState(false);

  const onSelect = React.useCallback((api: CarouselApi) => {
    if (!api) {
      return;
    }

    setCanScrollPrev(api.canScrollPrev());
    setCanScrollNext(api.canScrollNext());
  }, []);

  const scrollPrev = React.useCallback(() => {
    api?.scrollPrev();
  }, [api]);

  const scrollNext = React.useCallback(() => {
    api?.scrollNext();
  }, [api]);

  const handleKeyDown = React.useCallback(
    (event: React.KeyboardEvent<HTMLDivElement>) => {
      if (event.key === "ArrowLeft") {
        event.preventDefault();
        scrollPrev();
      } else if (event.key === "ArrowRight") {
        event.preventDefault();
        scrollNext();
      }
    },
    [scrollPrev, scrollNext],
  );

  React.useEffect(() => {
    if (!api || !setApi) {
      return;
    }

    setApi(api);
  }, [api, setApi]);

  React.useEffect(() => {
    if (!api) {
      return;
    }

    onSelect(api);
    api.on("reInit", onSelect);
    api.on("select", onSelect);

    return () => {
      api?.off("select", onSelect);
    };
  }, [api, onSelect]);

  return (
    <CarouselContext.Provider
      value={{
        carouselRef,
        api: api,
        opts,
        orientation: orientation || (opts?.axis === "y" ? "vertical" : "horizontal"),
        scrollPrev,
        scrollNext,
        canScrollPrev,
        canScrollNext,
      }}
    >
      <div
        ref={ref}
        onKeyDownCapture={handleKeyDown}
        className={cn("relative", className)}
        role="region"
        aria-roledescription="carousel"
        {...props}
      >
        {children}
      </div>
    </CarouselContext.Provider>
  );
};
Carousel.displayName = "Carousel";

const CarouselContent = ({ ref, className, ...props }: React.ComponentPropsWithRef<"div">) => {
  const { carouselRef, orientation } = useCarousel();

  return (
    <div ref={carouselRef} className="overflow-hidden">
      <div
        ref={ref}
        className={cn("flex", orientation === "horizontal" ? "-ml-4" : "-mt-4 flex-col", className)}
        {...props}
      />
    </div>
  );
};
CarouselContent.displayName = "CarouselContent";

const CarouselItem = ({ ref, className, ...props }: React.ComponentPropsWithRef<"div">) => {
  const { orientation } = useCarousel();

  return (
    <div
      ref={ref}
      role="group"
      aria-roledescription="slide"
      className={cn("min-w-0 shrink-0 grow-0 basis-full", orientation === "horizontal" ? "pl-4" : "pt-4", className)}
      {...props}
    />
  );
};
CarouselItem.displayName = "CarouselItem";

const CarouselPrevious = ({
  ref,
  className,
  variant = "outline",
  size = "icon",
  ...props
}: React.ComponentPropsWithRef<typeof Button>) => {
  const { orientation, scrollPrev, canScrollPrev } = useCarousel();

  return (
    <Button
      ref={ref}
      variant={variant}
      size={size}
      className={cn(
        "absolute h-8 w-8 rounded-full",
        orientation === "horizontal"
          ? "-left-12 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2"
          : "-top-12 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 rotate-90",
        className,
      )}
      disabled={!canScrollPrev}
      onClick={scrollPrev}
      {...props}
    >
      <ArrowLeft className="h-4 w-4" />
      <span className="sr-only">Previous slide</span>
    </Button>
  );
};
CarouselPrevious.displayName = "CarouselPrevious";

const CarouselNext = ({
  ref,
  className,
  variant = "outline",
  size = "icon",
  ...props
}: React.ComponentPropsWithRef<typeof Button>) => {
  const { orientation, scrollNext, canScrollNext } = useCarousel();

  return (
    <Button
      ref={ref}
      variant={variant}
      size={size}
      className={cn(
        "absolute h-8 w-8 rounded-full",
        orientation === "horizontal"
          ? "-right-12 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2"
          : "-bottom-12 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 rotate-90",
        className,
      )}
      disabled={!canScrollNext}
      onClick={scrollNext}
      {...props}
    >
      <ArrowRight className="h-4 w-4" />
      <span className="sr-only">Next slide</span>
    </Button>
  );
};
CarouselNext.displayName = "CarouselNext";

export { type CarouselApi, Carousel, CarouselContent, CarouselItem, CarouselPrevious, CarouselNext };



---
File: /web/src/components/ui/chart.tsx
---

import * as React from "react";
import * as RechartsPrimitive from "recharts";

import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";

// Format: { THEME_NAME: CSS_SELECTOR }
const THEMES = { light: "", dark: ".dark" } as const;

export type ChartConfig = {
  [k in string]: {
    label?: React.ReactNode;
    icon?: React.ComponentType;
  } & ({ color?: string; theme?: never } | { color?: never; theme: Record<keyof typeof THEMES, string> });
};

type ChartContextProps = {
  config: ChartConfig;
};

const ChartContext = React.createContext<ChartContextProps | null>(null);

function useChart() {
  const context = React.useContext(ChartContext);

  if (!context) {
    throw new Error("useChart must be used within a <ChartContainer />");
  }

  return context;
}

const ChartContainer = ({
  ref,
  id,
  className,
  children,
  config,
  ...props
}: React.ComponentPropsWithRef<"div"> & {
  config: ChartConfig;
  children: React.ComponentProps<typeof RechartsPrimitive.ResponsiveContainer>["children"];
}) => {
  const uniqueId = React.useId();
  const chartId = `chart-${id || uniqueId.replace(/:/g, "")}`;

  return (
    <ChartContext.Provider value={{ config }}>
      <div
        data-chart={chartId}
        ref={ref}
        className={cn(
          "flex aspect-video justify-center text-xs [&_.recharts-cartesian-axis-tick_text]:fill-muted-foreground [&_.recharts-cartesian-grid_line[stroke='#ccc']]:stroke-border/50 [&_.recharts-curve.recharts-tooltip-cursor]:stroke-border [&_.recharts-dot[stroke='#fff']]:stroke-transparent [&_.recharts-layer]:outline-none [&_.recharts-polar-grid_[stroke='#ccc']]:stroke-border [&_.recharts-radial-bar-background-sector]:fill-muted [&_.recharts-rectangle.recharts-tooltip-cursor]:fill-muted [&_.recharts-reference-line_[stroke='#ccc']]:stroke-border [&_.recharts-sector[stroke='#fff']]:stroke-transparent [&_.recharts-sector]:outline-none [&_.recharts-surface]:outline-none",
          className,
        )}
        {...props}
      >
        <ChartStyle id={chartId} config={config} />
        <RechartsPrimitive.ResponsiveContainer>{children}</RechartsPrimitive.ResponsiveContainer>
      </div>
    </ChartContext.Provider>
  );
};
ChartContainer.displayName = "Chart";

const ChartStyle = ({ id, config }: { id: string; config: ChartConfig }) => {
  const colorConfig = Object.entries(config).filter(([_, config]) => config.theme || config.color);

  if (!colorConfig.length) {
    return null;
  }

  return (
    <style
      dangerouslySetInnerHTML={{
        __html: Object.entries(THEMES)
          .map(
            ([theme, prefix]) => `
${prefix} [data-chart=${id}] {
${colorConfig
  .map(([key, itemConfig]) => {
    const color = itemConfig.theme?.[theme as keyof typeof itemConfig.theme] || itemConfig.color;
    return color ? `  --color-${key}: ${color};` : null;
  })
  .join("\n")}
}
`,
          )
          .join("\n"),
      }}
    />
  );
};

const ChartTooltip = RechartsPrimitive.Tooltip;

const ChartTooltipContent = ({
  ref,
  active,
  payload,
  className,
  indicator = "dot",
  hideLabel = false,
  hideIndicator = false,
  label,
  labelFormatter,
  labelClassName,
  formatter,
  color,
  nameKey,
  labelKey,
}: React.ComponentPropsWithRef<typeof RechartsPrimitive.Tooltip> &
  React.ComponentProps<"div"> & {
    hideLabel?: boolean;
    hideIndicator?: boolean;
    indicator?: "line" | "dot" | "dashed";
    nameKey?: string;
    labelKey?: string;
  }) => {
  const { config } = useChart();

  const tooltipLabel = React.useMemo(() => {
    if (hideLabel || !payload?.length) {
      return null;
    }

    const [item] = payload;
    const key = `${labelKey || item.dataKey || item.name || "value"}`;
    const itemConfig = getPayloadConfigFromPayload(config, item, key);
    const value =
      !labelKey && typeof label === "string" ? config[label as keyof typeof config]?.label || label : itemConfig?.label;

    if (labelFormatter) {
      return <div className={cn("font-medium", labelClassName)}>{labelFormatter(value, payload)}</div>;
    }

    if (!value) {
      return null;
    }

    return <div className={cn("font-medium", labelClassName)}>{value}</div>;
  }, [label, labelFormatter, payload, hideLabel, labelClassName, config, labelKey]);

  if (!active || !payload?.length) {
    return null;
  }

  const nestLabel = payload.length === 1 && indicator !== "dot";

  return (
    <div
      ref={ref}
      className={cn(
        "grid min-w-[8rem] items-start gap-1.5 rounded-lg border border-border/50 bg-background px-2.5 py-1.5 text-xs shadow-xl",
        className,
      )}
    >
      {!nestLabel ? tooltipLabel : null}
      <div className="grid gap-1.5">
        {payload.map((item, index) => {
          const key = `${nameKey || item.name || item.dataKey || "value"}`;
          const itemConfig = getPayloadConfigFromPayload(config, item, key);
          const indicatorColor = color || item.payload.fill || item.color;

          return (
            <div
              key={item.dataKey}
              className={cn(
                "flex w-full flex-wrap items-stretch gap-2 [&>svg]:h-2.5 [&>svg]:w-2.5 [&>svg]:text-muted-foreground",
                indicator === "dot" && "items-center",
              )}
            >
              {formatter && item?.value !== undefined && item.name ? (
                formatter(item.value, item.name, item, index, item.payload)
              ) : (
                <>
                  {itemConfig?.icon ? (
                    <itemConfig.icon />
                  ) : (
                    !hideIndicator && (
                      <div
                        className={cn("shrink-0 rounded-[2px] border-[--color-border] bg-[--color-bg]", {
                          "h-2.5 w-2.5": indicator === "dot",
                          "w-1": indicator === "line",
                          "w-0 border-[1.5px] border-dashed bg-transparent": indicator === "dashed",
                          "my-0.5": nestLabel && indicator === "dashed",
                        })}
                        style={
                          {
                            "--color-bg": indicatorColor,
                            "--color-border": indicatorColor,
                          } as React.CSSProperties
                        }
                      />
                    )
                  )}
                  <div
                    className={cn("flex flex-1 justify-between leading-none", nestLabel ? "items-end" : "items-center")}
                  >
                    <div className="grid gap-1.5">
                      {nestLabel ? tooltipLabel : null}
                      <span className="text-muted-foreground">{itemConfig?.label || item.name}</span>
                    </div>
                    {item.value !== undefined && (
                      <span className="font-mono font-medium tabular-nums text-foreground">
                        {item.value.toLocaleString()}
                      </span>
                    )}
                  </div>
                </>
              )}
            </div>
          );
        })}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};
ChartTooltipContent.displayName = "ChartTooltip";

const ChartLegend = RechartsPrimitive.Legend;

const ChartLegendContent = ({
  ref,
  className,
  hideIcon = false,
  payload,
  verticalAlign = "bottom",
  nameKey,
}: React.ComponentPropsWithRef<"div"> &
  Pick<RechartsPrimitive.LegendProps, "payload" | "verticalAlign"> & {
    hideIcon?: boolean;
    nameKey?: string;
  }) => {
  const { config } = useChart();

  if (!payload?.length) {
    return null;
  }

  return (
    <div
      ref={ref}
      className={cn("flex items-center justify-center gap-4", verticalAlign === "top" ? "pb-3" : "pt-3", className)}
    >
      {payload.map((item) => {
        const key = `${nameKey || item.dataKey || "value"}`;
        const itemConfig = getPayloadConfigFromPayload(config, item, key);

        return (
          <div
            key={item.value}
            className={cn("flex items-center gap-1.5 [&>svg]:h-3 [&>svg]:w-3 [&>svg]:text-muted-foreground")}
          >
            {itemConfig?.icon && !hideIcon ? (
              <itemConfig.icon />
            ) : (
              <div
                className="h-2 w-2 shrink-0 rounded-[2px]"
                style={{
                  backgroundColor: item.color,
                }}
              />
            )}
            {itemConfig?.label}
          </div>
        );
      })}
    </div>
  );
};
ChartLegendContent.displayName = "ChartLegend";

// Helper to extract item config from a payload.
function getPayloadConfigFromPayload(config: ChartConfig, payload: unknown, key: string) {
  if (typeof payload !== "object" || payload === null) {
    return undefined;
  }

  const payloadPayload =
    "payload" in payload && typeof payload.payload === "object" && payload.payload !== null
      ? payload.payload
      : undefined;

  let configLabelKey: string = key;

  if (key in payload && typeof payload[key as keyof typeof payload] === "string") {
    configLabelKey = payload[key as keyof typeof payload] as string;
  } else if (
    payloadPayload &&
    key in payloadPayload &&
    typeof payloadPayload[key as keyof typeof payloadPayload] === "string"
  ) {
    configLabelKey = payloadPayload[key as keyof typeof payloadPayload] as string;
  }

  return configLabelKey in config ? config[configLabelKey] : config[key as keyof typeof config];
}

export { ChartContainer, ChartTooltip, ChartTooltipContent, ChartLegend, ChartLegendContent, ChartStyle };

import * as DialogPrimitive from "@radix-ui/react-dialog";

const DialogClose = DialogPrimitive.Close;

const DialogOverlay = ({ ref, className, ...props }: React.ComponentPropsWithRef<typeof DialogPrimitive.Overlay>) => (
  <DialogPrimitive.Overlay
    ref={ref}
    className={cn(
      "fixed inset-0 z-50 bg-black/80 data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0",
      className,
    )}
    {...props}
  />
);

  ref,
  className,
  children,
  ...props

    <DialogOverlay />

      ref={ref}

        className,
      )}
      {...props}
    >
      {children}
      <DialogPrimitive.Close className="absolute right-4 top-4 rounded-sm opacity-70 ring-offset-background transition-opacity data-[state=open]:bg-accent data-[state=open]:text-muted-foreground hover:opacity-100 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-ring focus:ring-offset-2 disabled:pointer-events-none">
        <X className="h-4 w-4" />

      className,

    {...props}

      <DropdownMenuPrimitive.ItemIndicator>
        <Circle className="h-2 w-2 fill-current" />
      </DropdownMenuPrimitive.ItemIndicator>
    </span>

);
