import { useCallback, useEffect, useMemo, useState, type ReactNode } from "react";
import { useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";
import { Flag, Layers, ScrollText, Users } from "lucide-react";

import { BattleDispatch } from "@/components/game/BattleDispatch";
import { BattleView } from "@/components/game/BattleView";
import { FieldPanel } from "@/components/game/FieldPanel";
import { PieceIcon } from "@/components/game/PieceSprite";
import { TournamentOverlay } from "@/components/game/TournamentOverlay";
import {
  DiplomacyOverlay,
  HandoffOverlay,
  OccupyOverlay,
  ProposalOverlay,
  TradeOverlay,
  VictoryOverlay,
} from "@/components/game/GameOverlays";
import { MapViewport } from "@/components/game/MapViewport";
import { PlayerRoster } from "@/components/game/PlayerRoster";
import { TopBar } from "@/components/game/TopBar";
import { MAP_VIEW_LABEL, WorldMap, type MapViewMode } from "@/components/game/WorldMap";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { Sheet, SheetContent, SheetHeader, SheetTitle } from "@/components/ui/sheet";
import { Slider } from "@/components/ui/slider";
import { preloadBattleViews } from "@/game/battleViews";
import { computeAttention } from "@/game/camera";
import { electionBudget, influenceSources } from "@/game/engine";
import { TERRITORY_MAP } from "@/game/mapData";
import { PIECE_LABEL, PIECE_VALUES, type PieceType } from "@/game/pieces";
import type { GameAction, TerritoryId } from "@/game/types";
import { playActionSound, useGameSounds } from "@/hooks/useGameSounds";
import { useGame } from "@/state/GameContext";
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";

const LEGEND_PIECES: PieceType[] = ["infantry", "cavalry", "artillery"];

const VIEW_MODES: MapViewMode[] = ["board", "ownership", "threats", "strength", "empire"];

const BATTLE_VIEW_PREF_KEY = "risk2.battleViews";

/** The commander's desk: map, HUD, roster and dispatches. */
const GamePage = () => {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const { game, dispatch: rawDispatch, abandonGame } = useGame();

  // Every human order gets its RISK II sound cue before it hits the engine.
  const dispatch = useCallback(
    (action: GameAction) => {
      playActionSound(action);
      rawDispatch(action);
    },
    [rawDispatch],
  );
  const [selected, setSelected] = useState<TerritoryId | null>(null);
  const [fortifyTarget, setFortifyTarget] = useState<TerritoryId | null>(null);
  const [fortifyCount, setFortifyCount] = useState<number>(1);
  const [deployAmount, setDeployAmount] = useState<number>(1);
  const [allOut, setAllOut] = useState<boolean>(false);
  const [cardsOpen, setCardsOpen] = useState<boolean>(false);
  const [diplomacyOpen, setDiplomacyOpen] = useState<boolean>(false);
  const [viewMode, setViewMode] = useState<MapViewMode>("board");
  const [viewsOpen, setViewsOpen] = useState<boolean>(false);
  const [rosterOpen, setRosterOpen] = useState<boolean>(false);
  const [dispatchOpen, setDispatchOpen] = useState<boolean>(false);
  const [battleViews, setBattleViews] = useState<boolean>(
    () => localStorage.getItem(BATTLE_VIEW_PREF_KEY) !== "off",
  );

  // State-transition sound director: battles, proposals, handoffs, victory.
  useGameSounds(game, battleViews);

  const toggleBattleViews = useCallback(() => {
    setBattleViews((on) => {
      localStorage.setItem(BATTLE_VIEW_PREF_KEY, on ? "off" : "on");
      return !on;
    });
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!game) navigate("/", { replace: true });
  }, [game, navigate]);

  const player = game?.players[game.currentPlayer];
  const isHumanTurn = Boolean(game && player?.isHuman && !game.awaitingHandoff && game.phase !== "gameOver");

  // Clear local selection whenever the turn or phase changes.
  useEffect(() => {
    setSelected(null);
    setFortifyTarget(null);
    setFortifyCount(1);
  }, [game?.currentPlayer, game?.phase]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (game?.mustTrade && isHumanTurn) setCardsOpen(true);
  }, [game?.mustTrade, isHumanTurn]);

  const neighborsOf = useCallback(
    (id: TerritoryId): TerritoryId[] => {
      if (!game) return [];
      const active = new Set(game.activeIds);
      return TERRITORY_MAP[id].neighbors.filter((n) => active.has(n));
    },
    [game],
  );

  const interactive = useMemo(() => {
    const set = new Set<TerritoryId>();
    if (!game || !player || !isHumanTurn) return set;
    if (game.phase === "territoryGrab") {
      for (const id of game.activeIds) {
        if (game.territories[id].owner === -1) set.add(id);
      }
    } else if (game.phase === "initialDeploy") {
      for (const id of game.activeIds) {
        if (game.territories[id].owner === player.id) set.add(id);
      }
    } else if (game.phase === "chooseCapital") {
      for (const id of game.activeIds) {
        if (game.territories[id].owner === player.id) set.add(id);
      }
    } else if (game.phase === "reinforcement" && !game.mustTrade) {
      for (const id of game.activeIds) {
        if (game.territories[id].owner === player.id) set.add(id);
      }
    } else if (game.phase === "attack" && !game.pendingOccupy) {
      for (const id of game.activeIds) {
        const t = game.territories[id];
        if (t.owner === player.id && t.armies >= 2 && neighborsOf(id).some((n) => game.territories[n].owner !== player.id)) {
          set.add(id);
        }
      }
    } else if (game.phase === "fortify") {
      for (const id of game.activeIds) {
        const t = game.territories[id];
        if (t.owner === player.id && t.armies >= 2 && neighborsOf(id).some((n) => game.territories[n].owner === player.id)) {
          set.add(id);
        }
      }
    }
    return set;
  }, [game, player, isHumanTurn, neighborsOf]);

  const targets = useMemo(() => {
    const set = new Set<TerritoryId>();
    if (game?.phase === "election" && game.election) {
      set.add(game.election.territory);
      return set;
    }
    if (!game || !player || !isHumanTurn || !selected) return set;
    if (game.phase === "attack" && !game.pendingOccupy) {
      for (const n of neighborsOf(selected)) {
        if (game.territories[n].owner !== player.id) set.add(n);
      }
    } else if (game.phase === "fortify" && !fortifyTarget) {
      for (const n of neighborsOf(selected)) {
        if (game.territories[n].owner === player.id) set.add(n);
      }
    }
    return set;
  }, [game, player, isHumanTurn, selected, fortifyTarget, neighborsOf]);

  // Warm the fly-to backdrops for every ground the selected army can strike.
  useEffect(() => {
    if (game?.phase === "attack" && targets.size > 0) preloadBattleViews(targets);
  }, [game?.phase, targets]);

  // Attention director: weighted points of interest for the current scene.
  // The MapViewport solves the actual frame at the live viewport aspect.
  const attention = useMemo(() => computeAttention(game, selected), [game, selected]);

  // Scene signature — a change hands the camera back to the auto director.
  const autoKey = game
    ? `${game.phase}|${game.currentPlayer}|${game.pendingOccupy ? "occupy" : ""}|${game.awaitingHandoff ? "handoff" : ""}`
    : "";

  const handleTerritoryClick = useCallback(
    (id: TerritoryId) => {
      if (!game || !player || !isHumanTurn) return;
      if (game.phase === "territoryGrab") {
        if (!interactive.has(id)) return;
        dispatch({ type: "CLAIM_TERRITORY", territory: id });
        return;
      }
      if (game.phase === "initialDeploy") {
        if (!interactive.has(id)) return;
        dispatch({ type: "PLACE_INITIAL", territory: id });
        return;
      }
      if (game.phase === "chooseCapital") {
        if (!interactive.has(id)) return;
        dispatch({ type: "CHOOSE_CAPITAL", territory: id });
        return;
      }
      if (game.phase === "reinforcement") {
        if (!interactive.has(id) || game.mustTrade) return;
        const count = deployAmount === 0 ? game.reinforcementsRemaining : deployAmount;
        dispatch({ type: "DEPLOY", territory: id, count });
        return;
      }
      if (game.phase === "attack") {
        if (game.pendingOccupy) return;
        if (targets.has(id) && selected) {
          dispatch({ type: "ATTACK", from: selected, to: id, allOut });
          return;
        }
        setSelected(interactive.has(id) ? (selected === id ? null : id) : null);
        return;
      }
      if (game.phase === "fortify") {
        if (targets.has(id) && selected) {
          setFortifyTarget(id);
          const max = game.territories[selected].armies - 1;
          setFortifyCount(Math.max(1, max));
          return;
        }
        setFortifyTarget(null);
        setSelected(interactive.has(id) ? (selected === id ? null : id) : null);
      }
    },
    [game, player, isHumanTurn, interactive, targets, selected, deployAmount, allOut, dispatch],
  );

  if (!game || !player) return null;

  const hint = !isHumanTurn
    ? `General ${player.name} is directing the field...`
    : game.phase === "territoryGrab"
      ? "Territory Grab — claim an unowned territory for your banner."
    : game.phase === "election"
      ? "Territory Election — bid Election Points for the highlighted ground, or pass."
    : game.phase === "initialDeploy"
      ? `Initial muster — tap your territories to place your ${game.initialRemaining[player.id] ?? 0} remaining armies.`
    : game.phase === "chooseCapital"
      ? "Choose one of your territories to be your capital city. Defend it with your life."
      : game.phase === "reinforcement"
      ? game.mustTrade
        ? "You must trade cards before mustering."
        : "Tap your territories to place reinforcements."
      : game.phase === "attack"
        ? selected
          ? "Choose an adjacent enemy territory to strike."
          : "Select a territory with 2+ armies to lead the attack."
        : selected
          ? fortifyTarget
            ? "Confirm the manoeuvre below."
            : "Choose an adjacent friendly territory to reinforce."
          : "Select a territory to move armies from, or hold positions.";

  return (
    <div className="relative h-dvh overflow-hidden">
      {/* Full-bleed board — every other panel is minimized and floats over it */}
      <div className="absolute inset-0 px-1 pb-9 pt-12">
        <MapViewport className="h-full w-full" attention={attention} autoKey={autoKey}>
          <WorldMap
            game={game}
            selected={selected}
            targets={targets}
            interactive={interactive}
            viewMode={viewMode}
            onTerritoryClick={handleTerritoryClick}
          />
        </MapViewport>
      </div>

      <TopBar
        game={game}
        dispatch={dispatch}
        deployAmount={deployAmount}
        onDeployAmountChange={setDeployAmount}
        onOpenCards={() => setCardsOpen(true)}
        onOpenDiplomacy={() => setDiplomacyOpen(true)}
        allOut={allOut}
        onAllOutChange={setAllOut}
      />

      {/* Left rail — collapsed panels */}
      <div className="absolute bottom-9 left-2 z-20 flex flex-col items-start gap-1">
        {viewsOpen && (
          <div
            role="tablist"
            aria-label="Map view"
            className="flex flex-col gap-0.5 rounded-sm border border-gold-dim/50 bg-[hsl(28_35%_12%/0.88)] p-1 shadow-md backdrop-blur-[2px]"
          >
            {VIEW_MODES.map((mode) => (
              <button
                key={mode}
                type="button"
                role="tab"
                aria-selected={viewMode === mode}
                onClick={() => {
                  setViewMode(mode);
                  setViewsOpen(false);
                }}
                className={cn(
                  "border px-2 py-1 text-left font-display text-[10px] uppercase tracking-widest transition-colors",
                  viewMode === mode
                    ? "border-gold bg-gold/15 text-gold"
                    : "border-transparent text-[hsl(45_45%_72%)] hover:text-gold",
                )}
              >
                {MAP_VIEW_LABEL[mode]}
              </button>
            ))}
            <div aria-hidden className="my-0.5 h-px bg-gold-dim/40" />
            <button
              type="button"
              role="switch"
              aria-checked={battleViews}
              onClick={toggleBattleViews}
              className={cn(
                "border px-2 py-1 text-left font-display text-[10px] uppercase tracking-widest transition-colors",
                battleViews
                  ? "border-gold bg-gold/15 text-gold"
                  : "border-transparent text-[hsl(45_45%_72%)] hover:text-gold",
              )}
            >
              Battle View: {battleViews ? "On" : "Off"}
            </button>
          </div>
        )}
        <RailButton
          active={viewsOpen || viewMode !== "board"}
          label="Map views"
          onClick={() => setViewsOpen((open) => !open)}
        >
          <Layers className="h-4 w-4" />
        </RailButton>
        <RailButton label="Field commanders" onClick={() => setRosterOpen(true)}>
          <Users className="h-4 w-4" />
        </RailButton>
        <RailButton label="Field dispatch" onClick={() => setDispatchOpen(true)}>
          <ScrollText className="h-4 w-4" />
        </RailButton>
      </div>

      {/* Slim order-of-the-day strip */}
      <div className="pointer-events-none absolute inset-x-0 bottom-0 z-10 flex justify-center px-2 pb-1.5">
        <p
          aria-live="polite"
          className="rounded-sm border border-gold-dim/40 bg-[hsl(28_35%_12%/0.78)] px-3 py-1 text-center font-body text-xs italic leading-snug text-[hsl(45_60%_82%)] shadow-md backdrop-blur-[2px]"
        >
          {hint}
        </p>
      </div>

      {game.phase === "election" && game.election && (
        <FieldPanel className="absolute inset-x-2 bottom-9 z-30 mx-auto max-w-md">
              <p className="font-display text-[10px] uppercase tracking-imperial text-muted-foreground">
                Territory Election — {game.election.queue.length} remain on the docket
              </p>
              <p className="mt-1 font-body text-lg font-semibold">
                {TERRITORY_MAP[game.election.territory].name}
              </p>
              <p className="font-body text-sm text-muted-foreground" aria-live="polite">
                {game.election.highBidder !== null
                  ? `Current bid: ${game.election.bid} points by ${game.players[game.election.highBidder]?.name ?? "?"}`
                  : "No bids yet — unclaimed ground goes by lot."}
              </p>
              <div className="mt-2 flex flex-wrap gap-x-4 gap-y-1">
                {game.players.map((p) => (
                  <span key={p.id} className="flex items-center gap-1.5 font-body text-xs">
                    <span
                      aria-hidden
                      className="h-2.5 w-2.5 rounded-full border border-[#3a2812]"
                      style={{ backgroundColor: p.color }}
                    />
                    <span className={cn(game.currentPlayer === p.id && "font-bold text-gold")}>
                      {p.name}: {game.election?.points[p.id] ?? 0}
                      {game.election?.passed.includes(p.id) ? " (passed)" : ""}
                    </span>
                  </span>
                ))}
              </div>
              {isHumanTurn && !game.election.passed.includes(player.id) && game.election.highBidder !== player.id ? (
                <>
                  <p className="mt-2 font-body text-xs italic text-muted-foreground">
                    {influenceSources(game, player.id, game.election.territory).length > 0
                      ? `${influenceSources(game, player.id, game.election.territory).length} neighbouring ${
                          influenceSources(game, player.id, game.election.territory).length === 1
                            ? "holding lends"
                            : "holdings lend"
                        } ${influenceSources(game, player.id, game.election.territory).length * 10} points of one-time influence.`
                      : "No neighbouring holdings — every point comes from your war chest."}
                  </p>
                  <div className="mt-3 flex gap-2">
                    {([5, 10] as const).map((raise) => (
                      <Button
                        key={raise}
                        className="flex-1 font-display text-xs uppercase tracking-imperial"
                        disabled={(game.election?.bid ?? 0) + raise > electionBudget(game, player.id)}
                        onClick={() => dispatch({ type: "ELECTION_BID", raise })}
                      >
                        Bid {(game.election?.bid ?? 0) + raise}
                      </Button>
                    ))}
                    <Button
                      variant="outline"
                      className="flex-1 font-display text-xs uppercase tracking-imperial"
                      onClick={() => dispatch({ type: "ELECTION_PASS" })}
                    >
                      Pass
                    </Button>
                  </div>
                </>
              ) : (
                <p className="mt-2 font-body text-xs italic text-muted-foreground" aria-live="polite">
                  {game.election.highBidder === player.id && player.isHuman
                    ? "You hold the highest bid — awaiting the other commanders."
                    : `Awaiting ${game.players[game.currentPlayer]?.name ?? "the floor"}...`}
                </p>
              )}
            </FieldPanel>
      )}

      {isHumanTurn && game.phase === "fortify" && selected && fortifyTarget && (
        <FieldPanel className="absolute inset-x-2 bottom-9 z-30 mx-auto max-w-md">
              <p className="font-body text-sm">
                March from <span className="font-semibold">{TERRITORY_MAP[selected].name}</span> to{" "}
                <span className="font-semibold">{TERRITORY_MAP[fortifyTarget].name}</span>
              </p>
              <div className="mt-3 flex items-center gap-3">
                <Slider
                  min={1}
                  max={Math.max(1, game.territories[selected].armies - 1)}
                  step={1}
                  value={[fortifyCount]}
                  onValueChange={(value) => setFortifyCount(value[0] ?? 1)}
                />
                <span className="w-8 text-right font-display text-lg font-bold text-gold">{fortifyCount}</span>
              </div>
              <div className="mt-3 flex gap-2">
                <Button
                  className="flex-1 gap-1.5 font-display text-xs uppercase tracking-imperial"
                  onClick={() => dispatch({ type: "FORTIFY", from: selected, to: fortifyTarget, count: fortifyCount })}
                >
                  <Flag className="h-3.5 w-3.5" /> Manoeuvre & End Turn
                </Button>
                <Button
                  variant="outline"
                  className="font-display text-xs uppercase tracking-imperial"
                  onClick={() => setFortifyTarget(null)}
                >
                  Cancel
                </Button>
              </div>
            </FieldPanel>
      )}

      <Sheet open={rosterOpen} onOpenChange={setRosterOpen}>
        <SheetContent side="left" className="flex w-80 flex-col gap-3 overflow-y-auto p-3 pt-10">
          <SheetHeader className="sr-only">
            <SheetTitle>Field Commanders</SheetTitle>
          </SheetHeader>
          <PlayerRoster game={game} />
          <FieldPanel>
            <p className="mb-2 font-display text-[10px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-imperial text-muted-foreground">
              Piece Values
            </p>
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-2" aria-label="Piece values">
              {LEGEND_PIECES.map((type) => (
                <span key={type} className="flex items-center gap-1">
                  <PieceIcon type={type} color="#6b4a26" size={24} />
                  <span className="font-display text-[10px] uppercase tracking-widest text-muted-foreground">
                    {PIECE_LABEL[type]} = {PIECE_VALUES[type]}
                  </span>
                </span>
              ))}
            </div>
          </FieldPanel>
        </SheetContent>
      </Sheet>

      <Sheet open={dispatchOpen} onOpenChange={setDispatchOpen}>
        <SheetContent side="left" className="flex w-80 flex-col p-3 pt-10">
          <SheetHeader className="sr-only">
            <SheetTitle>Field Dispatch</SheetTitle>
          </SheetHeader>
          <div className="flex min-h-0 flex-1 flex-col">
            <BattleDispatch game={game} />
          </div>
        </SheetContent>
      </Sheet>

      <BattleView game={game} enabled={battleViews} />
      <HandoffOverlay game={game} dispatch={dispatch} />
      <OccupyOverlay game={game} dispatch={dispatch} />
      <DiplomacyOverlay game={game} dispatch={dispatch} open={diplomacyOpen} onClose={() => setDiplomacyOpen(false)} />
      <ProposalOverlay game={game} dispatch={dispatch} />
      <TradeOverlay game={game} dispatch={dispatch} open={cardsOpen || (game.mustTrade && isHumanTurn)} onClose={() => setCardsOpen(false)} />
      {game.setup.tournamentGame !== undefined ? (
        <TournamentOverlay game={game} />
      ) : (
        <VictoryOverlay game={game} onExit={abandonGame} />
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

/** Compact floating toggle matching the map's camera buttons. */
function RailButton({
  active,
  label,
  onClick,
  children,
}: {
  active?: boolean;
  label: string;
  onClick: () => void;
  children: ReactNode;
}) {
  return (
    <button
      type="button"
      aria-label={label}
      title={label}
      aria-pressed={active}
      onClick={onClick}
      className={cn(
        "flex h-9 w-9 items-center justify-center rounded-sm border shadow-md backdrop-blur-[2px] transition-colors",
        active
          ? "border-gold bg-gold/25 text-gold"
          : "border-gold-dim/50 bg-[hsl(28_35%_12%/0.72)] text-[hsl(45_60%_80%)] hover:border-gold hover:text-gold",
      )}
    >
      {children}
    </button>
  );
}

export default GamePage;

File: /web/src/pages/Index.tsx

import { useState } from "react";
import { useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";
import { Landmark, Lock, ScrollText, Swords, Trophy } from "lucide-react";
import { toast } from "sonner";

import { FieldPanel, ImperialDivider } from "@/components/game/FieldPanel";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { OBJECTIVE_INFO } from "@/game/types";
import { ART } from "@/lib/art";
import { useGame } from "@/state/GameContext";
import { usePremium } from "@/state/PremiumContext";

/** Main menu — the "Anno Domini MDCCCXII" heraldic hall. */
const Index = () => {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const { game, savedSummary, resumeSavedGame } = useGame();
  const { isPremium, openPaywall } = usePremium();
  const [resuming, setResuming] = useState<boolean>(false);

  const activeGame = game && game.phase !== "gameOver" ? game : null;
  const continueMeta = activeGame
    ? {
        turn: activeGame.turn,
        objective: OBJECTIVE_INFO[activeGame.setup.objective].name,
        names: activeGame.players.filter((p) => p.alive).map((p) => p.name),
      }
    : savedSummary
      ? {
          turn: savedSummary.turn,
          objective: OBJECTIVE_INFO[savedSummary.objective]?.name ?? "Campaign",
          names: savedSummary.playerNames,
        }
      : null;

  const handleContinue = async () => {
    if (activeGame) {
      navigate("/game");
      return;
    }
    setResuming(true);
    const restored = await resumeSavedGame();
    setResuming(false);
    if (restored) {
      navigate("/game");
    } else {
      toast.error("The saved campaign could not be restored.");
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="flex min-h-screen flex-col items-center justify-center px-4 py-10">
      <main className="w-full max-w-lg animate-fade-up text-center">
        <img
          src={ART.warCrest}
          alt=""
          aria-hidden
          className="mx-auto mb-4 h-32 w-32 object-contain drop-shadow-[0_4px_10px_rgba(0,0,0,0.6)]"
        />

        <p className="text-on-wood-muted font-display text-xs uppercase tracking-imperial">
          Anno Domini MDCCCXII
        </p>
        <h1 className="text-gilded mt-2 font-display text-5xl font-black leading-tight sm:text-6xl">
          World
          <span className="text-gilded-crimson block">Domination</span>
        </h1>

        <ImperialDivider className="mx-auto my-6 max-w-xs" />

        <figure
          className="mx-auto mb-6 max-w-md overflow-hidden rounded-sm border-4 border-double border-gold/60 bg-black/40 shadow-[0_10px_30px_rgba(0,0,0,0.7),inset_0_0_0_2px_rgba(0,0,0,0.5)]"
          aria-hidden
        >
          <img
            src={ART.heroPainting}
            alt=""
            className="block aspect-[3/2] w-full object-cover"
            loading="eager"
            decoding="async"
          />
        </figure>

        <p className="text-on-wood-muted mx-auto max-w-md font-body text-base italic leading-relaxed">
          A Napoleonic campaign of global conquest. Muster your regiments, command the field with dice and
          diplomacy, and bend every continent to your banner.
        </p>

        <div className="mx-auto mt-8 flex max-w-xs flex-col gap-3">
          {continueMeta && (
            <div>
              <Button
                size="lg"
                className="h-12 w-full gap-2 font-display text-sm font-bold uppercase tracking-imperial"
                onClick={handleContinue}
                disabled={resuming}
              >
                <Swords className="h-4 w-4" /> {resuming ? "Restoring..." : "Continue Campaign"}
              </Button>
              <p className="text-on-wood-muted mt-1.5 font-body text-xs italic">
                Turn {continueMeta.turn} — {continueMeta.objective} · {continueMeta.names.slice(0, 3).join(", ")}
                {continueMeta.names.length > 3 ? "…" : ""}
              </p>
            </div>
          )}
          <Button
            size="lg"
            variant={continueMeta ? "outline" : "default"}
            className="h-12 gap-2 font-display text-sm font-bold uppercase tracking-imperial"
            onClick={() => navigate("/setup")}
          >
            <Swords className="h-4 w-4" /> New Campaign
          </Button>
          <Button
            size="lg"
            variant="outline"
            className="h-12 gap-2 font-display text-sm font-bold uppercase tracking-imperial"
            onClick={() => (isPremium ? navigate("/tournament") : openPaywall())}
          >
            <Trophy className="h-4 w-4" /> Tournament
            {!isPremium && <Lock className="h-3 w-3 text-muted-foreground" aria-label="Premium" />}
          </Button>
          <Button
            size="lg"
            variant="outline"
            className="h-12 gap-2 font-display text-sm font-bold uppercase tracking-imperial"
            onClick={() => navigate("/records")}
          >
            <Landmark className="h-4 w-4" /> Hall of Records
          </Button>
        </div>

        <FieldPanel className="mt-10 text-left">
          <div className="mb-2 flex items-center gap-2">
            <ScrollText className="h-4 w-4 text-gold" />
            <h2 className="font-display text-[11px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-imperial text-muted-foreground">
              Rules of Engagement
            </h2>
          </div>
          <ul className="space-y-1.5 font-body text-sm leading-snug text-muted-foreground">
            <li>
              <span className="font-semibold text-foreground">I. Muster</span> — receive reinforcements for
              territories held and continents controlled; trade card sets for extra armies.
            </li>
            <li>
              <span className="font-semibold text-foreground">II. Engagement</span> — attack adjacent enemy
              territories. Dice decide the field; conquer to earn a Risk card.
            </li>
            <li>
              <span className="font-semibold text-foreground">III. Manoeuvre</span> — make one fortifying march
              between adjacent territories, then yield the turn.
            </li>
            <li className="pt-1 italic">
              Hot-seat multiplayer: share one device among up to six commanders — human or any of sixteen AI
              generals. Campaigns are saved automatically and archived in the Hall of Records.
            </li>
          </ul>
        </FieldPanel>
      </main>
    </div>
  );
};

export default Index;

import { useEffect } from "react";
import { useLocation } from "react-router-dom";

const NotFound = () => {
  const location = useLocation();

  useEffect(() => {
    console.error("404 Error: User attempted to access non-existent route:", location.pathname);
  }, [location.pathname]);

  return (
    <div className="flex min-h-screen items-center justify-center bg-muted">
      <div className="text-center">
        <h1 className="mb-4 text-4xl font-bold">404</h1>
        <p className="mb-4 text-xl text-muted-foreground">Oops! Page not found</p>
        <a href="/" className="text-primary underline hover:text-primary/90">
          Return to Home
        </a>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

File: /web/src/pages/RecordsPage.tsx
---

import { useQuery } from "@tanstack/react-query";
import { format } from "date-fns";
import { ArrowLeft, Bot, Landmark, Trophy, User } from "lucide-react";
import { useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";

import { FieldPanel, ImperialDivider, SectionHeader } from "@/components/game/FieldPanel";
import { listCampaigns, listCommanderStats } from "@/db/repository";
import { OBJECTIVE_INFO } from "@/game/types";
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";

function formatDate(iso: string): string {
  const date = new Date(iso);
  return Number.isNaN(date.getTime()) ? "—" : format(date, "d MMM yyyy, HH:mm");
}

/** "Hall of Records" — the campaign archive and lifetime commander ledger. */
const RecordsPage = () => {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const campaignsQuery = useQuery({ queryKey: ["campaigns"], queryFn: () => listCampaigns() });
  const commandersQuery = useQuery({ queryKey: ["commander-stats"], queryFn: () => listCommanderStats() });

  const campaigns = campaignsQuery.data ?? [];
  const commanders = commandersQuery.data ?? [];
  const humanWins = campaigns.filter((c) => c.winnerIsHuman).length;
  const aiWins = campaigns.length - humanWins;
  const longest = campaigns.reduce((max, c) => Math.max(max, c.turns), 0);

  return (
    <div className="mx-auto min-h-screen w-full max-w-2xl px-4 py-8">
      <button
        type="button"
        onClick={() => navigate("/")}
        className="text-on-wood-muted mb-4 flex items-center gap-1.5 font-display text-[11px] uppercase tracking-imperial transition-colors hover:text-gold"
      >
        <ArrowLeft className="h-3.5 w-3.5" /> Main Hall
      </button>

      <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
        <Landmark className="h-7 w-7 text-[hsl(42_62%_66%)] drop-shadow-[0_1px_2px_rgba(0,0,0,0.7)]" />
        <h1 className="text-gilded font-display text-3xl font-black">Hall of Records</h1>
      </div>
      <p className="text-on-wood-muted mt-1 font-body text-sm italic">
        Every concluded campaign, engraved in the imperial ledger.
      </p>
      <ImperialDivider className="my-5" />

      <FieldPanel className="animate-fade-up">
        <SectionHeader index={1} title="Campaign Ledger" />
        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3 sm:grid-cols-4">
          {[
            { label: "Campaigns", value: campaigns.length },
            { label: "Human Victories", value: humanWins },
            { label: "AI Victories", value: aiWins },
            { label: "Longest (turns)", value: longest },
          ].map((stat) => (
            <div key={stat.label} className="border border-gold-dim/40 bg-background/40 p-2.5 text-center">
              <p className="font-display text-2xl font-black text-gold">{stat.value}</p>
              <p className="mt-0.5 font-display text-[9px] uppercase tracking-imperial text-muted-foreground">
                {stat.label}
              </p>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      </FieldPanel>

      <FieldPanel className="mt-4 animate-fade-up">
        <SectionHeader index={2} title="Commanders of Renown" />
        {commanders.length === 0 ? (
          <p className="font-body text-sm italic text-muted-foreground">
            No commander has yet concluded a campaign.
          </p>
        ) : (
          <ul className="space-y-1">
            {commanders.slice(0, 10).map((commander, i) => (
              <li
                key={commander.name}
                className={cn(
                  "flex items-center gap-2 px-2 py-1.5",
                  i === 0 && commander.wins > 0 && "border border-gold-dim/60 bg-gold/10",
                )}
              >
                <span className="w-6 font-display text-[11px] font-bold text-gold">{i + 1}.</span>
                <span className="min-w-0 flex-1 truncate font-body text-sm font-semibold">{commander.name}</span>
                {commander.isHuman ? (
                  <User className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-muted-foreground" aria-label="Human" />
                ) : (
                  <Bot className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-muted-foreground" aria-label="AI general" />
                )}
                <span className="w-24 text-right font-display text-[11px] text-muted-foreground">
                  {commander.wins} {commander.wins === 1 ? "win" : "wins"} / {commander.games}
                </span>
              </li>
            ))}
          </ul>
        )}
      </FieldPanel>

      <FieldPanel className="mt-4 animate-fade-up">
        <SectionHeader index={3} title="Campaign Archive" />
        {campaignsQuery.isLoading ? (
          <p className="font-body text-sm italic text-muted-foreground">Consulting the archives...</p>
        ) : campaigns.length === 0 ? (
          <p className="font-body text-sm italic text-muted-foreground">
            The archive is empty. Conclude a campaign and history shall remember it.
          </p>
        ) : (
          <ul className="space-y-2">
            {campaigns.map((campaign) => (
              <li key={campaign.id} className="border border-gold-dim/40 bg-background/40 p-2.5">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                  <span
                    aria-hidden
                    className="h-3.5 w-3.5 shrink-0 rounded-full border border-[#3a2812] shadow-[inset_-1px_-1px_1px_rgba(0,0,0,0.3),inset_1px_1px_1px_rgba(255,255,255,0.4)]"
                    style={{ backgroundColor: campaign.winnerColor }}
                  />
                  <span className="min-w-0 flex-1 truncate font-body text-sm font-semibold">
                    {campaign.winnerName}
                  </span>
                  <Trophy className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-gold" aria-hidden />
                  <span className="font-display text-[10px] uppercase tracking-widest text-muted-foreground">
                    {OBJECTIVE_INFO[campaign.objective]?.name ?? campaign.objective}
                  </span>
                </div>
                <p className="mt-1 font-body text-xs italic text-muted-foreground">
                  {campaign.winReason ? `Victory by ${campaign.winReason}. ` : ""}
                  {campaign.turns} turns · {campaign.playerCount} commanders · {campaign.battles} battles ·{" "}
                  {campaign.territoryCount} territories
                </p>
                <p className="mt-0.5 font-display text-[9px] uppercase tracking-imperial text-muted-foreground/70">
                  {formatDate(campaign.completedAt)}
                </p>
              </li>
            ))}
          </ul>
        )}
      </FieldPanel>
    </div>
  );
};

export default RecordsPage;

File: /web/src/pages/SetupPage.tsx
---

import { useMemo, useState } from "react";
import { useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";
import { ArrowLeft, Bot, Minus, Plus, User } from "lucide-react";

import { FieldPanel, ImperialDivider, SectionHeader } from "@/components/game/FieldPanel";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { Input } from "@/components/ui/input";
import { Switch } from "@/components/ui/switch";
import { GENERAL_LIST, GENERALS } from "@/game/generals";
import type { Allocation, CardRule, GeneralId, Objective, PlayerSetup } from "@/game/types";
import { ALLOCATION_INFO, CARD_RULE_INFO, OBJECTIVE_INFO, PLAYER_COLORS } from "@/game/types";
import { useGame } from "@/state/GameContext";
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";

const OBJECTIVES: Objective[] = ["domination100", "domination80", "domination60", "capital", "mission"];

const CARD_RULES: CardRule[] = ["ascending", "ascendingByOne", "setValue"];

const ALLOCATIONS: Allocation[] = ["random", "grab", "election"];

const DEFAULT_GENERALS: GeneralId[] = ["wellington", "bonaparte", "marmont", "dErlon", "vauban"];

function defaultPlayers(): PlayerSetup[] {
  return [
    { name: "You", colorIdx: 0, isHuman: true, generalId: null },
    { name: "Wellington", colorIdx: 1, isHuman: false, generalId: "wellington" },
    { name: "Bonaparte", colorIdx: 2, isHuman: false, generalId: "bonaparte" },
  ];
}

/** "Orders of Battle" campaign briefing screen. */
const SetupPage = () => {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const { startGame } = useGame();
  const [players, setPlayers] = useState<PlayerSetup[]>(defaultPlayers());
  const [objective, setObjective] = useState<Objective>("domination100");
  const [cardRule, setCardRule] = useState<CardRule>("ascending");
  const [allocation, setAllocation] = useState<Allocation>("random");
  const [useExtra, setUseExtra] = useState<boolean>(false);
  const [generalPickerFor, setGeneralPickerFor] = useState<number | null>(null);

  const usedColors = useMemo(() => players.map((p) => p.colorIdx), [players]);

  const updatePlayer = (index: number, patch: Partial<PlayerSetup>) => {
    setPlayers((prev) => prev.map((p, i) => (i === index ? { ...p, ...patch } : p)));
  };

  const addPlayer = () => {
    setPlayers((prev) => {
      if (prev.length >= 8) return prev;
      const colorIdx = PLAYER_COLORS.findIndex((_, i) => !prev.some((p) => p.colorIdx === i));
      const generalId = DEFAULT_GENERALS[prev.length % DEFAULT_GENERALS.length] ?? "spencer";
      const general = GENERALS[generalId];
      return [...prev, { name: general.name, colorIdx: Math.max(0, colorIdx), isHuman: false, generalId }];
    });
  };

  const removePlayer = () => {
    setPlayers((prev) => (prev.length > 2 ? prev.slice(0, -1) : prev));
  };

  const cycleColor = (index: number) => {
    const player = players[index];
    if (!player) return;
    let next = (player.colorIdx + 1) % PLAYER_COLORS.length;
    while (usedColors.includes(next) && next !== player.colorIdx) {
      next = (next + 1) % PLAYER_COLORS.length;
    }
    updatePlayer(index, { colorIdx: next });
  };

  const commence = () => {
    startGame({ players, objective, useExtraTerritories: useExtra, cardRule, allocation });
    navigate("/game");
  };

  return (
    <div className="mx-auto min-h-screen w-full max-w-2xl px-4 py-8">
      <button
        type="button"
        onClick={() => navigate("/")}
        className="text-on-wood-muted mb-4 flex items-center gap-1.5 font-display text-[11px] uppercase tracking-imperial transition-colors hover:text-gold"
      >
        <ArrowLeft className="h-3.5 w-3.5" /> Main Hall
      </button>

      <h1 className="text-gilded font-display text-3xl font-black">Orders of Battle</h1>
      <p className="text-on-wood-muted mt-1 font-body text-sm italic">
        Assemble your commanders and choose the terms of victory.
      </p>
      <ImperialDivider className="my-5" />

      <FieldPanel className="animate-fade-up">
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
          <SectionHeader index={1} title="Commanders" className="mb-0 flex-1" />
          <div className="ml-3 flex items-center gap-1">
            <Button size="icon" variant="outline" className="h-7 w-7" onClick={removePlayer} disabled={players.length <= 2} aria-label="Remove commander">
              <Minus className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
            </Button>
            <span className="w-6 text-center font-display text-sm font-bold text-gold">{players.length}</span>
            <Button size="icon" variant="outline" className="h-7 w-7" onClick={addPlayer} disabled={players.length >= 8} aria-label="Add commander">
              <Plus className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
            </Button>
          </div>
        </div>

        <ul className="mt-3 space-y-2">
          {players.map((player, i) => (
            <li key={i} className="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-2 rounded border border-gold-dim/40 bg-background/50 p-2">
              <button
                type="button"
                onClick={() => cycleColor(i)}
                aria-label={`Change color for commander ${i + 1}`}
                className="h-6 w-6 rounded-full border-2 border-[#3a2812] shadow-[inset_-1px_-2px_2px_rgba(0,0,0,0.3),inset_1px_1px_2px_rgba(255,255,255,0.4)] transition-transform hover:scale-110"
                style={{ backgroundColor: PLAYER_COLORS[player.colorIdx]?.hex ?? "#e63333" }}
              />
              <Input
                value={player.name}
                onChange={(e) => updatePlayer(i, { name: e.target.value })}
                className="h-8 w-36 flex-1 border-gold-dim/50 bg-transparent font-body"
                maxLength={16}
                aria-label={`Commander ${i + 1} name`}
              />
              <Button
                size="sm"
                variant="outline"
                className="h-8 gap-1.5 font-display text-[10px] uppercase tracking-widest"
                onClick={() => {
                  if (player.isHuman) {
                    const generalId = player.generalId ?? DEFAULT_GENERALS[i % DEFAULT_GENERALS.length] ?? "spencer";
                    updatePlayer(i, { isHuman: false, generalId, name: GENERALS[generalId].name });
                  } else {
                    updatePlayer(i, { isHuman: true });
                  }
                }}
              >
                {player.isHuman ? <User className="h-3 w-3" /> : <Bot className="h-3 w-3" />}
                {player.isHuman ? "Human" : "AI"}
              </Button>
              {!player.isHuman && (
                <button
                  type="button"
                  onClick={() => setGeneralPickerFor(generalPickerFor === i ? null : i)}
                  className="border border-gold-dim/50 px-2 py-1 font-body text-xs text-gold transition-colors hover:bg-gold/10"
                >
                  Gen. {player.generalId ? GENERALS[player.generalId].name : "—"}{" "}
                  <span className="text-muted-foreground">
                    {"★".repeat(player.generalId ? GENERALS[player.generalId].difficulty : 0)}
                  </span>
                </button>
              )}
              {generalPickerFor === i && !player.isHuman && (
                <div className="w-full border border-gold-dim/40 bg-background/60 p-2">
                  <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-1.5 sm:grid-cols-4">
                    {GENERAL_LIST.map((general) => (
                      <button
                        key={general.id}
                        type="button"
                        title={general.description}
                        onClick={() => {
                          updatePlayer(i, { generalId: general.id, name: general.name });
                          setGeneralPickerFor(null);
                        }}
                        className={cn(
                          "border p-1.5 text-left transition-colors",
                          player.generalId === general.id
                            ? "border-gold bg-gold/15"
                            : "border-gold-dim/40 hover:bg-gold/5",
                        )}
                      >
                        <p className="font-display text-[10px] font-bold uppercase">{general.name}</p>
                        <p className="text-[9px] text-gold">{"★".repeat(general.difficulty)}</p>
                      </button>
                    ))}
                  </div>
                  {player.generalId && (
                    <p className="mt-1.5 font-body text-xs italic text-muted-foreground">
                      {GENERALS[player.generalId].description}
                    </p>
                  )}
                </div>
              )}
            </li>
          ))}
        </ul>
      </FieldPanel>

      <FieldPanel className="mt-4 animate-fade-up">
        <SectionHeader index={2} title="Terms of Victory" />
        <div className="grid gap-2 sm:grid-cols-2">
          {OBJECTIVES.map((obj) => (
            <button
              key={obj}
              type="button"
              onClick={() => setObjective(obj)}
              className={cn(
                "border p-2.5 text-left transition-colors",
                objective === obj ? "border-gold bg-gold/15" : "border-gold-dim/40 hover:bg-gold/5",
              )}
            >
              <p className="font-display text-[11px] font-bold uppercase tracking-widest">
                {OBJECTIVE_INFO[obj].name}
              </p>
              <p className="mt-0.5 font-body text-xs text-muted-foreground">{OBJECTIVE_INFO[obj].description}</p>
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>
      </FieldPanel>

      <FieldPanel className="mt-4 animate-fade-up">
        <SectionHeader index={3} title="Card Trading" />
        <div className="grid gap-2 sm:grid-cols-3">
          {CARD_RULES.map((rule) => (
            <button
              key={rule}
              type="button"
              onClick={() => setCardRule(rule)}
              className={cn(
                "border p-2.5 text-left transition-colors",
                cardRule === rule ? "border-gold bg-gold/15" : "border-gold-dim/40 hover:bg-gold/5",
              )}
            >
              <p className="font-display text-[11px] font-bold uppercase tracking-widest">
                {CARD_RULE_INFO[rule].name}
              </p>
              <p className="mt-0.5 font-body text-xs text-muted-foreground">{CARD_RULE_INFO[rule].description}</p>
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>
      </FieldPanel>

      <FieldPanel className="mt-4 animate-fade-up">
        <SectionHeader index={4} title="Territory Allocation" />
        <div className="grid gap-2 sm:grid-cols-2">
          {ALLOCATIONS.map((option) => (
            <button
              key={option}
              type="button"
              onClick={() => setAllocation(option)}
              className={cn(
                "border p-2.5 text-left transition-colors",
                allocation === option ? "border-gold bg-gold/15" : "border-gold-dim/40 hover:bg-gold/5",
              )}
            >
              <p className="font-display text-[11px] font-bold uppercase tracking-widest">
                {ALLOCATION_INFO[option].name}
              </p>
              <p className="mt-0.5 font-body text-xs text-muted-foreground">{ALLOCATION_INFO[option].description}</p>
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>
      </FieldPanel>

      <FieldPanel className="mt-4 animate-fade-up">
        <SectionHeader index={5} title="Theatre of War" />
        <label className="flex cursor-pointer items-center justify-between gap-3">
          <span className="font-body text-sm text-muted-foreground">
            Extended map — add Hawaii, Svalbard, the Philippines, the Falklands, Madagascar and New Zealand (48
            territories).
          </span>
          <Switch checked={useExtra} onCheckedChange={setUseExtra} aria-label="Toggle extended map" />
        </label>
      </FieldPanel>

      <Button
        size="lg"
        className="mt-6 h-12 w-full font-display text-sm font-bold uppercase tracking-imperial"
        onClick={commence}
      >
        Commence Campaign
      </Button>
    </div>
  );
};

export default SetupPage;

File: /web/src/pages/TournamentPage.tsx

import { useState } from "react";
import { useMutation, useQuery, useQueryClient } from "@tanstack/react-query";
import { ArrowLeft, Bot, Check, Crown, Lock, Medal, Swords, Trophy, User } from "lucide-react";
import { useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";

import { FieldPanel, ImperialDivider, SectionHeader } from "@/components/game/FieldPanel";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { Input } from "@/components/ui/input";
import {
  clearTournamentProgress,
  getTournamentProgress,
  listHighScores,
  saveTournamentProgress,
  submitHighScore,
} from "@/db/repository";
import { GENERALS } from "@/game/generals";
import {
  buildTournamentSetup,
  TOURNAMENT_GAMES,
  TOURNAMENT_LENGTH,
  tournamentMaxPoints,
} from "@/game/tournament";
import { ALLOCATION_INFO, OBJECTIVE_INFO } from "@/game/types";
import { useGame } from "@/state/GameContext";
import { usePremium } from "@/state/PremiumContext";
import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";

/** The RISK II Tournament hall — 16-game ladder, progress and high scores. */
const TournamentPage = () => {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const queryClient = useQueryClient();
  const { startGame } = useGame();
  const { isPremium, isLoading: premiumLoading, openPaywall } = usePremium();
  const [name, setName] = useState<string>("");

  const progressQuery = useQuery({ queryKey: ["tournament"], queryFn: () => getTournamentProgress() });
  const scoresQuery = useQuery({ queryKey: ["high-scores"], queryFn: () => listHighScores() });

  const progress = progressQuery.data ?? null;
  const currentGame = progress?.currentGame ?? 1;
  const currentDef = TOURNAMENT_GAMES[currentGame - 1] ?? TOURNAMENT_GAMES[0];

  const startMutation = useMutation({
    mutationFn: async () => {
      const commanderName = progress?.name ?? (name.trim() === "" ? "You" : name.trim());
      if (!progress) {
        await saveTournamentProgress({ name: commanderName, currentGame: 1, totalPoints: 0 });
      }
      return commanderName;
    },
    onSuccess: (commanderName) => {
      queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ["tournament"] });
      if (currentDef) {
        startGame(buildTournamentSetup(currentDef, commanderName));
        navigate("/game");
      }
    },
  });

  const resignMutation = useMutation({
    mutationFn: async () => {
      if (!progress) return;
      if (progress.totalPoints > 0) {
        await submitHighScore(progress.name, progress.totalPoints, progress.currentGame - 1);
      }
      await clearTournamentProgress();
    },
    onSuccess: () => {
      queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ["tournament"] });
      queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ["high-scores"] });
    },
  });

  const scores = scoresQuery.data ?? [];

  return (
    <div className="mx-auto min-h-screen w-full max-w-2xl px-4 py-8">
      <button
        type="button"
        onClick={() => navigate("/")}
        className="text-on-wood-muted mb-4 flex items-center gap-1.5 font-display text-[11px] uppercase tracking-imperial transition-colors hover:text-gold"
      >
        <ArrowLeft className="h-3.5 w-3.5" /> Main Hall
      </button>

      <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
        <Trophy className="h-7 w-7 text-[hsl(42_62%_66%)] drop-shadow-[0_1px_2px_rgba(0,0,0,0.7)]" />
        <h1 className="text-gilded font-display text-3xl font-black">The Tournament</h1>
      </div>
      <p className="text-on-wood-muted mt-1 font-body text-sm italic">
        Sixteen campaigns in sequence, designed by die-hard RISK stalwarts. Fall in battle and the
        tournament ends — win, or destroy at least one rival, to advance.
      </p>
      <ImperialDivider className="my-5" />

      {!isPremium && !premiumLoading && (
        <FieldPanel className="animate-fade-up mb-4 text-center">
          <Crown className="mx-auto h-6 w-6 text-gold" aria-hidden />
          <p className="mt-1.5 font-body text-sm text-muted-foreground">
            The Tournament is reserved for commissioned officers. Unlock premium to take the field.
          </p>
          <Button
            className="mt-3 gap-1.5 font-display text-xs uppercase tracking-imperial"
            onClick={openPaywall}
          >
            <Crown className="h-3.5 w-3.5" /> Unlock Premium
          </Button>
        </FieldPanel>
      )}

      <FieldPanel className={cn("animate-fade-up", !isPremium && "pointer-events-none opacity-50")}>
        <SectionHeader index={1} title={progress ? "Your Campaign" : "Enlist"} />
        {progress ? (
          <div>
            <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-3">
              {[
                { label: "Commander", value: progress.name },
                { label: "Next Battle", value: `${progress.currentGame} of ${TOURNAMENT_LENGTH}` },
                { label: "Points Banked", value: progress.totalPoints },
              ].map((stat) => (
                <div key={stat.label} className="border border-gold-dim/40 bg-background/40 p-2.5 text-center">
                  <p className="truncate font-display text-lg font-black text-gold">{stat.value}</p>
                  <p className="mt-0.5 font-display text-[9px] uppercase tracking-imperial text-muted-foreground">
                    {stat.label}
                  </p>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
            <div className="mt-3 flex gap-2">
              <Button
                className="flex-1 gap-1.5 font-display text-xs uppercase tracking-imperial"
                onClick={() => startMutation.mutate()}
                disabled={startMutation.isPending}
              >
                <Swords className="h-3.5 w-3.5" /> Fight Game {progress.currentGame}: {currentDef?.title}
              </Button>
              <Button
                variant="outline"
                className="font-display text-xs uppercase tracking-imperial"
                onClick={() => resignMutation.mutate()}
                disabled={resignMutation.isPending}
              >
                Resign
              </Button>
            </div>
          </div>
        ) : (
          <div>
            <p className="font-body text-sm text-muted-foreground">
              Sign your name in the tournament ledger and take the field against Solignac and Freire.
            </p>
            <div className="mt-3 flex gap-2">
              <Input
                value={name}
                onChange={(e) => setName(e.target.value)}
                placeholder="Your name, commander"
                maxLength={16}
                className="h-10 border-gold-dim/50 bg-transparent font-body"
                aria-label="Tournament commander name"
              />
              <Button
                className="h-10 gap-1.5 font-display text-xs uppercase tracking-imperial"
                onClick={() => startMutation.mutate()}
                disabled={startMutation.isPending}
              >
                <Swords className="h-3.5 w-3.5" /> Begin
              </Button>
            </div>
          </div>
        )}
      </FieldPanel>

      <FieldPanel className="mt-4 animate-fade-up">
        <SectionHeader index={2} title="The Sixteen Campaigns" />
        <ul className="space-y-1.5">
          {TOURNAMENT_GAMES.map((def) => {
            const done = progress !== null && def.index < currentGame;
            const isNext = def.index === currentGame;
            const stars = Math.round(
              def.opponents.reduce((sum, g) => sum + GENERALS[g].difficulty, 0) / def.opponents.length,
            );
            return (
              <li
                key={def.index}
                className={cn(
                  "flex items-center gap-2 border px-2.5 py-2",
                  isNext
                    ? "border-gold bg-gold/10"
                    : done
                      ? "border-gold-dim/40 bg-background/40"
                      : "border-gold-dim/30 bg-background/20 opacity-70",
                )}
              >
                <span className="w-6 shrink-0 text-center font-display text-[11px] font-bold text-gold">
                  {def.index}
                </span>
                <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
                  <p className="truncate font-body text-sm font-semibold">{def.title}</p>
                  <p className="truncate font-body text-[11px] italic text-muted-foreground">
                    {OBJECTIVE_INFO[def.objective].name} · {ALLOCATION_INFO[def.allocation].name} ·{" "}
                    {def.opponents.length} generals {"★".repeat(stars)}
                    {def.useExtraTerritories ? " · 48 territories" : ""}
                  </p>
                </div>
                <span className="shrink-0 font-display text-[10px] uppercase tracking-widest text-muted-foreground">
                  max {tournamentMaxPoints(def)}
                </span>
                {done ? (
                  <Check className="h-4 w-4 shrink-0 text-gold" aria-label="Completed" />
                ) : isNext ? (
                  <Swords className="h-4 w-4 shrink-0 text-gold" aria-label="Next battle" />
                ) : (
                  <Lock className="h-3.5 w-3.5 shrink-0 text-muted-foreground/60" aria-label="Locked" />
                )}
              </li>
            );
          })}
        </ul>
      </FieldPanel>

      <FieldPanel className="mt-4 animate-fade-up">
        <SectionHeader index={3} title="High Scores" />
        {scores.length === 0 ? (
          <p className="font-body text-sm italic text-muted-foreground">Consulting the ledger...</p>
        ) : (
          <ul className="space-y-1">
            {scores.map((score, i) => (
              <li
                key={`${score.name}-${i}`}
                className={cn(
                  "flex items-center gap-2 px-2 py-1.5",
                  score.isHuman && "border border-gold-dim/60 bg-gold/10",
                )}
              >
                <span className="w-6 font-display text-[11px] font-bold text-gold">{i + 1}.</span>
                {i === 0 && <Medal className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-gold" aria-hidden />}
                <span className="min-w-0 flex-1 truncate font-body text-sm font-semibold">{score.name}</span>
                {score.isHuman ? (
                  <User className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-muted-foreground" aria-label="Human" />
                ) : (
                  <Bot className="h-3.5 w-3.5 text-muted-foreground" aria-label="AI general" />
                )}
                <span className="w-28 text-right font-display text-[11px] text-muted-foreground">
                  {score.score} pts · {score.gamesCompleted} games
                </span>
              </li>
            ))}
          </ul>
        )}
      </FieldPanel>
    </div>
  );
};

export default TournamentPage;

File: /web/src/state/GameContext.tsx
---

import { createContext, useCallback, useContext, useEffect, useMemo, useReducer, useRef, useState } from "react";
import type { ReactNode } from "react";

import type { SaveSummary } from "@/db/repository";
import {
  deleteSave,
  loadSavedState,
  loadSaveSummary,
  recordCompletedCampaign,
  saveCampaignState,
} from "@/db/repository";
import { aiNextAction } from "@/game/ai";
import { createGame, gameReducer } from "@/game/engine";
import type { GameAction, GameSetup, GameState } from "@/game/types";

interface GameContextValue {
  game: GameState | null;
  /** Metadata about the SQLite autosave slot, for the main menu. */
  savedSummary: SaveSummary | null;
  dispatch: (action: GameAction) => void;
  startGame: (setup: GameSetup) => void;
  abandonGame: () => void;
  /** Restore the autosaved campaign from SQLite. Returns false if unavailable. */
  resumeSavedGame: () => Promise<boolean>;
}

const GameContext = createContext<GameContextValue | null>(null);

type ReducerState = GameState | null;

type RootAction =
  | { type: "START"; setup: GameSetup }
  | { type: "RESUME"; state: GameState }
  | { type: "ABANDON" }
  | { type: "GAME"; action: GameAction };

function rootReducer(state: ReducerState, action: RootAction): ReducerState {
  switch (action.type) {
    case "START":
      return createGame(action.setup);
    case "RESUME":
      return action.state;
    case "ABANDON":
      return null;
    case "GAME":
      return state ? gameReducer(state, action.action) : state;
  }
}

export function GameProvider({ children }: { children: ReactNode }) {
  const [game, rawDispatch] = useReducer(rootReducer, null);
  const [savedSummary, setSavedSummary] = useState<SaveSummary | null>(null);
  const [aiTick, setAiTick] = useState<number>(0);
  const timerRef = useRef<number | null>(null);
  const recordedRef = useRef<boolean>(false);

  const dispatch = useCallback((action: GameAction) => {
    rawDispatch({ type: "GAME", action });
  }, []);

  const startGame = useCallback((setup: GameSetup) => {
    rawDispatch({ type: "START", setup });
  }, []);

  const abandonGame = useCallback(() => {
    rawDispatch({ type: "ABANDON" });
    deleteSave()
      .then(() => setSavedSummary(null))
      .catch((error) => console.warn("Failed to clear the saved campaign.", error));
  }, []);

  const resumeSavedGame = useCallback(async (): Promise<boolean> => {
    try {
      const state = await loadSavedState();
      if (!state) return false;
      rawDispatch({ type: "RESUME", state });
      return true;
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Failed to resume the saved campaign.", error);
      return false;
    }
  }, []);

  // Discover an existing autosave on boot.
  useEffect(() => {
    let cancelled = false;
    loadSaveSummary()
      .then((summary) => {
        if (!cancelled) setSavedSummary(summary);
      })
      .catch((error) => console.warn("Could not read the campaign archive.", error));
    return () => {
      cancelled = true;
    };
  }, []);

  // Autosave every state change to SQLite; archive the campaign once it ends.
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!game) return;
    if (game.phase === "gameOver") {
      if (recordedRef.current) return;
      recordedRef.current = true;
      recordCompletedCampaign(game)
        .then(() => setSavedSummary(null))
        .catch((error) => console.warn("Failed to archive the campaign.", error));
      return;
    }
    recordedRef.current = false;
    const timer = window.setTimeout(() => {
      saveCampaignState(game)
        .then((summary) => setSavedSummary(summary))
        .catch((error) => console.warn("Autosave failed.", error));
    }, 400);
    return () => window.clearTimeout(timer);
  }, [game]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!game || game.phase === "gameOver" || game.awaitingHandoff) return;
    const current = game.players[game.currentPlayer];
    if (!current || current.isHuman) return;

    const setupPhase = game.phase === "territoryGrab" || game.phase === "initialDeploy";
    const delay =
      game.phase === "election" ? 380 : setupPhase ? 260 : game.phase === "reinforcement" ? 350 : 700;
    timerRef.current = window.setTimeout(() => {
      const action = aiNextAction(game);
      if (action) {
        rawDispatch({ type: "GAME", action });
      }
      setAiTick((n) => n + 1);
    }, delay);

    return () => {
      if (timerRef.current !== null) {
        window.clearTimeout(timerRef.current);
        timerRef.current = null;
      }
    };
  }, [game, aiTick]);

  const value = useMemo<GameContextValue>(
    () => ({ game, savedSummary, dispatch, startGame, abandonGame, resumeSavedGame }),
    [game, savedSummary, dispatch, startGame, abandonGame, resumeSavedGame],
  );

  return <GameContext.Provider value={value}>{children}</GameContext.Provider>;
}

export function useGame(): GameContextValue {
  const ctx = useContext(GameContext);
  if (!ctx) throw new Error("useGame must be used within GameProvider");
  return ctx;
}

File: /web/src/state/PremiumContext.tsx
---

import { createContext, useCallback, useContext, useMemo, useState } from "react";
import type { ReactNode } from "react";
import { useMutation, useQuery, useQueryClient } from "@tanstack/react-query";
import { ErrorCode, PurchasesError } from "@revenuecat/purchases-js";
import type { CustomerInfo, Package } from "@revenuecat/purchases-js";
import { toast } from "sonner";

import { getPurchases, PREMIUM_ENTITLEMENT } from "@/lib/purchases";

interface PremiumContextValue {
  /** True once the premium entitlement is active for this customer. */
  isPremium: boolean;
  /** True while the first customer-info fetch is still in flight. */
  isLoading: boolean;
  paywallOpen: boolean;
  openPaywall: () => void;
  closePaywall: () => void;
  /** Formatted one-time price of the lifetime package (e.g. "$3.00"). */
  priceLabel: string;
  purchase: () => void;
  purchasePending: boolean;
  restore: () => void;
  restorePending: boolean;
}

const PremiumContext = createContext<PremiumContextValue | null>(null);

const CUSTOMER_INFO_KEY = ["rc-customer-info"] as const;

function hasPremium(info: CustomerInfo | undefined): boolean {
  return info ? Object.keys(info.entitlements.active).includes(PREMIUM_ENTITLEMENT) : false;
}

export function PremiumProvider({ children }: { children: ReactNode }) {
  const queryClient = useQueryClient();
  const [paywallOpen, setPaywallOpen] = useState<boolean>(false);

  const customerQuery = useQuery({
    queryKey: CUSTOMER_INFO_KEY,
    queryFn: () => getPurchases().getCustomerInfo(),
    staleTime: 60_000,
    retry: 1,
  });

  const offeringsQuery = useQuery({
    queryKey: ["rc-offerings"],
    queryFn: () => getPurchases().getOfferings(),
    staleTime: Infinity,
    retry: 1,
  });

  const lifetimePackage: Package | null = useMemo(() => {
    const current = offeringsQuery.data?.current ?? null;
    if (!current) return null;
    return current.lifetime ?? current.availablePackages[0] ?? null;
  }, [offeringsQuery.data]);

  const priceLabel = lifetimePackage?.webBillingProduct?.currentPrice?.formattedPrice ?? "$3.00";

  const purchaseMutation = useMutation({
    mutationFn: async () => {
      if (!lifetimePackage) throw new Error("The premium offer is not available right now.");
      const { customerInfo } = await getPurchases().purchase({ rcPackage: lifetimePackage });
      return customerInfo;
    },
    onSuccess: (info) => {
      queryClient.setQueryData(CUSTOMER_INFO_KEY, info);
      if (hasPremium(info)) {
        setPaywallOpen(false);
        toast.success("Premium commission granted. The Tournament awaits, commander.");
      }
    },
    onError: (error: unknown) => {
      if (error instanceof PurchasesError && error.errorCode === ErrorCode.UserCancelledError) {
        return;
      }
      console.error("[premium] purchase failed", error);
      toast.error("The purchase could not be completed. Please try again.");
    },
  });

  const restoreMutation = useMutation({
    mutationFn: () => getPurchases().getCustomerInfo(),
    onSuccess: (info) => {
      queryClient.setQueryData(CUSTOMER_INFO_KEY, info);
      if (hasPremium(info)) {
        setPaywallOpen(false);
        toast.success("Premium restored. Welcome back, commander.");
      } else {
        toast.info("No previous premium purchase was found for this account.");
      }
    },
    onError: (error: unknown) => {
      console.error("[premium] restore failed", error);
      toast.error("Could not reach the store to restore purchases.");
    },
  });

  const openPaywall = useCallback(() => setPaywallOpen(true), []);
  const closePaywall = useCallback(() => setPaywallOpen(false), []);
  const purchase = useCallback(() => purchaseMutation.mutate(), [purchaseMutation]);
  const restore = useCallback(() => restoreMutation.mutate(), [restoreMutation]);

  const value = useMemo<PremiumContextValue>(
    () => ({
      isPremium: hasPremium(customerQuery.data),
      isLoading: customerQuery.isLoading,
      paywallOpen,
      openPaywall,
      closePaywall,
      priceLabel,
      purchase,
      purchasePending: purchaseMutation.isPending,
      restore,
      restorePending: restoreMutation.isPending,
    }),
    [
      customerQuery.data,
      customerQuery.isLoading,
      paywallOpen,
      openPaywall,
      closePaywall,
      priceLabel,
      purchase,
      purchaseMutation.isPending,
      restore,
      restoreMutation.isPending,
    ],
  );

  return <PremiumContext.Provider value={value}>{children}</PremiumContext.Provider>;
}

/** Access premium/paywall state. Must be used inside PremiumProvider. */
export function usePremium(): PremiumContextValue {
  const ctx = useContext(PremiumContext);
  if (!ctx) throw new Error("usePremium must be used within PremiumProvider");
  return ctx;
}

import { render } from "vitest-browser-react";

import { Calendar } from "@/components/ui/calendar";

test("renders a month grid with navigation controls", async () => {
  // Fix the month so the calendar grid remains deterministic across test runs.
  const screen = await render(<Calendar mode="single" defaultMonth={new Date(2026, 0, 1)} />);

  await expect.element(screen.getByRole("grid")).toBeInTheDocument();
  await expect.element(screen.getByRole("button", { name: /previous/i })).toBeInTheDocument();
  await expect.element(screen.getByRole("button", { name: /next/i })).toBeInTheDocument();
  expect(screen.getByRole("gridcell").all().length).toBeGreaterThan(27);
});

import { ALL_TERRITORIES } from "@/game/mapData";
import type { TerritoryId } from "@/game/types";
import { ART } from "@/lib/art";

const EXPECTED_BOARD_COORDINATES: Partial<Record<TerritoryId, [number, number]>> = {
  alaska: [0.0911, 0.1729],
  northwestTerritory: [0.1725, 0.1797],
  greenland: [0.4063, 0.1201],
  alberta: [0.1673, 0.2588],
  ontario: [0.2493, 0.2744],
  quebec: [0.3203, 0.2734],
  westernUS: [0.1771, 0.3496],
  easternUS: [0.2493, 0.3652],
  centralAmerica: [0.1921, 0.4150],
  venezuela: [0.2363, 0.5479],
  peru: [0.2565, 0.6670],
  brazil: [0.3145, 0.6475],
  argentina: [0.2624, 0.7773],
  iceland: [0.4375, 0.2002],
  scandinavia: [0.5098, 0.1504],
  greatBritain: [0.4401, 0.3018],
  northernEurope: [0.4967, 0.3105],
  westernEurope: [0.4290, 0.4014],
  southernEurope: [0.5098, 0.3750],
  ukraine: [0.5612, 0.2715],
  northAfrica: [0.4349, 0.5127],
  egypt: [0.5098, 0.5068],
  eastAfrica: [0.5384, 0.6016],
  congo: [0.5052, 0.6719],
  southAfrica: [0.5000, 0.7920],
  westAfrica: [0.4688, 0.6035],
  ural: [0.6569, 0.2393],
  siberia: [0.7188, 0.1992],
  yakutsk: [0.8190, 0.1895],
  kamchatka: [0.8926, 0.1836],
  irkutsk: [0.7832, 0.2715],
  mongolia: [0.8125, 0.3281],
  japan: [0.8451, 0.3477],
  afghanistan: [0.6413, 0.3516],
  china: [0.7116, 0.4189],
  middleEast: [0.5768, 0.4551],
  india: [0.6790, 0.5137],
  siam: [0.7402, 0.5107],
  indonesia: [0.7813, 0.6084],
  newGuinea: [0.8789, 0.6367],
  westernAustralia: [0.7773, 0.7773],
  easternAustralia: [0.8496, 0.7549],
};

describe("world map alignment", () => {
  it("uses the already uploaded GitHub public map asset", () => {
    expect(ART.worldBoard).toBe("/risk/world-map.png");
  });

  it("keeps all territory anchors normalized inside the map", () => {
    for (const territory of ALL_TERRITORIES) {
      expect(territory.x, territory.id).toBeGreaterThanOrEqual(0);
      expect(territory.x, territory.id).toBeLessThanOrEqual(1);
      expect(territory.y, territory.id).toBeGreaterThanOrEqual(0);
      expect(territory.y, territory.id).toBeLessThanOrEqual(1);
    }
  });

  it("locks the standard territory anchors to the painted map piece centers", () => {
    const byId = new Map(ALL_TERRITORIES.map((territory) => [territory.id, territory]));

    for (const [id, [x, y]] of Object.entries(EXPECTED_BOARD_COORDINATES) as [TerritoryId, [number, number]][]) {
      const territory = byId.get(id);
      expect(territory, id).toBeDefined();
      expect(territory?.isExtra, id).toBe(false);
      expect(territory?.x, id).toBeCloseTo(x, 3);
      expect(territory?.y, id).toBeCloseTo(y, 3);
    }
  });
});

import { QueryClient, QueryClientProvider } from "@tanstack/react-query";
import { BrowserRouter, Routes, Route } from "react-router-dom";

import { PaywallOverlay } from "@/components/game/PaywallOverlay";
import { Toaster as Sonner } from "@/components/ui/sonner";
import { Toaster } from "@/components/ui/toaster";
import { TooltipProvider } from "@/components/ui/tooltip";
import { GameProvider } from "@/state/GameContext";
import { PremiumProvider } from "@/state/PremiumContext";

import Index from "./pages/Index";
import GamePage from "./pages/GamePage";
import NotFound from "./pages/NotFound";
import RecordsPage from "./pages/RecordsPage";
import SetupPage from "./pages/SetupPage";
import TournamentPage from "./pages/TournamentPage";

const queryClient = new QueryClient();

const App = () => (
  <QueryClientProvider client={queryClient}>
    <TooltipProvider>
      <Toaster />
      <Sonner />
      <PremiumProvider>
        <GameProvider>
          <BrowserRouter future={{ v7_startTransition: true, v7_relativeSplatPath: true }}>
            <Routes>
            <Route path="/" element={<Index />} />
            <Route path="/setup" element={<SetupPage />} />
            <Route path="/game" element={<GamePage />} />
            <Route path="/records" element={<RecordsPage />} />
            <Route path="/tournament" element={<TournamentPage />} />
              {/* ADD ALL CUSTOM ROUTES ABOVE THE CATCH-ALL "*" ROUTE */}
              <Route path="*" element={<NotFound />} />
            </Routes>
            <PaywallOverlay />
          </BrowserRouter>
        </GameProvider>
      </PremiumProvider>
    </TooltipProvider>
  </QueryClientProvider>
);

export default App;
